Reverend Sun Myung Moon's Words Compilation Committee  

Foreword  
                   President of the World Peace Unification Family, Hwang Seon-jo

1)  
The Path of Life to Find the Hometown  
Luke 15:11-32  
<Prayer (I)> We who were struggling in death have gathered again today, longing for our Father. Now, please allow our hearts to dwell in the Father's heart. Thus, may our bodies and minds move as Yours, Father.  
Father, You have tirelessly labored through the ages and centuries, accompanying our ancestors with great effort. How much have You toiled to pave the way for our ancestors? Yet, despite this, our ancestors have trampled upon the fruits of Heaven's labor and have shown shameful appearances that have caused You to worry. Please forgive us.  
We know that the sins of our ancestors remain as a bitter legacy, and we understand that their actions of lamentable fall have led countless humanity into suffering for six thousand years. We fear that we may inherit the broken hearts of our historical ancestors who betrayed and saddened the Father's heart. We are in a situation where we must overcome the peaks of sorrow caused by the fall and step upon the grievances left by our ancestors. Therefore, please allow our hearts to be captivated by the Father's heart, and grant us a glorious moment where our bodies can represent the Father. We earnestly hope and wish for this, Father.  
Is there anyone who can weep and appeal to the Father’s heart in anger? Is there anyone who can fight on behalf of the Father's circumstances? There are many people living on this earth, and humanity takes many forms, but there is no one, no place, and no region that can discuss the circumstances and feelings that the Father holds in His heart. We know that You have endured a history of sorrow and lament. Therefore, let this time be one where we can unburden our hearts and lay everything before You, Father.  
Father, may this hour not be one that does not accept our entirety, but may it be a time where we can enjoy being connected with You. We cannot help but appeal to You sincerely during this time.  
On this day, we, the unworthy, have knelt down in admiration and reverence. My Father, who knows our pitiful circumstances, who has fought alongside us in dire environments, we have gathered our hearts before You today, so please accept us. We know that we cannot be without You, and we must be governed before You. Therefore, we have come forth with all our sincerity and hearts, not minding the years of toil, and we have endured the difficult and sorrowful paths.  
The reason we have endured this path is to leave a historical connection with the Father. We, who have come to this place today, know that the Father has not disregarded those who seek, has not rejected enemies, and has labored to place those who ask in the position of friends. Father, today we want to seek with all our hearts, we want to search with all our sincerity, and we want to give everything to connect with You. So, Father, please look upon us with compassion.  
Please fulfill the desires we seek, fulfill the intentions we pursue, and hear the circumstances of those who knock at the door, Father. We earnestly hope and wish for this.  
Now, if we, the insufficient, have something we long for before You, it is to have a time where we can enjoy together with Your heart. This is our entire request, our entire wealth, and our entire life. So, Father, please look upon Your sons and daughters who have gathered at this time with compassion.  
Father, please guide us to establish the path of life we must walk. Until this day, You have allowed us to endure even in difficult circumstances, and You have helped us to bear through persecution, and You have worked to ensure that we do not leave behind grievances even in our fallen states. We know that You are the Father who has labored for us. Today, many of Your sons and daughters have gathered to once again offer their sincerity and hearts before You, so Father, You must personally move within their hearts. You must move upon their hearts, and please allow the heavenly life to touch their lives.  
It is now time to fulfill the mission of fighting against enemies with the deep-seated grievances in our hearts, so Father, please reveal Your strength and manifest with the authority of life.  
If we are to risk our lives to resolve the grievances of the Father, please allow us to proceed with the principles of love and make us courageous enough to face and fight against the enemies before the Lord of life. Thus, may we become children equipped with the conditions of life that can allow the myriad beings on this earth to look upon such selves and live on in the restored garden. We earnestly hope and wish for this, Father.  
Until today, may we have hearts that can repent of the faith we have claimed to hold, hearts that can reflect and repent of our actions, hearts that can regret the hopes we have pursued, and hearts that can laugh at the inner feelings we have sought. Thus, may we deny all of ourselves and connect all that belongs to the Father, leading us to the glorious position where we can call upon the Father. I earnestly hope and wish for this, my Father.  
Father, please look upon the Korean Peninsula with compassion. This land has been trampled upon by many nations throughout the ages and has been a land that has been oppressed by enemies. We know that the thirty million people of this land carry the grievances of a bloody history. Father, please soften Your heart upon the hearts of this nation, and soften Your circumstances upon the circumstances of this nation, and lead this nation’s hopes to align with Your hopes.  
Please do not let us remain in a position of resenting the sorrowful past, but allow us to be sons and daughters who can worry and appeal to meet the heavenly time approaching us. I earnestly hope and wish for this, beloved Father.  
Father, may there never be a day when the footsteps of the Father, who has come to this nation on behalf of many nations, are turned back due to sighs and sorrows. May this land not become one that leaves behind the sorrow of grief, and may this nation not become one that is such. I earnestly hope and wish for this, Father.  
The two billion seven hundred million sleeping humanity does not know that the Father is preparing a time when He can light the lamp of happiness in each heart. We know that we have the mission to awaken this humanity and the mission to untangle the complex circumstances of humanity to build a new ideal heavenly kingdom, the mission of building welfare. Today, we, in our unworthy and insufficient forms, kneel down with humble and apologetic hearts, so please bestow upon us the wondrous grace of heaven through our heartfelt appeals. May the Father manifest and remove anything that is not of that heart, and may this time be one where we can connect all that we have to the Father, so that the Father can recognize us as Your successors. I earnestly hope and wish for this, Father.  
Father, the family members remaining in Seoul and those who have gathered from the provinces have come together to build a new altar before You, so please look upon Your young sons and daughters with compassion. There are many words of encouragement and comfort, but please understand the circumstances that prevent us from speaking. Even in sadness, for the sake of heaven’s will; even in loneliness, for the sake of this one will; even in persecution, for the sake of this one will; even in discouragement, for the sake of this one will, we have gathered here with the sorrowful hearts that can only appeal to the Father.  
On this day, may we unburden our hearts and discuss with the Father, and may we be able to lay all circumstances before the Father and become a form that can please the Father. Even if I die, I will become a pure offering for this path. May this time allow us to renew our vows.  
I earnestly hope and wish for this, Father.  
It is not only through words that heaven’s will is fulfilled, nor is it achieved solely through sincerity. I long for that heart that can sing for heaven, a heart that can sing for heaven with deep emotion, and I miss the sight of forgetting everything and struggling for heaven. If there is a time and a place where we can sing the glory of the Father with such longing, I bow my head with a humble heart, so please recognize our earnest intentions and heartfelt desires and come to us at this time, Father.  
No one who has not walked a path can know that path, and the words of one who has not experienced it are lifeless. We know that the reason this nation has been driven into a pitiful position until today is to make known the Father’s pitiful circumstances. We know the circumstances of the Father, who must remain in lonely and sorrowful places, and we understand the grievances and frustrations that lead You to place us in positions of persecution.  
Today, may our hearts become the Father’s, and may You come to find our hearts. We have come to this place, wishing to be forms that can carry the Father in our hearts and weep with the Father. The reason the past is regrettable is because we know the Father, and the reason past events feel frustrating is also because we know the Father, and the reason we have sorrow is because we know heaven.  
The Father must accept us in this way and must tolerate us in that way, and we are in a position where we must resent the history that has left behind the grievances of restoration. Realizing this about ourselves, may we continue to cling to heaven in our lives of struggle without ceasing. Father, You know our circumstances so well, so may this day allow us to forget everything and become offerings of life dedicated to the Father’s presence.  
On this day, may You bestow new gifts of life upon the hearts of Your sons and daughters who are widely kneeling down in the provinces, and allow them to be sent to desolate places to light the lamp of life. May this time be one of reverence where we can manifest as lights of glory. I earnestly hope and wish for this, Father.  
Even if each circumstance is different, please allow us to share the same circumstances through Your history, and even if our hearts are different, please allow us to share the same heart through Your history. Father, may this hour be one where You operate, removing everything that is not Yours, and may it be a time that pleases the Trinity. I pray all these things in Your name. Amen.  
<Prayer (II)> Father, You know our hearts before we speak. We know that this hour is a time when You are personally present. Please allow us to feel that heaven is watching over all our matters at this time.  
Father, who has gone through a laborious historical process, please appear before us today and adorn us with new words. Please regard us with a new heart. We wish to lay aside all our unfaithfulness and, with childlike hearts, offer all that we have before Your presence during this hour. Please allow us to place all our worldly thoughts, attentions, and concepts before You, and grant us gentle and humble hearts like children. We wish to present ourselves with humble hearts that can be reshaped as You desire, so please accept us. May the Trinity operate.  
Please do not allow any satanic elements to remain as opposing elements before heaven, Father. May this not be a time when we are invaded by Satan, but may we be equipped with the shield of victory.  
In the midst of the heavenly hosts, may this hour of worship be a blessed altar that can lead all life to victory. I earnestly request and wish for this.  
We have entrusted everything. Please allow us to lay bare all our genuine thoughts and hearts before You. Thus, may this hour be one where all that we have can be transformed into the Father’s. I pray this in Your name. Amen.  
<Prayer (III)> At this time, please look upon Your bowed sons and daughters with compassion.  
Who among us will be the leader, and who will represent heaven’s words? These people do not wish for anyone other than the Father to appear, so please manifest Yourself, Father. Please allow us to experience heaven through our hearts, and let us feel the circumstances of the Father that we cannot help but feel. Please work in such a way that we cannot help but repent before You.  
Wherever people gather, things become tangled, but where people gather centered on heaven, the burdens in their hearts are released. We know this truth. Now, may all that has been tangled due to the sinful lineage be fundamentally untangled through the history of indemnity, the history of repentance, and the history of inspiration, allowing us to reflect upon ourselves, repent of the past, and yearn for a new day.  
Thus, please allow the heart that holds onto this to enable a new creation where we can once again repent of our sins. I earnestly hope and wish for this, Father.  
Now, as I wish to convey the words, may Your love be upon all who have gathered here.
Please extend your protective hand. I know that both the heart of the messenger and the heart of the recipient must move from the point of heart. Today, we do not only hope for physical happiness, nor do we wish to live solely intoxicated by our hearts; we desire only the garden where we can place our hearts and live forever. I earnestly ask, Father, that you allow the conditions of heartistic connections to explode from each person's innermost heart, so that deep connections can be established.

Father, until now, you have given many words to your beloved sons and daughters. Centered on these words, it is our path to unite and fulfill our responsibilities and missions. Therefore, Father, please be with us and protect us so that our path does not become blocked. May this word help us bear fruit that is in accordance with your inner heart. Otherwise, I fear that we may become sons and daughters who leave regrets before heaven due to the words we have received. I earnestly hope and wish for this, Father.

14 The Path of Life to Find Our Hometown
This day is a holy day, so please bestow the grace of blessings upon all people. I know that many sons and daughters are embracing hearts on behalf of your will, building hidden altars, and praying, so please bless them as well. The multitude in the spirit world, who are struggling with lonely hearts and hoping for a day of restoration, are also connected to us. Therefore, Father, please allow their endeavors to manifest good results through us.

May the Triune God surround us, looking forward to the standard of heart, and may we not call upon you without fulfilling that measure. Please establish us as joyful beings who can call you Father from a place where your flock is fulfilled. If we do not possess such grace, I earnestly ask that you lead us to become sons and daughters who, like children, humbly draw upon your heart of compassion and mercy during this hour.

Please bless the family members scattered in this region today. Many lives are anxiously calling out for heaven's timing, so I earnestly ask that you grant them the grace of life. I pray all these words in your name. Amen.

<Words> The title of the message I wish to share with you is The Path of Life to Find Our Hometown. I will speak on this title.

Today's message will be about this content.

Humanity on the Path to Find Our Hometown
Currently, humanity in this world is longing for peace. Furthermore, everyone, without exception, desires to be individuals enjoying freedom, living in a society of freedom, a nation of freedom, and a world of freedom. 

Without peace in my heart and without freedom in my heart, true happiness cannot exist. If there is someone who wishes to walk the true path of life, they will hope to enjoy true freedom and true happiness within true peace.

So, in comparing your ideological conditions to walk the true path of life, what position do you find yourself in? I believe it is time to clearly reveal whether you are in conflict or in harmony with this.

Today, both the wise and the foolish unanimously say that this world is not a world of peace. They cry out for freedom but acknowledge that they cannot live in a free environment that arises from the heart. For this reason, we cannot deny that we have not become the selves of happiness that we ideologically long for.

We know very well what this nation is, what we are, what this society is, what this world is, and what the historical path we have walked is like. 

If we acknowledge this, we must admit that we are not living in the world of our hometown, where we can find joy, and if we are not living in the garden of our hometown, where we can enjoy happiness, then no one can refute the fact that we are not living in the original world where we can move and govern as we think.

Yet, we must still hope for happiness, and we must still hope for peace and freedom; our heart's movements are urging ourselves and our environment, and you will feel this well within your living sphere.

Thus, whether internally or externally, the world of our hometown that humanity desires has not been realized, and because humanity cannot live in that world, today we are struggling on the street of searching for our hometown. We must clearly understand that we are in such a situation. Therefore, both the wise and the foolish are struggling to find their hometown.

Every being that has the form of a human must feel that they cannot escape the historical currents of seeking their hometown. So, I will speak on the title of The Path of Life to Find Our Hometown.

Where to Find the Path to Our Hometown
Until now, sages and wise individuals have come to this earth to teach the path of life. They have provided direction, saying, "Go this way," or "Live according to this principle." However, there are also philosophical directions, paths through ideologies set by sovereigns, and paths through social ethics. Furthermore, there are religious directions that seek to connect the external world with eternal ideals. 

In a broad sense, this is true, and in a narrow sense, there are directions for individuals, families, and interpersonal relationships.

All of these must be in a position to move toward a moment of happiness that the overall and cosmic ideals are aiming for. If one cannot stand in such a position, then all of this will inevitably become a position that is caught up in the heavenly principles when the day comes to clarify the heavenly will.

Then, how can we find a world of peace and freedom that can introduce a world of happiness centered on the paths of religion, ethics, or the truths that philosophy aims for? The heart of a person is the same for everyone. The feelings held thousands of years ago are the same as those that will appear millions of years in the future. The world of heart does not develop.

Is there not a world where we can cultivate the heart that can create a garden of happiness, a social standard where we can feel happiness, and a religious consciousness where we can taste happiness? If we conclude that such things do not exist, then where is God? In that case, it would be concluded that God cannot be with humanity.

If there is a heavenly principle that holds and governs humanity, guiding them toward goodness through ethics and morality, then heaven must inevitably clarify all that is related to us and connected to us, and furthermore, there will come a day when anyone, regardless of gender, can affirm this emotionally. In such a place, we must be able to shout that this happiness is our happiness, this peace is our peace, and this freedom is our freedom. If not, you must understand that neither God nor any great thinker has any relationship with us.

When we analyze people, we can analyze them both internally and externally. When we consider the realities of society, we see that there are social organizations and planned organizations that do not appear outwardly. In this way, everything unfolds both internally and externally.

Humans are the same. A person lives with external circumstances while also living with internal circumstances, so they must communicate both internal and external situations, and there must be an environment where hearts can connect and sing of happiness from the same position. Furthermore, searching for that environment cannot be anything other than our life's journey.

Many sages and wise individuals have come and gone throughout history, but no one has ever called out to the masses with a victorious slogan, saying, "Everyone! Go this way." No one has ever said, "You should live this way, relying on me and my heart and my love."

Jesus spoke of love, but he did not clarify the concept of happiness centered on love, the concept of peace centered on love, or the ideology of freedom centered on love. He said, "Follow me, believe in me, look to me," but he could not express that we should share our hearts and live centered on heavenly feelings.

For this reason, despite the many pioneers who have come and gone throughout history, they have not been able to introduce the content that allows us to enjoy happiness centered on the heart, nor have they been able to introduce the joy of connecting the world of freedom and peace that resonates with the heart of heaven.

So, where does humanity long for? It is the same as what was mentioned earlier. The world of our hometown, that is, a world where once we go, we never want to return, a world that we do not tire of seeing again and again, a world where the feelings we once felt do not fade away, a world where if there is laughter, we can laugh forever, and a world where if we find one owner, we can never lose that owner again. There must be such a place.

Our Reality Longing for Our Hometown
Such a place is where each individual with a heart can live, and such a hometown must be introduced in the end times of human history. If this is not the case, then today this world cannot be managed even if we try to manage it. You must understand that the time is approaching when we cannot establish any ideology or principle that can introduce all of this from a logical perspective. Therefore, we long for the world of our hometown where we can live forever, the land of our hometown, the brothers of our hometown, the family of our hometown, the relatives of our hometown, and the garden of our hometown.

So, among you today, is there anyone who can confidently say, "I have found such a hometown"? There is none. Therefore, we are inevitably beings destined to seek that hometown. Jesus also came to this earth as a savior, saying, "Follow me," and presented that path, but he could not establish a garden of our hometown where we could live together. God also leads humanity, but today he cannot say, "Let us live together here," and instead speaks of going to the garden of our desired hometown to live, conducting such providence.

Just as God did and just as Jesus, the Son of God, did, you, living on this earth today, are in the same destiny. You who are struggling while longing for your hometown, has anyone ever rejoiced upon meeting that day? Has anyone ever sung, "I am happy," upon meeting that day? No one has done so yet. Did God enjoy such a day? He did not either. Then, is there any principle that can bring that day? There is none. Heaven also could not enjoy it. The contents of heaven and earth are such.

Therefore, humans with a conscience who cannot live outside the heavenly fate are experiencing the process of finding direction under a common goal and ideology. Thus, you must understand that the heart of happiness grows more earnest as you go, but happiness itself moves further away from you. You may feel that you have earnestly longed for freedom, peace, and happiness and have struggled to reach that destination, yet in reality, it reflects your inner world as something distant and unattainable.

From here, we must become individuals who can sing of the hometown of happiness by stepping on the process we must inevitably go through. Only then must we meet the day when we can harmonize with the universe, sing together, and be happy together. That is the purpose of history, and if there is any religion, that is the purpose of that religion. If there is a Creator, that Creator is also pushing humanity toward such a goal. Because humans who cannot escape such providence cannot help but move in the same direction, whether they are wise or foolish.

In this situation where both the wise and the foolish are walking the same path of life, do not boast of your excellence. Do not boast of your favorable environment. Do not boast of your powerful status. You cannot solve the path of life with that. You cannot solve the world of your hometown. Why is that? Because the direction humanity is aiming for today is created by humans, it cannot be resolved through that. You must understand this.

If heaven has been conducting providence from this perspective, it has only taught us direction in terms of morality or truth, but it has not taught us in terms of heart. It has not taught us about happiness that can be felt in real life, nor has it taught us about peace and freedom that can be felt in our lives. For this reason, God's providence has made humanity look at these things as distant hopes.

20 The Path of Life to Find Our Hometown
Because we cannot escape such a fate, whether we are wise or foolish, whether we are sad or happy, we may have freedom in our daily lives, we may have emotional freedom in our yearly lives, and we may have emotional freedom in our lifetime. However, in terms of the historical heart, life, ideology, and perspective centered on oneself, it is the same. Heaven must see it this way, and we must also see it this way.

Jesus could not achieve this on this earth. Therefore, whether we look at this person or that person, we feel pity. The time has come when we need someone who can teach us that we are the pitiable ones blocking this pitiable humanity. We must lament our own pity, we must weep for our pitiable selves, we must hold heaven and earth and weep, and we must ponder what will become of our footsteps. What will the results of the changing environment contain as we reach our destination? It is time for a leader to emerge who can clarify these issues and urge us to be concerned about ourselves.

Throughout history, in the process of creating a revolutionary new culture, many people have come forth with new ideologies, new goals, new happiness, new freedom, and newness, striving to clarify the pitiable self. However, they were merely mission bearers who influenced their times and were needed for specific periods or eras.

Today, this era is the era of new global ideologies. Therefore, something must emerge that can make you, who should be the model for the world, lament that you do not know where to go and remain in that place.

Jesus came 2,000 years ago and claimed to be the Son of God. At that time, the Jewish people, who boasted of being the chosen people, had received the grace of countless prophets throughout their 4,000-year-long history, yet they still longed for the Messiah.
What has appeared is something that was not known. It was only after sending Jesus to the cross that they realized he was the Messiah and found themselves in a sorrowful position. 

Then, when we call Jesus our Savior, what kind of Savior should he have been before humanity at that time? He should have been a Savior who could take on your sorrows and be confident in doing so. Therefore, Jesus said, "Come to me, all you who are weary and burdened, and I will give you rest." (Matthew 11:28) This is a grateful and thankful message. That one word was a great proclamation for humanity.

If there are young men and women who are anxious and trying to clarify themselves with a heart full of sorrow, upon hearing that one word, they would raise their hands and come forward. Thus, they would say, "Thank you, Jesus, who came and spoke 2,000 years ago. Thank you, God, who gave us the word through Jesus." They would be grateful for the words that flowed from this spirit and ideology.

Now, we need a protagonist who can take charge of this world, this nation, and the issues of the heart, and relieve the burdens of the heart. It is because of this that Jesus left behind the promise of his return.

What did Jesus come to this earth to accomplish? He came to take on all the burdens of humanity's crosses, but he could not take on humanity's emotional burdens. Thus, today, all of humanity is waiting for that day to once again entrust their emotional burdens to Jesus, saying, "Lord, come quickly."

Therefore, we must recognize that the time has come for something that can stand in the midst of the historically miserable environment of my own self, the world we live in, or history that flows, to say, "Know your sorrowful circumstances, know your pity, know your heartache, and you must do this and that."

We are living in a world where we walk an unknown path of life, filled with the fear of not knowing what may happen as we go along. So, where is the destination of the path we are on? We are walking a path that cannot be explained as such and such, searching for our original homeland. We are being dragged along without knowing. However, we must know whether we will hit a rock or fall off a cliff as we go along. 

How would your heart feel if you found yourself in such a position? It would be turned upside down. Among you, there are those who have walked the path of life for 40 years, or perhaps 70 or 80 years. There may be those among you who boast of having found happiness, but there is no one who has broken through this path of life. Therefore, everyone is a pitiful person.

Thus, we must find someone who has a pitiful situation that can be connected to our own pitiful circumstances and can resonate with the world. If there is some loneliness within oneself, that loneliness must not only connect with the world but also, if there is something unknown that feels suffocating and burdensome in one’s heart, we must find someone who can clarify all of this, someone who can take on my unhappiness, my pity, my loneliness, and my sorrow. 

Furthermore, we must find someone who can introduce us to a world beyond what we long for, someone who can fulfill the feelings we have always wanted to experience in a world of happiness, peace, and freedom, and someone who can create happiness in relation to eternity as a subject of motivation. If we meet such a person, they will be a successful figure in the journey of life.

I believe and know that it must be Jesus or God who can make us feel and experience such an hour in this sad world. Today, you must seek someone who can teach you the secret to overcoming the time you must inevitably pass through, while walking with the thought that you know.

To do this, one must go through their own circumstances and must be able to surpass the standards of their own hopes, while also being able to resolve such issues in a substantive way, which is why we can trust and believe in God.

Moreover, one must walk with the ideals of such a heart, so that even when faced with sorrow on the difficult path of life, one can contain the emotions felt in that world of heart. No matter how much one is beaten and struck, if there is something that becomes stronger and does not betray heaven, that something, felt through the connection of the heart, will not be conquered even if it is pushed to the depths of hell. Such a place must exist. The direction in which God governs humanity is that one place, the original garden.

Thus, God's providence, which governs history, has established that one standard through countless twists and turns, and humans who must follow this must also go through many painful processes to stand before that one standard. We must understand that this is a point that all beings in the world of existence should aim for. We are pitiful people who must walk this path.

When you think of your homeland, what comes to mind? In the homeland, there are always beloved parents, a beloved village, a beloved home, and beloved siblings. When we leave our hometown and go far away to a foreign land, the scope of that homeland expands to include our country, that is, our nation. Furthermore, from the perspective of the universe or heaven, this world becomes our homeland. The broader the perspective we have, the more proportionally the scope of our homeland expands, and you will feel this well in various life processes.

So, what kind of homeland do we desire? It is not a place that you can say is your hometown. The homeland, the homeland of the heart, is a resting place for the heart where the heart can find joy, a nest for the world of the heart. We must understand this.

We say that God has been carrying out the providence of salvation by coming to find humanity. If heaven seeks me and humanity seeks me, I will say to God, "Please find me based on emotional conditions rather than situational conditions." Why? Because situations can be varied, but the heart has only one condition. Therefore, I think this is the appearance of someone who is seeking the true faith.

Jesus said, "Where is the kingdom of heaven?" He said, "It is within your heart." Where is one's true homeland? It is not in life but in the heart. The kingdom of heaven has a historical background that can connect with the heart, which is why we long for that homeland with our hearts. Because the emotions felt in the heart are intertwined with an unbreakable bond, we yearn for that homeland. Therefore, we must live a life that can connect with the original heart in our journey of life, and we must not forget to feel the garden of our homeland.

Then, such a place, not where we live today, but the true garden of happiness that history desires, can be introduced as such, and who will be there in that homeland of true peace and true freedom? Think about it. Who will be in that homeland? The great, high, and majestic God will be there. Also, the Lord we have longed for will be there. Then, the Holy Spirit will be there, and many saints who have come and gone throughout the history of providence will be there. Wouldn't that be so? There will also be loyal subjects who cannot be compared with anyone in the world, and filial sons and daughters who cannot be compared with anyone in the world will be there. However, if you do not expand your heart's connection and cannot feel the ideological aspects, you will not be able to connect with that world.

Thus, many saints have taught humanity about morality, and Moses introduced the Ten Commandments, and many sages have undoubtedly worked hard to pave the way for such aspects. Religions, ethics, and ideologies that do not have the mission to develop the heart's field (the heart's soil) in humanity's journey toward the homeland will retreat from this universe. Even if they do not want to retreat, God will cast them out.

You are longing for your homeland and are on your way to find it. We are people who are on a path of destiny that we must inevitably take, a process we cannot avoid. No matter how confident someone is in their intelligence and abilities, we know that there is no one who can boldly say, "All of humanity! All of heaven and earth! Respond to my words."

So, where should we turn our steps in our journey of life as we seek our homeland today? It is to the place where true loving parents exist, where there is a true resting place of love. That is where we should stay, where we can find rest. Furthermore, that is where the world of peace overflowing with happiness and hope will be, the garden of freedom. The stronger your longing for that place becomes, the greater your resentment toward the earth will grow. You will want to live cleanly regarding the earth. Historical figures of the past all lived like that.

Today, in the world, there are people who say that the long journey to find lost parents is not far, and they run to meet their loved ones, regardless of the distance. If you, who are on your way to find the garden of your homeland, cannot do as much, you must reflect. Have you ever wandered in search of your homeland at any one time, any one hour, or during any period of your life? You must not be irresponsible in such matters. You must be able to take responsibility on that path and leave a part of your responsible life on that path to recreate the history of your homeland and establish the will of the providence of your homeland before heaven. Those who have walked that way could become historical figures, and those who have walked that way could form religions. Therefore, today, we must long for the parents of our homeland, the mountains and rivers of our homeland, the families of our homeland, and the world of our homeland. The time has come for that.

Today, communists dream of a global homeland centered on materialism, but that will not suffice.
제압하고 하나님을 중심으로 한 국가를 세우려는 그 마음을 이해하지 못했습니다. 그들은 예수님을 배척하고 십자가에 못 박았습니다. 예수님은 그들의 죄를 대신 짊어지셨고, 그로 인해 인류를 구원하고자 하셨습니다. 그러나 그들은 그분의 마음을 이해하지 못했습니다.

오늘날 우리가 예수님을 통해 본향을 찾고, 그분의 뜻을 이루기 위해 나아가야 할 책임이 있습니다. 우리는 그분의 심정을 이해하고, 그분이 지니고 있었던 사랑과 희생의 정신을 이어받아야 합니다. 그러므로 우리는 그분의 길을 따르며, 인류를 위한 진정한 지도자가 되어야 합니다.

이제 우리는 각자의 인생길에서 본향을 향한 여정을 계속해야 합니다. 그 길은 결코 쉽지 않겠지만, 우리는 서로를 격려하고 도우며 나아가야 합니다. 우리의 심정이 하나가 되어, 본향을 향한 그리움을 품고, 그 길을 함께 걸어가야 합니다. 그렇게 할 때, 우리는 진정한 성공을 이룰 수 있을 것입니다.
아버님이 먼저 아프셨음을 알았사옵니다. 저희가 슬퍼하기 전에 아버님이 먼저 슬퍼하셨음을 알았사옵니다. 그러므로 저희가 아버님을 붙들고 울고 싶습니다. 아버님, 저희를 긍휼히 여기시고, 저희가 본향을 찾는 길에서 아버님의 사랑을 느낄 수 있도록 도와주시옵소서. 저희가 이 길을 가는 동안 아버님의 마음을 이해하고, 아버님과 함께 울며, 아버님의 슬픔을 나누는 참된 자녀가 되기를 원하옵니다. 아버님, 저희가 아버님을 붙들고 울 수 있는 그날이 오기를 간절히 기도합니다. 아버님의 사랑을 느끼며, 저희의 본향을 찾는 그 길에서 아버님과 함께할 수 있도록 인도하여 주시옵소서. 저희의 모든 상처와 아픔을 아버님께 맡기고, 아버님의 사랑으로 치유받기를 원하옵니다. 아버님, 저희가 아버님의 마음을 이해하고, 아버님과 함께 이 길을 걸어갈 수 있도록 도와주시옵소서. 아버님, 저희가 아버님을 붙들고 울 수 있는 그날이 오기를 간절히 기도합니다.
Father, I have come to know that you were the first to suffer, and I have come to understand that you fell before we did.  
As I discover that I am a lacking being who goes silently toward heaven, how much has heaven longed for sons and daughters who can bow their heads and call you Father? Through today’s words, I ask that such feelings arise in our hearts, and when we face this nation, the world, and heaven, may those feelings be stirred within us. Only when such feelings arise can we say we have a confident faith from the individual to the entire ideological realm, and knowing that we will become the position of heaven with the highest heart to establish our ideals, I earnestly ask that you uplift our hearts so that we can pave the way in such an environment.  
Through today’s words, I ask that we be able to criticize ourselves for the sadness we felt on the path of life we must walk, to live in the joy of happiness, and to be children who can bow our heads and exalt the glory of the Father while valuing our connection with heaven.  
I entrust all things to you, so please guide and assert that there is no deviation from the Father’s heart regarding their lives, their entire existence, and all the ideals they hold. I earnestly hope and wish for this, and I pray all these words in your name. Amen.  
2)  
Father and I  
John 14:1-19  
<Prayer> Father! Through over thirty years of life, we cannot help but recall that the heart of Jesus, who had to face the Jewish people proud of being the chosen people of Israel, lost the heart that wished to realize peace and freedom for that nation. The history of the Father’s toil to send a single son for four thousand years was carried out alongside the Israelite people, and the traces of the blood and sweat shed are permeated in the history of the Israelite people. Despite enduring such toil and shedding blood and sweat, it is infinitely sorrowful that the Israelite people at that time could not establish a relationship with heaven.  
Today, we know and believe in Jesus, who came and went throughout past history, but there is no one who knows and believes in the tragic Jesus, who was chased and pursued by the Israelite people at that time, wandering from this village to that village, from this town to that town. No one can find those who know the appearance of Jesus, who came to represent the heart of heaven.  
The Israelite people, who awaited the Messiah, fought for thousands of years with the hope of welcoming the Messiah, and although they longed for the time when the Messiah would come, when the very sign of that hope appeared, they fell into a deep sleep, overwhelmed by their own circumstances and the environment they were in, unable to know the heart of heaven. We cannot help but recall this lamentable history, and if we have the responsibility to resolve the resentment that is deeply embedded in the Father’s heart today, please allow us to bear the sins of the Israelite people who failed to recognize the coming Jesus.  
Please allow us to be those who can take responsibility for the mistakes of the Israelite people that saddened Jesus and repent on their behalf.  
Jesus spent over thirty sorrowful years of life. Moreover, he had a three-year public ministry in which he devoted everything, but who understood his heart, and who knew his circumstances? Not a single person. Even the disciples, who shared in his joys and sorrows, who were supposed to be his followers, did not know. The disciples, who should have earnestly held onto heaven and appealed to it out of concern for their master walking the path of death, were instead in a position to question who Jesus was, feeling that the three years of public ministry were in vain. If there is sorrow in Jesus’ heart, how could there be greater sorrow than this? If there is pain, how could there be greater pain than this?  
There are Christians who can honor and serve Jesus, who performed miracles, but there are none who wish to live holding onto the footsteps of Jesus, who was trampled and pushed aside. Father, we cannot help but appeal with tears of blood that many sons and daughters who can grasp the heart of the pitiful Jesus may emerge among all people.  
Living God, who controls the course of history, we know that you quietly teach us the way to go. Father, please do not let us be those who merely long for the past Jesus, but allow us to be those who can testify to the Jesus of the times.  
Now, please allow us to sympathize with the heart of Jesus, who had to go before the Father, and to bow our heads before that heart. If there is anything that Jesus wished for and rejoiced in, please allow us to be those who can fulfill it. Please guide us to be sons and daughters who can resonate with the heart of Jesus, who had to resolve the issue of humanity’s life two thousand years ago and establish a relationship with his heart.  
Children of yours who have gathered, suffering with lonely hearts in the world of death, please allow them to repent from where they sit, and may you strike them with the whip of life so that they can deny all the wrongs of the past and establish a new connection with heaven during this time.  
Father, how earnest is your heart to speak to humanity? How much have you longed to rejoice in finding humanity? In this hour, may we open our hearts, renew all sensations of our bodies, and experience all the realities of your world, longing for your heart. May this be a time of joy where we can call upon you in the spirit of goodwill and be reshaped and recreated by your words. I earnestly hope and wish for this, my Father.  
Father! Please govern this hour so that it is not in vain. I wish to speak, so please allow there to be no gap between the speaker and the listener. When we feel sorrowful, allow us to feel it together, and when we feel reverence before you, let us feel it together. Although there may be many gathered, I earnestly hope and wish that they may become one, one altar, one mountain offering.  
On this day, please bless the countless altars gathered on behalf of humanity, and if there are your hidden sons and daughters earnestly appealing from a pitiful position, be their deep heart’s interlocutor, and establish a connection of grace with them so that they may be led to the resolution of life. I earnestly hope and wish for this.  
Please govern the remaining time as well. I entrust all things before you, so may it not be a time where Satan can take advantage. I pray in your name. Amen.  
<Words> The title of the message I wish to think about with you today is “Father and I.” If we say this in a larger context, it becomes “Father, our God, and humanity.” I will speak for a moment with the title “Father and I.”  
If there is anything sorrowful in the world, there is nothing sadder than a child losing a beloved parent. Likewise, there is nothing sadder than a parent losing a beloved child.  
The Problem of Fallen Humanity  
In Christianity, it is said that humanity has fallen. This is a fact that cannot be denied when we look at the current society or examine it. It can be inferred that this has resulted in the society we see today due to some source of sin. Some twists and turns have caused the society we see today, and we cannot deny that we stand on the historical path of that result and that we are troubled by our own existence as a result.  
What is the greatest concern among our troubles? It is the sorrow of losing a parent that should not be lost, the concern of searching for a lost parent; there can be no greater concern than this. Furthermore, there is no greater concern than being in a position where one should have a parent but does not, or being in a position where one should have children but cannot have them.  
Though it is said that humanity has fallen, there is a connection between humanity and heaven. We cannot deny that there is also a self that is not aligned with any ideology. When we acknowledge that humanity has fallen, we must recognize that falling is impossible without establishing a relative relationship. If I feel that I am not good, it is because there is something good to aspire to, and if I wish to rise higher, it is because there is something higher to attain. This relationship extends from the individual to the whole.  
There may be many events tangled due to various circumstances, but the problem tangled in our hearts is only one: humanity has lost its parents. Humanity must find the severed connection due to losing parents, and God must find the lost children. We must first resolve the important issue of re-establishing the lost connection, rediscovering the lost joy, and regaining the lost happiness.  
Then, how will all of this be resolved for us, who acknowledge that we live in a world of sin? It cannot be solved by any philosophy with a well-structured system, nor can it be resolved by any ideology or conceptual faith. There is only one way to resolve it: by placing our hearts on the line. The world of that heart has no before or after, no high or low, and can be both the beginning and the end. We must keep in mind that it can only be resolved through that heart.  
What is the sorrow of humanity? It is the sorrow of having lost the true owner in Eden due to the fall, and the sorrow of losing the connection that allows us to harmonize and sing with the ideology of the Creator, the heart of the Creator, and the vitality of the Creator, drawing eternal happiness into our lives.  
The Relationship Between God and Humanity  
Who is the Creator who made us? He is, of course, the owner of our bodies and hearts, the subject of our ideologies and emotional worlds, and furthermore, the owner and subject of our hearts. We absolutely need such a God. It is not something that is conceptually needed based on our consciousness or recognition, but absolutely necessary. The sorrow of losing such a master is profound.  
Not only is He our master, but furthermore, God is in the position of being the Father of humanity. The God who created heaven and earth is not only our master but also our Father. He wishes to clarify the relationship that says, “I am your Father, and you are my sons and daughters,” and to sing of happiness in that relationship. We must understand that this is the center of the Father’s life, the center of His ideology, and the purpose for which God created humanity.  
Christians refer to God as Father. Humanity, which should stand before the Father as sons and daughters, is living in a pitiful state due to the fall. What is the position of the Father who wishes to call humanity sons and daughters, and what is the form of humanity that should stand as sons? Humanity is in a situation where it cannot be in a position to call the Father or respond to the Father. This is the fall. The historical path that has come down to eliminate this sorrowful noun is the history of humanity.  
If God exists, His work would be to trample upon that sorrowful noun and to fight to eliminate it.  
When we think this way, it is easy to call Him Father, but it is difficult to experience Him as a real Father. We can conceptually sense that Father, but it is difficult to serve the Father who is truly addressing us.  
What is the reason for this? It is due to the fall. Because of the fall, we have fallen into this position. When we acknowledge that we are struggling in such an environment and that we are still fighting to live without dying, we may feel how distant the gap is between us and the Father.  
We must long for a leader who can bridge this distance to appear on this earth. We should hope for a global leader who can pave a smooth path to bridge this distance. That leader must not only be the leader of my body, nor just the leader of my heart, but must be the leader of my heart. He must be an eternal and absolute leader, not one who changes with the times or merely embodies revolutionary content.  
If you have never even thought of such a leader, then at this time, you must reflect on yourself and criticize the self that is trapped in concepts. You must understand the position where you are and reassess the value of your self, and you must examine what position you stand in before the great fortune of heaven and earth.  
If there is anything grateful for fallen humanity, it is that there is nothing more grateful than introducing the lost Father, and if there is anything joyful for heaven, it is that there is nothing more joyful than finding the lost children. If one person can come forth who can re-establish this connection, that person will be one who can relieve the historical toil of God.  
What Fallen Humanity Must Long For  
It is not heaven’s intention to destroy humanity, but rather, heaven has a responsibility to find a way for them to live, and thus heaven has established the will of providence. Therefore, the protagonist who can restore the father-son relationship that heaven desires and humanity longs for must surely appear. This is an undeniable fact when we consider history.  
As we struggle in the fallen world, we must criticize our sinful selves and resent the events of the fall. Then what should we long for? We must seek our lost original parents. The heart that longs to find the lost original master, the lost original Father, will open the path of resurrection. If such a person, such a group, such a movement exists on this earth, then heaven, which is searching for lost children, will move through that group, and heaven, which is striving to establish the father-son relationship, will be able to reach out to such individuals.  
As we have traversed thousands of years of historical paths, if we have not heard from all people that someone is indeed so, we should blame all humanity, and if the sages of history have not introduced such facts, we should blame the sages of history. Furthermore, if we cannot find such content in the words of those who have come forth to fulfill the will of God, we may as well deny the existence of God.  
The God who governs to save humanity dwells within us and longs for us to dwell within Him. That is why Jesus said to his disciples, “I am the only begotten Son of God, and you are my brothers.” He also said, “I do not go according to my own will, but according to the will of the Father. The kingdom I desire is not my kingdom, but the Father’s kingdom. The people I seek are not my people, but the Father’s people. The place where I wish to live is not my place, but the Father’s place.”
It is not a family, but the family of the father. The country I can boast about is not my country, but my father's country. He said so. He also said that heaven is the father and the earth is the mother, and regarding humanity, he said, "I am the bridegroom, and you are the bride." Such a precious proposition must remain in the heavenly order for us to affirm that heaven exists, and there must be something with such content for us to find that path, which is why religions are established to guide people in that direction. 

From this perspective, a religion that introduces the relationship between father and son, the relationship between husband and wife, and the relationship between siblings will be the final religion. In this light, we cannot deny that the principles of Christianity lie here. We must think of this as a great honor. 

No matter how many saints have come and gone throughout history, they only introduced heaven in a conceptual and vague manner and could not present the content that allows for the existential experience of heaven. However, Jesus called God the Father in the presence of the mocking Jewish people, and even when persecution intensified, he cared for heaven. This signifies that Jesus stood firmly in a position where he had a self that no one had ever experienced or understood, and he elucidated a worldview and perspective on life that no one had ever realized. 

Jesus did not explain this in terms of circumstances but rather in terms of heart. Furthermore, because he manifested as the reality that elucidated this, he was the Messiah. Even if someone appeared among those whom heaven did not send, they would still have to be recognized as the Messiah. The history of the heavenly order moves in such a way. 

Jesus is the one sent by heaven. He came not to move under sin but to resolve all grievances caused by the sins and corruption of history until he could resolve everything from the place where the heart of the Father remains to the place where that heart's movement ends. Therefore, from that standpoint, Jesus sought to connect the love of heaven with the earth. He said, "I am the bridegroom, and you are the bride." Now we must prepare the position of children, possess the heart of the bride and groom, and eventually advance to the place where he called God the Father. 

The relationship between the father and me must be sought again. 

Christians around the world call the Lord the bridegroom and seem to acknowledge themselves as brides who can stand confidently before him. However, it is not that simple. This is not achieved through circumstances but can only be possible with a single-minded heart. Moreover, that heart must not only be one's own but must also encompass the historical heart that God has been guiding for 6,000 years, a heart that can traverse through this reality into the future. Only with such a heart can one become a bride who moves for heaven and recognizes the value of the subject, saying, "Oh! Lord, who is the bridegroom!" and only then will heaven respond. 

We cherish the words left behind. While we value what has been said, we cannot value those who keep and act upon the words. The promised Messiah, whom we knew to be precious, was not valued as the embodiment of the word, and this is the historical sorrow. When we listen to the words, they sound plausible, but we see that humans are just like ordinary people. 

Reflecting on this historical twist, unless we elucidate our own sorrowful position and the relationship between father and son, there can be no hope for us, no heaven, and no ideal world. There is none. 

We, who have inherited the bloodline of sin, who cannot escape the fetters of sinful history, who live within the realm of sin and cannot surpass that environment, how can we elucidate the relationship between the father and me? This is something we cannot do even if we try, which is why we were told to place our hearts and believe. This is the gospel that Christianity has conveyed. It is not about believing with conditions but believing through the heart. 

It is more important to understand the heart of the Father that was to be revealed through the 66 books of the Bible than to be proficient in all the words of the 66 books. We must understand the heart of the Father, who wanted to live without corruption, the heart that seeks to restore what was lost due to the fall, and the heart that desires to save fallen humanity and place them in a position that is not so. That is the issue. If you want to call God your Father and wish to be his sons and daughters, you must cross this distance. 

That is why heaven did not tell us humans to only look at the words of the Bible until death. Jesus did not say to only listen to my words until death, but rather to pray without ceasing. During his three years of public ministry, Jesus spoke many words. However, he has not told us to hold onto everything he said until now. He hoped that we would hold onto the reality of who he is and care for it. 

In the world of the heart, there is no difference; God is supremely good and high, yet we can dare to call him Father. When we grasp the heart that is deeply connected to the relationship between father and son, we cannot say, "Your hand is a different hand, your body is a different body, your heart is a different heart." If we enter the position of oneness in heart, we are the extension of the Father. We are the extension and the embodiment of the Father. That is why the Bible says our bodies are the temple of God. 

Then, how do we reconcile the content of Jesus calling God Father and our calling him Father? The issue is not whether that content is the same or different, but whether we can achieve the point of unity in heart. If that is the case, the words of Jesus, "On that day, you will know that I am in the Father, and you are in me, and I am in you" (John 14:20), are precious. 

The world of the heart transcends time. It transcends space. Here, the noun "revolution" cannot exist. Therefore, we can receive Jesus, who went 2,000 years ago, as today's Jesus and establish a relationship with him today. How can we establish this relationship? It cannot be done merely through words. We cannot have a conceptual understanding that Jesus died on the cross for me. It can only be possible through the heart. 

When we consider this perspective, Jesus, who came for the sake of earthly humans, was infinitely sorrowful. Jesus, who came on behalf of heaven, was infinitely sorrowful. His tears were tears that replaced human sorrow, and his sorrow was sorrow that replaced heavenly sorrow, which no one knew. The suffering he endured during his three years of public ministry was suffering for humanity and suffering for heaven, which no one realized. His death was a death that replaced humanity, and no one knew it was to remove the bloody marks left in the heart of heaven. 

When Jesus prayed to heaven for the last time, he said, "Abba, Father, if it is possible, let this cup pass from me; yet not as I will, but as you will" (Matthew 26:39). This was a prayer that transcended all circumstances. It was a prayer made from a position that transcended all worldly matters. Jesus thought, "I am the Father's, and the Father is mine," and he felt that his sorrow was the Father's sorrow. Therefore, he felt that his death was not a mere grievance but a unified emotion that made the Father suffer more, grieve more, and feel more pain. He knew that even while suffering such pain, there was a purpose to hold onto humanity and save all people, and we must recognize that he was able to bravely overcome that path. 

We must understand that Jesus died with the intention of finding all humanity centered around the purpose of the cross. 

It is easy to say we believe, but the problem is whether we can reach the place where we can connect our hearts with that content. If God does not seek those who can connect hearts, then true love cannot exist. 

The voice of Jesus, who called God Father, the words of Jesus who cried out for the poor children, all of those words came from God's heart and were spoken through Jesus. When you look at the words of the Bible, have you ever felt as if he is right in front of you, wanting to grasp him, saying, "Lord!"? Furthermore, have you been able to say, "Father, I am yours. My body is yours, my heart is yours, and my heartfelt emotions are yours. I have nothing that is mine apart from you"? If you have not been able to feel that, you must recognize that you have not stood in the position of a child. 

Even when Jesus forgot sleep and prayed through the night, he prayed with a grateful heart, knowing that the Father was with him. Throughout his 30 years of life, even when persecution came and the difficult cross lay before him, he lived with a heart that could overcome it. That is why Satan could not invade him. 

The world of the heart cannot be divided and remain as two. In the world of circumstances, many can move, but in the world of the heart, there cannot be two. In the position of carrying the heart of 4,000 years of history, there is nothing we can offer other than the relationship between father and son. We cannot establish any other argument there. Therefore, we must understand that every word of Jesus is the word of the Father, and Jesus's demands can be expressed as the demands of the Father. 

Do not boast about going to church and living a life of faith today. I have seen that those who may not know the words but can connect their hearts and know how to be grateful before heaven will be in a higher position in the next world than those who have lived for decades in faith and take pride in their spiritual character. 

Thus, the path to heaven is a path where everything is lost. It is a path where everything in the world must be abandoned. The sinful world, the sinful body, everything must be cast aside. What is left? It is the heart that can say, "Father!" to heaven. It is this heart that allows us to meet the Lord, who is the bridegroom. This is a worldview that can encompass the universe. Today, there is no need for any doctrine centered around any particular observance. Because Jesus was the one who had such a heart, God was present with him. We also need that. 

Jesus had almost nothing. He only had a single garment to wear. If he had anything, it would have been a staff. However, even if he had something, what would have been the most precious? There is something that cannot be exchanged for the whole universe, and that is the earnest heart that can call God Father. We must recognize that this is the entirety of Jesus's value. 

Where is the gospel of humanity? 

Paul said that all words will pass away. Faith, hope, and love, these three remain, but the greatest of these is love. The Father, who has loved humanity, which has come through the trials of history, bearing sorrow and unjust wounds, has an earnest heart. The more the persecution comes from the left and right, and the more the arrows of enemies target him, the more Paul felt the love of the Father, who earnestly wished for him to overcome it. 

That is why Paul said, "Who shall separate us from the love of Christ? Shall tribulation, or distress, or persecution, or famine, or nakedness, or peril, or sword?" (Romans 8:35). That statement is true. We cannot violate all the words and life of Jesus. God was able to raise the dead Jesus because he had such a heart for Jesus. 

The historical connections also revolutionized society at such turning points, and the connections of the heavenly order are the same. Only the heart can swallow the sorrowful history stained by sin. 

Therefore, today's history is bending into the ideological realm of Jesus. We cannot deny this. If there is any person who can remain in the ideal new world beyond the history of this reality, that person will be one who has the heart to call God Father. Furthermore, they will be one who can call Jesus the bridegroom and brother. Jesus himself said, "You are my friends," and called them brothers, so we must become those who can do so. 

If there is a gift to be given to humanity at the end of history, it is nothing other than this. All 2.7 billion people can call God Father, and not only can they emotionally elucidate the historical personality of the Father, but they can also feel that touch and elucidate themselves. If that is the case, humanity will welcome a new world. 

The hearts of humans are all heavenly. Jesus appeared with the words of the gospel and said, "You shall love me more than anyone else." He said, "I am the Son of God," and "I am the bridegroom, and you are the bride." Where is such a contradictory statement? However, it is a precious word. Before humanity, who must walk the sorrowful path of restoration, he called God Father and called us brides, so has everything not been accomplished? 

Jesus lived with such a heart from birth, spoke with such a heart, and fought against Satan for decades with such a heart. 

The gospel of humanity is not a world of circumstances but a world of hearts. It is a world where borders are transcended, and feelings seep into the heart, allowing us to say, "Oh, I see." If humans today cannot transcend the historical circumstances with such feelings of the heart, the unification ideology of God cannot be realized. If that happens, sending Jesus would be in vain, a futile effort. Calling him the bridegroom or the Father would all be mere public discourse. Therefore, when the heart becomes deeply connected, the issue is not the nation, nor is it any doctrine of the earth. If one has a heartfelt connection, they can overcome and overcome again, discard and discard again, and still be able to rejoice. At the end of history, they will inherit that. 

Jesus said, "The kingdom of heaven is within you." What does this mean? It means that the infinite kingdom of heaven is within my heart; it means that the kingdom of heaven is connected from my heart. Therefore, when we approach heaven, we cannot do so without a connection of hearts. 

If God is the Father and we are the children, then our bodies and his body are one. The blood and flesh of the Father and my blood and flesh are one, one. Isn't that the case in the world? Why do parents love their children? It is because they are extensions of their own bodies. It is the same as loving oneself. To call him Father, the bloodline must be the same. It means that the bloodline must be connected. 

In terms of heart, God and Jesus were one. When God's arteries moved, Jesus's arteries also moved, and when God's pulse beat, Jesus's pulse also beat. It was determined together. Isn't that so? And is there anyone who says to their child, "I love you"?
loves and longs for their parents. Do you have someone you love? It is something that happens automatically through blood relations. That world is a realm that transcends any logical conditions.

In Romans 8, Paul said that we are adopted children because we are fallen humans, adopted children. Please do not shout. He said that fallen humans are adopted children, adopted children. Adopted children have a different lineage.

Therefore, God is liquidating the lineage of the adopted children and is looking forward to a son who has inherited the lineage connected to the heart of the Father, a son who can naturally love even if he does not want to. This means that even if I do not say I love the Father, the Father can love me, and even if I do not say I long for the Father, I can long for Him, and even if I do not say I fight for the Father, I must have a heart that can fight for Him. However, the lack of such a heart is the heart of the fall.

Jesus was different in that regard. 

When He cried out, "Father!" even the sorrowful Father responded, "Yes." In that one word, the Father felt a heart that transcended the prayers of countless millions. The "Yes" of the Father is a natural connection centered on God's creation purpose that transcends the sorrowful history. There is a place that cannot be denied by anything, cannot be obstructed by any condition. Have you ever entered such a place?

When you enter such a place, even your cells will be moved. You may think that this young person is talking nonsense, but it does not matter what anyone says. The heart of love, the sensation of love is the essence of the entire existential world and has the taste that encompasses the whole. That is why we yearn for heaven.

If you enter such a place and pray, then night is not a problem. You transcend the awareness of whether you have eaten or slept. The world of love contains internal emotions that surpass human recognition by tens of millions of times. Isn't that so? The time when Jesus, weary and persecuted, entered the Mount of Olives and prayed quietly to heaven was a happy time that others did not know.

In that moment of crying out "Father," all of His being was immersed in the world of heart. Because He had the emotional content to forget even the death on the cross, He could bless His enemies. 

It is necessary for a place to appear in this world where one can call out "Father" with such a heart and love as a son. Jesus brought such content but could not explain the life content of the heart, which is why He must come again.

To find the point of return to call God "Father," my body must become the Father's body. My blood must become the Father's blood. When you stand in such a position, you will become a temple.

When you become a temple, that heart and body are not yours. They belong to the Father. Your origin is not yourself. It began with the Father, so it must end with the Father. Therefore, you are not yours; you are the Father's.

When you enter the emotional position where your blood and flesh replace the Father's blood and flesh, when heaven is sad, you will shed tears without even realizing it. Those who are here for the first time may wonder where such a place exists, but it does exist. The world of heart is a world that surpasses the value of all existence by tens of millions of times. When we relate to this world, we transcend awareness.

After becoming the true sons and daughters of the Father, what must we do?

To enter such a place, you must first be blood-related. You must feel that your blood and flesh are the same as the Father's blood and flesh. If you have become the true sons and daughters of the Father, then next, you must share the same will, the will. What is that will? It is to restore the fallen world. In other words, it is to create a world where the original being, the good being, can live embraced in the Father's bosom, resolving the history of human sin. Therefore, our bodies must inherit the Father's blood and flesh, and our hearts must hold the will to establish the Father's kingdom. Additionally, in our lives, we must feel the heart of the Father. Otherwise, we cannot stand as the Father's children. Isn't that right?

When the Father is sad, the children must also be sad, and when the Father is in pain, the children must also be in pain, and when the parents are living in difficult circumstances, the children must also live in difficult circumstances. Isn't that so? A true filial son must act according to the will of the parents. Thus, we must have connections through the Father's blood and flesh, connections through the will, and we must have a heart that is connected to that in order to call upon heaven as "Father." You must understand that heaven has been working hard to graft this content onto humanity.

You must not forget that heaven has worked tirelessly in ways that humanity cannot even imagine to fulfill such connections. Heaven is infinitely striving to elevate us, who are in the position of adopted children, to the position of true sons and daughters whose hearts can resonate. Even if we have grievances, they cannot be compared to God's grievances, and even if we have sorrow, it cannot be compared to God's sorrow, and even if we have anger, it cannot be compared to God's anger. Moreover, even if we suffer wounds, they cannot be compared to the wounds God has endured. God has experienced historical grievances beyond our own and has carried a sorrowful heart throughout history, and He has borne a pain that is millions of times greater than our own. We must understand that God is such a being.

The reason Satan could not accuse Jesus

Jesus knew God as His Father, but what kind of Father did He know? He felt that when He wore the crown of thorns, God was wearing a crown of thorns that was millions of times more painful than His own, and even when He was nailed to the cross, He knew that God was suffering millions of times more than He was. Even when a spear pierced His heart, Jesus accepted it as natural because He understood that God was a Father who was laboring for His children from a place of greater suffering than His own.

Thus, He could not leave behind any resentment. Even while suffering, He resolved not to leave any resentment before humanity. When He thought of the unbearable pain and resentment toward His enemies, He could not harbor such feelings. Because He was Jesus, who came to save sorrowful humanity, He had to overcome His own death and suffering. Only such a Jesus can be the Savior. Because He was a human who lost His life, He must enter a position where He does not blame heaven even if He loses His life and gives up all desires. Because Jesus entered such a position, we must understand that He could become the Savior of life who represented God's heart.

Because Jesus did not harbor feelings of resentment, did not feel anger, and was not dominated by historical grievances, Satan could not accuse Him. What is Satan? He is an existence that presents historical grievances to accuse, and when one becomes trapped in circumstances, he prevents them from going forward. However, Satan could not accuse Jesus because there were no conditions for him to latch onto, even the grievances of this fallen world, even the grievances of heaven. Satan, who protested to God with this condition, raised his hands in surrender.

When Jesus said to love your enemies, it was not a pretense. If one weeps for humanity, worrying more about their eternal death than about their own death, then Satan's very essence is destroyed. Such a person cannot be controlled by Satan. Only God can govern them. While Satan can accuse as much as he wants within the realms of faith and hope, he cannot touch the heartfelt, single-minded, earnest heart. The world that transcends all of Satan's connections is heaven, so we must understand that heaven is a world without any connection to Satan.

Today, we call upon the Father whom Jesus called, relying on His merits. It is a solemn matter. Today, we are struggling within the realm of sin, holding onto a part of our sorrowful lives and shedding tears. When we look at today's society and this world, the flowing currents are filled with historical grievances and are engulfed in fear. In this world, what occupies our emotions? It is fear. What sweeps through our lives? It is the irreparable loyalty that cannot be expressed. Furthermore, heaven wants to establish a new world and true righteousness, yet there is no one who can establish them. However, we must understand that heaven is still searching for such people today.

The position of the Korean people from the perspective of providence and their path to survival

Even if the thirty million people of this nation do not know God, we must understand that God has been with the history of this nation. If there was any loyal person who disappeared like dew on the gallows to establish the loyalty of a faithful heart, heaven remembers that person's footsteps and heart, or has traversed over that nation.

Today, I am a debtor. This nation is a nation among debtor nations. If heaven is a God who seeks to save the poor, a God who weeps for fallen children, then He will look upon a nation that is poorer with more pity than a nation that is well-off.

Our nation has nothing to boast about before other nations. We have not been able to possess what we should have. Everything has been taken away, and we have lost everything. If we can gain anything again from here, I desire that the passionate young men and women who are wandering without knowing their path may awaken the burning heart that Jesus had when He called heaven "Father."

If they become like that, no other nation will be able to dominate this nation.

Before the heart of the Father who looks upon us with pity, we must say, "Father! This is how I was." Even if there are many sons and daughters, we will renew the will and ideology that must be abandoned in this world and that must inevitably fall apart. Under the oppression of Rome, the religious currents were in chaos, the spirit of the nation had completely fallen apart, and everything associated with it was shaken. In such a time of profound sorrow, heaven sent Jesus.

The lamentable and sorrowful fact is why Korea has appeared as a sacrifice at the focal point of the confrontation between the two major camps of democracy and communism. It is a sad fact. If anything can emerge that can establish a relationship with heaven, this nation will survive.

We must understand that the Korean people today are in a period of spiritual confusion. They are in an environment where they cannot boast of their character, feeling fear in their lives, and all currents are sweeping away our nation entirely. In this time, what can we hold onto for rest?

The path the Korean people must take

Jesus came to this earth as the Son of God, but He walked a tragic life of over thirty years filled with sorrow and a three-year public ministry of suffering. However, regardless of what obstacles may arise, He possessed a noble spirit and a burning heart that could have restored the entire nation of Israel. Such a courageous person is needed in this era. When that nation pushed Jesus into a corner, He was the one who went up to the Garden of Gethsemane, unable to sleep, praying for them. That demeanor is admirable.

When Jesus faced persecution from the state and nation, He sought a quiet place to call upon the Father in heaven, and He overcame those challenges. Thus, the path to survival for this nation does not lie elsewhere. There must be a heart. Forgetting about eating, forgetting about wearing clothes, and disregarding all human conditions, we must be able to say, "Father, I am Your son, I am Your daughter." This nation, in a pitiful situation, is searching for a path to survival, seeking the heart of God. Even in such a position, we must be able to say, "Father, thank You." There is a world of difference between a nation that complains against heaven in a free situation and a nation that sheds tears of gratitude toward heaven even in difficult circumstances.

Now, God and we are like a father and son.
