Therefore, even if you are wounded while working for the will, do not become one who weeps over your own wounds, but rather comfort the Father who is wounded even more than you. He is the Father who forgets His own wounds and comes to us, shedding tears over us. It is a solemn and profound matter.

Now we must do something. The national spirit of this nation is becoming thin. What will this nation present before the heavenly principle? Today, this world and this era have no content to present. What has not been touched until today? It is because of God's heart. Then, who can deeply feel this world of heart? It is those who participate in difficult situations. That is why we find ourselves in such difficult circumstances. If we look closely, our nation has no need to lament. If heaven were not present, it would be sorrowful, but if heaven is present, there is no need to be sorrowful. Personally, we must approach Heaven with the heart of a filial son, and nationally and ethnically with the spirit of a loyal subject. Isn't that right? The same applies to this world. The content of the heart may differ, but it is the same.

Members of the Unification Church! Our issue is not with denomination. Our label is not the problem. This sanctuary or home is not the issue. The problem is people. It is not just any person, but those who carry a heart. Even if there are 2.7 billion people in the world, there is only one person who can resonate with your heart. Isn't that so? The same goes for God. Even now, God, who moves all things in the heavenly realm and the entire universe, desires one person who can forget everything and fall asleep after giving all their heart, rather than many people. Isn't that so? More than many, He dreamed of that one person.

Where are the sons and daughters who can call out to the Father, longing for Him whom they have sought and wandered for? The day we find such sons and daughters is the day of hope and the day of resolution. If we were to borrow the words of religious masters, that day is called the day of the Lamb's feast.

Then what kind of true Christian is one? It is not someone who dances with joy. It is someone who prays with concern for God. It is not someone who prays out of concern for themselves, but someone who prays out of concern for God. It is not someone who worries about not being able to become a bride, but someone who worries that the Bridegroom, Jesus, may not be pleased.

It is someone who prays not to be sent to heaven, but rather, "Father, please resolve Your grief." It is not asking for recognition of one's value in heaven, but rather, "Even if I die now, let my Father's value be recognized on earth."

Today, we must overturn our beliefs. We must fundamentally overturn them. Do I believe I will go to heaven? What will I do in heaven? Will I steal again? That is to lose the essence of heaven and rejoice in it. What is meant to be given has become the essence. Even the fallen nature can feel that the essence of love is such. For those who struggle to receive, the pit of death awaits, while for those who strive to give, the right to resurrection of life awaits.

The one who lived for over 30 years striving to give was Jesus. During His three years of public life, He strived to give and ultimately gave His own body. We must understand that the prince who struggled to give and to lose was the Messiah.

We must reflect on how much we have become a sacrifice to resolve the Father's grief in our daily lives. If there is such a person, they would be someone who has no concept of heaven or hell. They would say, "What does it matter if I go to hell or heaven?" When such a person is resurrected by Heaven, even Satan will have no choice but to say, "That is right." We must understand that this is where the historical standard of life is established.

Today, for you members of the Unification Church to comfort the grieving Father, what must be done? The words of the Bible are necessary. A teacher is necessary. However, I do not want you to look to any teacher. I hope you will become those who can connect the heart of the Father through that teacher. If you pray for the nation, you must become those who can emotionally appeal to Heaven, strive to introduce the heart of Heaven, and be willing to become a sacrifice. If you do so, Heaven will not abandon you. Heaven will not give up on us.

When you think of Heaven, remember that Heaven is the master of all things, but has He ever acted as such? Has He ever said to humanity, "I love you"? He has not. Even from a position where He can possess everything, He has never claimed humanity as His own and taken them freely. He intended to establish a relationship with the earthly realm by appointing Jesus to command the angelic world, but that has not happened. Although He has given the ideal of a bride to humanity on earth and sought a bride, He has not found even one person who can boast of being a bride before Satan. We are deeply sorry before such a God.

This is not the time to fight over that. It is a time when I am busy living and trying to reach the stage where I can be recognized before the Father.

Dear friends, we are all equally pitiful beings. There was a time when we vowed to call the Father while saying we would die together. There were times when we called the Father with tears. We had to stand in this position on behalf of this nation, and even if it was a sorrowful time, we must go on the path left by the Father. No matter how torn or miserable this body may be, we are those who should not feel sorrowful about collapsing somewhere. Today, if there is a gathering where I can share my heart, where I can kneel in harmony with the heart, where I can speak and cry with the heart, then I assure you that Heaven will surely lead that gathering along with history.

The faith of Mary Magdalene towards Jesus
When Mary Magdalene, who was merely a sinner, knelt down and poured perfume worth 300 denarii on Jesus' feet and wiped His feet with her hair, and when Judas Iscariot rebuked her, Jesus defended Mary. She was not a person who understood the situation. She worried about the heart of Jesus, who was to die, and a part of God's sorrowful heart appeared in Mary, which is why Jesus foretold that her name would be remembered wherever the gospel is preached.

When Mary Magdalene saw the resurrected Jesus at the tomb and tried to hold Him, Jesus stopped her, fearing that the resurrection itself might be defiled. He had the heart that was more joyful to welcome the Father than to be welcomed Himself, and that before being joyful about Himself, He wanted to be joyful about the Father and hoped that humanity could have hope for revival. It was with such feelings that He stopped her. It is a sorrowful thing that the Jesus who came with such unfair feelings is the same Jesus we believe in today. It is a sad thing.

Today, we must let all Christians around the world know this. We need people who can boast of Jesus while being trampled by history and pushed out, rather than those who call out the name of Jesus and boast of their faith. We need people like Mary Magdalene, who sought Him on Calvary, rather than the twelve disciples who turned away, saying they did not know Him and sought their own way.

To become the sons and daughters that the Father desires

The title of today's message is "The Father and I," but it is a humbling thing to even dare to call Him Father. We must have a time when saying "Father" is a solemn matter. "Father, how can someone like me dare to call You Father?" We must hold such a heart. There is no need for other words. Human beings are explorers searching for truth.  
John 10:1-18  
<Prayer> We have read the permitted words. We see that countless people living on this earth are busy boasting of themselves before the universe while being in the place of death. The final decision on the value of my heart and body is not something I can make, and I am a miserable self who cannot lead myself to the destination through the process of manifested phenomena. Please allow me to feel this at this time.
Before us, we acknowledge that if we have life, it is not from ourselves. If there is any ideology that guides our hearts towards goodness, it is also derived from something that is not ours. May this moment allow us to feel that truth.

Father, today we despise the appearance of those who were busy justifying themselves. It is time to find the heart that seeks the truth. We must know how to disregard and trample upon the arrogance that seeks to elevate itself, and become victors who can conquer the self. Let us realize that this is what heaven, earth, the world, humanity, society, our families, and ourselves are seeking at this time.

Jesus said, "Forsake all and follow me." He said, "Those who seek to live will die, and those who seek to die will live." He also said, "Those who seek to be high will be brought low, and those who seek to be low will be exalted." When we come to understand the meaning of these words, we will realize that we, as individuals who bear the lineage of the fallen ancestors and cannot escape the ties of fallen history, are destined to abandon, abandon, and abandon again.

For this reason, our life journey today is a tragic one, and our living environment is so complex that we live in a state of confusion where we cannot discern between good and evil. Heaven has strived to pave a path of life on this earth, and we know that many prophets have come and gone to introduce the true appearance of a true person, a true ideology, and the true nature of the universe.

Among them, we must long for the majestic figure of Jesus Christ, who appeared on this earth as the Messiah of all people, who could pray for the blessings of all even as he disappeared like a mere speck on the cross, and the deep heart and fervent ideology that flowed from him.

Even in this time when we should despise ourselves, we have elevated ourselves, despising all things, and we earnestly hope that you will forgive us, Father. If we wish to move towards a true heart and true goodness, let us realize that we are indebted before heaven and earth and that we are a sinful lineage that has suffered countless wounds throughout human history. Now, what we need is a heart that can search for the Father and a loyalty that can seek our original self. Father, please grant us that.

We cannot deny that the life journey of Jesus was a path of tears and that every page of the history we have lived through has been woven with bloody battles. Thus, we earnestly hope that we may realize that we cannot explain anything historically nor possess anything to boast about in this era, and that we stand as cosmic failures.

However, let us examine ourselves to see if we possess the qualities, loyalty, and heart that are worthy to approach that Messiah. Even if we are not in such a position, we earnestly hope that you will guide us to be humble sons and daughters who can kneel and seek the grace of atonement with a heart that longs for that position.

Father, how shall we treat the words you have allowed us? Father, please be with us. We have heard many words until now, taken many steps, and experienced various circumstances, yet we stand before you empty-handed, having nothing to offer. Father, do not cast us away but look upon us with compassion. We earnestly ask that this hour may be one where we empty our hearts and bodies so that only you can govern and fill us with your grace.

May the hearts of the messenger and the receiver become one, and may their hearts harmonize so that they can communicate with your heart and directly receive your grace during this hour. We earnestly ask this, and we pray all these words in your name. Amen.

Fallen Humanity and Jesus

You possess a heart and a body. Humans demand a heart that can resonate with their ideals. Therefore, unless we establish some standard that can govern our feelings and the external life that can govern our flesh and adjust our actual lives, humanity will not be able to escape the position of struggling in any era.

Therefore, there was a single heart that resonated with Jesus as he sought that boundary. Thus, even if anything from heaven and earth were to sweep over him, the heart that was resonating within him remained inviolable.

The reason Jesus could strike down Satan in the process of fighting centered around providential conditions was not because of his own greatness. It was because he had a deep heart for heaven. In the battle against Satan occurring in heaven, even Satan had to raise his hands before his profound heart. Every time he faced such situations, Noah said to himself, "I must endure; heaven has promised and is leading me. How can I change against the heart that heaven has established?" He struck his own body and overcame all difficulties. 

If Noah's family had cast aside all worldly conditions and looked toward the nation with Noah's heart, God's will would have been fulfilled at that time. If Noah's family had established the family purpose and looked toward the nation, God's will would have been accomplished through that nation.

However, Noah's family could not establish the family purpose and broke apart. Nevertheless, the providence to fulfill the will continued. It is not the time of heavenly principles to hold onto the individual just because the individual has broken. Just because the family has broken does not mean that the heavenly principles do not move forward. Even if the individual breaks, the heavenly principles continue to move.

Thus, even if the individual has broken, because the time for the family has come, God must carry out the providence to establish the family. It must work on both the individual and the family. Moreover, just because the family breaks does not mean that the time of providence can be delayed. This time of providence moves forward to restore society.
Furthermore, the environment has expanded to a national level. After losing Noah and his family, God established Abraham to work again after 400 years. However, even the lost heaven until Abraham was restored again through Moses after 400 years. As the national era approached, the Israelite people were driven into Egypt and were refined. Refinement means being struck. What does striking mean? It is an operation to unite. It is an operation to create one.

God said to the Israelite people, "The land you are living in is the land of the enemy, and the palace you are facing is the palace of the enemy, and the Egyptians are your eternal enemies." The place where the Israelite people should live is all correct. It must be a place they can enter, so heaven drove out the Israelite people while looking forward to the time when they could enter that one place. And because that time was when providence had to be carried out from a national perspective, Moses, who represented the nation, was appointed as the vanguard of the adventure. This vanguard of the adventure, Moses, was the greatest explorer among those going toward the unknown land of Canaan and the greatest scout among the scouts. Moses appeared as the greatest warrior of exploration.

The path that Moses took, leading the Israelite people while breaking through the obstacles of the palace, was not a smooth path. It was an unknown journey. However, he had a firm heart that no matter what difficulties lay ahead, if they were to block him, let them block him. Would the heart he bore to find the land of Canaan, which God had promised since the time of his ancestors, change? Even though he lived in Pharaoh's land, he had the heart to sing of happiness in the land of Canaan. Until that day came, he persevered with an indomitable spirit and forged ahead with a united heart.

Thus, he set out toward Canaan with 600,000 people but lost them all during the 40 years in the wilderness. If the Israelite people had known how to take risks like Moses, they would not have perished. If their earnest desire to find the promised land had been stronger than the feelings or perceptions they experienced in their lives, the Israelite people would not have fallen in the wilderness. But they cried out, "Oh, we are hungry. Oh, we are going to die." And so they died in the wilderness without ever entering the land of Canaan.

Historical figures or pioneers did not seek the pleasures or satisfactions of the world, but rather possessed an adventurous spirit that overcame everything toward a higher ideal, aiming for the promised one place as their destination. Moses was no different. What was the Red Sea to the Israelite people rushing forward, and what was the attack of the Amalekites in the wilderness? During the 40 years of wandering, all the able-bodied men who had been released from Pharaoh's bondage fell along the way.

When Moses sent 12 men to scout the land on behalf of the 12 tribes, when they returned to report, 10 said, "We cannot take them." But Joshua and Caleb did not say that. Joshua and Caleb were not the smartest people of their time. You are smarter than them now. They were stubborn adventurers, not knowing whether they would live or die. Joshua and Caleb boldly declared before the nation that was raising a banner, "The God who has led us until now is alive. The God who defeated Pharaoh's sorcery is alive. The God who parted the Red Sea that was blocking us is alive. The God who fed us quail and manna when we were starving in the wilderness is alive." This is something you should understand, as it opened the way for the Israelite people who were wandering to find the path of restoration.

Not only that, but the historical process has been entirely such a path. After passing through the national era, the state era came to Israel. What God seeks in the end time

What I want to shout to this era is this: Where is the historical individual that heaven seeks? Where is the family that replaces Noah's family? 4) True Sons and Daughters of the Father Who Will Remain in the End Times
Romans 8:12-27

104   In the last days, I know that there will be true sons and daughters of the Father. I earnestly ask that we become one heart, one mind, and that we may be able to serve the Father together in this time. I offer all these words in the name of the Lord. Amen.

<Words> Today, I will speak to you on the topic of the true sons and daughters of the Father who will remain in the last days.

To become God's true sons and daughters, 

Throughout human history, no matter how much power, character, or glory one may possess, there has never been a person who stood up and boasted, "I am a true son or daughter of God." To become a true son or daughter, one must have true parents, must be connected through the relationship of a true family, and must have some content connected to true siblings. Without these, one cannot stand in the environment or position of a son or daughter.

If God exists and has been carrying out a certain providence for humanity, what would be the highest purpose that God desires through this providence? It is nothing other than finding and establishing a person who can say, "You are my true son or daughter." Thus, the highest purpose of God is to have a day when He can say, "You are my son, you are my daughter," in a position where He can communicate with that true son or daughter and connect with all relationships in the world of existence. We must not forget that God is longing for such a day.

If there is a Creator, the root of the universe, and a center that becomes the subject of all existence, then the ideal world that this center desires cannot be the world of existence on this earth. The world that God desires is not the world of any ideal in the heavens, nor is it an external world. That world is one where the flow of heart can be centered around relationships, where one can be called a son or daughter. Therefore, no matter how great, wonderful, or absolute God may be, we cannot deny that He desires a person who possesses such content.

History is aiming for the true. It seeks true people, true nations, and a true world. We ourselves also look forward to becoming true beings.

So, what is the standard relationship among true relationships? It is the relationship of father and son established between God and humanity. The heart that arises from this relationship is eternal, unchanging, and unique, and cannot be bent by any authority of existence. Furthermore, the authority of this heart is absolute. Therefore, when it manifests with this authority, all beings will have no choice but to bow before it, and when it moves with this authority, everything must follow it. This is the iron rule of the universe. If this is not the case, we will not be able to achieve the true purpose we desire, and it will be concluded that we cannot establish an absolute relationship.

For this reason, no matter how high and great God may be, the greatest sorrow is that He cannot have a day when He can say, "My beloved true son, my beloved daughter." There is nothing more sorrowful than this. Additionally, if humanity, created through the heavenly relationship, cannot bring forth such a person, such a son or daughter, it is the greatest sorrow. This is the sorrow of sorrows for humanity.

If there are true sons and daughters whom God can call His children, and if in that moment He can forget the hardships of the past 6,000 years and all the twists and turns of history, the heavenly restoration will begin from there. Humanity will then be able to sing the song of happiness brought by God. We must anticipate that such a time will come.

If there is an end to humanity and the heavenly principle, what kind of day should that end be? It should be a day when God can say to humanity, "You are my true son and daughter, whom I can never deny. My son, my daughter, I have now resolved all grievances." It must be a day when we can rest assured and enjoy ourselves. The day when such sons and daughters appear on this earth will mark the beginning of God's new ideal world.

However, until now, such sons and daughters have not emerged, and we have not established a time that can determine the relationship of true sons and daughters. No being has appeared who can be proclaimed as a true son or daughter. Until such a being appears, we must understand that God's will and humanity's hope will not be fulfilled.

God's effort to find true sons and daughters and the mission of religion

Today, we recognize that we are fallen descendants. No matter how great anyone in the world may claim to be, or how they boast of their traditions and historical contributions, all of it is merely the pride of fallen descendants. Even if one possesses a noble appearance or claims to have the authority to pierce the heavens, it is still the authority of fallen descendants. Because humanity is in a situation of adversity and in an environment that heaven cannot permit, the human world is a world of sin that is in opposition to heaven. It is a world of sinful humanity and sinful existence. This is something that everyone knows well.

The appearance of God's true sons and daughters is that of the utmost goodness and height, while our appearance living on this earth is extremely evil and wretched. How can we bridge this gap? The history of God's salvation is aimed at overcoming this gap. God has worked tirelessly over the long span of 6,000 years to fill and connect this gap, and we must understand that the history of God is the bloody battle that humanity has fought behind the scenes, whether they know it or not.

As we contemplate how to repay such historical efforts of heaven, no one feels ashamed or humbled before heaven, nor do they repent of themselves.

Today, when we establish the noun "religion" or raise leaders with the content of religion to announce and advise humanity, what is it? It is a teaching that instructs us to know the historical content that God has providentially guided through the course of life and to connect with the heart of heaven through our own sentiments. This is the role of religion.

However, it has been easy for religious individuals to ignore or forget the relationships that extend from heart to heart, becoming fixated only on the facts that appear today. The significant task of religion has been to transcend the relationships of fall and to possess a heart that can accompany the historical sorrow and pain that heaven has endured while holding onto humanity. Yet, religion has not fulfilled the task of supplementing human history and connecting the hearts of humanity from such a standpoint.

For this reason, the more earnest the heart of heaven is to find true sons and daughters, the more it has longed for them throughout the ages and centuries, laboring for humanity until now.

To achieve this one purpose, heaven has established individuals, families, nations, and global leading ideologies and has been carrying out providence. Heaven has worked so hard to achieve this one purpose. Nevertheless, the chosen Israelite nation, which was to be responsible for that purpose, has gone astray. The 600,000 Israelites who were drawn from the palace have vanished without a trace. The more we understand history and God's providential will, the more we realize that God's sorrow is beyond expression. The end days and the Lord of the Second Advent

What is the purpose that God aims for? It is the mission to connect from true children who can communicate with the true to families, nations, states, the world, and the cosmos. That person is the Lord who is coming.

Jesus taught us, "I am the bridegroom, and you are the bride." That day will be the day when the world connected to those sons and daughters will be mobilized to praise heaven all at once.

Before God, who has come forth with humanity, who has grieved with humanity, and who has fought alongside humanity, what will humanity pray? It will be, "Please let the true son you wish to establish appear." Then, who is that true son? He must be a true son who also possesses the qualifications of a true bridegroom, seeking a true bride and becoming the true parent of humanity.

Therefore, God's history of salvation is to lead humanity historically and to connect them with true sons and daughters.

Among the words we read today, it was said, "You have received the spirit of adoption, by which we cry, 'Abba, Father.'" It was also said that even we, who have received the first fruits of the Spirit, are eagerly awaiting adoption. Therefore, no matter how well someone living on this earth believes, they are merely adopted children before heaven. If there is a son of heaven, how will that son appear? There are those who are not sons, there are adopted children, and there are true sons. Isn't it the same in the world? There are children who are not my own, and when there are no sons, there are adopted children who can serve as a bridge, and there are true sons. The principles of heaven and earth are the same.

Today, this earth is in chaos, with good and evil intersecting and colliding, where what seems true is not true, and what seems not true is true. This is the reality. Heaven has a heart and an ideal to find true sons and daughters, and even with such sentiments, as it has walked through the historical course, who are the true sons and daughters on this earth? Humanity does not know. No one will know. However, heaven must gather those who are not sons in the human world in the form of adopted children and must conclude them as direct children. This is the history of heaven's providence of salvation.

The relationship of a son must be connected by blood. One can only establish the title of son or daughter from a position where their bloodline is directly connected, or where their father or ancestor's bloodline is connected. This is the principle of the world. The principle of heaven is the same.

From the day Adam and Eve, the ancestors of humanity, were created, God's heart flowed through their bones to establish a single conclusion, and if the entirety of that ideal had been bestowed upon Adam and Eve, we would have become children who could communicate through the direct lineage of God's bloodline. However, due to the fall, we are now connected to an unwanted different bloodline. Therefore, no matter how great we may think we are today, our bloodlines are different, so we are adopted. No matter how much we strive for the providential will, we can only continue the bloodline of adopted children. This is the content of the New Testament salvation providence that Jesus has established and has continued until now.

Then, can God establish that adopted child and say, "You are my true son or daughter"? No, He cannot. The same goes for worldly matters. Even if someone who has suffered pain and injustice speaks words that are filled with emotion, those who stand in a position that does not connect with that emotion will only understand to a certain extent. Some may think, "That could be true," while others may think, "What do you mean by that?" However, those who have experienced it and are in a position to connect with that emotion will feel the sadness in the speaker's words when that sadness seeps into their hearts. Only then can one say they are in the same position. Is that not so?

The desires of humanity and the purpose of the Lord's return

What does humanity desire today? It is to remove the title of adopted child before God and to become direct true sons and daughters. This is the highest purpose that humanity desires and the central purpose of God's providence that history aims to establish. Only in this way can the purpose of salvation be achieved, and the providence of salvation be concluded.

If the great God, the essence of love, and the center of love loves us humans from the position of adopted children, we do not desire such love. What is required is the reality of love, which can seep into the marrow of our hearts—true sons and daughters.

Today, no matter how much one lives a life of virtue and calls God "Father," the content of that Father is diverse. There may be those who call Him "Father" from the position of not being a son, and there may be those who call Him "Father" from the position of being an adopted child. However, what is the highest purpose that heaven desires to remain in the end? It is to look forward to true sons and daughters who transcend the position of adopted children and are direct children.

The Bible states that Jesus restores the relationship of adoption, and even if one finds satisfaction in that ideal world, that salvation is not complete. Many saints who have believed in Jesus until now have gone to the other world, but they are waiting in the waiting room of paradise, that is, heaven. Therefore, the purpose for which Jesus said He would return is to establish a direct relationship for us, not an adopted one.

God desires sons and daughters who can be intertwined with emotions, who do not move by teachings or commands but can look at the manifested appearance and move and establish relationships.

For this reason, even the saints who have come and gone in the historical course, known as the wise and enlightened, have not...
You can call Him Father, and if God does not have the content to say to that person, "You are my son," then they are incomplete. This must be clearly understood. 

The unique aspect of Christianity lies here. Jesus called God "My Father," and He referred to Himself as the only begotten Son. He was Jesus, who established a standard that could penetrate the fundamental principles of the universe and occupy the realm of heart. From this, we can see that Jesus is the Messiah of all people.

What is the Messiah, the Savior? It is a figure who can bring back to life those who are trapped in the realm of death. Therefore, if there is any condition of love that Christianity possesses, it is only this.

If a relationship is established where God is my Father, then no matter how high and good God is as the subject of goodness and the Absolute, that God becomes my Father. When that happens, what belongs to God becomes mine, and I become God's. This is likely to be the highest standard of hope that humanity desires.

If God proclaims the highest standard of love and yet cannot guide humanity to the destination of that love, then God would be a false being. If that were the case, it would lead to the conclusion that God has been working for His own desires and ambitions, not for the ideals of humanity and the ideals of the whole. That is why Heaven is seeking true sons and daughters.

The reason God is seeking true sons and daughters
Through the 66 books of the Bible, we find Paul's words that correspond to this content. We, who are free from sin by bloodline, can receive the inheritance of adoption through our faith in the resurrected Jesus. However, this was not the ultimate purpose for which Jesus came.

The purpose for which God sent Jesus was to establish a connection between humanity and God's true Son, Jesus, and to graft them into Jesus. The Scripture also states, "I am the vine, and you are the branches." Thus, He intended to provide a process for humans from the world of Satan, who are not sons, to become direct sons through the relationship of adoption. However, because humanity did not believe, Jesus could not teach the method of becoming direct children while He was on earth; He only explained the content of how to become adopted.

Why do we long for the coming Lord? Why does all of humanity await the day of Jesus' second coming? No matter how capable one may be, they can only be in the position of an adopted child, and thus, there is a mission to establish a heartfelt connection that allows them to become direct children. Therefore, all of humanity will surely look forward to that day. We must know Jesus, who came and went with such a mission.

For us, who are moving forward while anticipating the day of the second coming, what kind of day will that day be? It will be a day when Heaven lays bare all the hard work of 6,000 years, a day when Heaven forgets all the sorrow of 6,000 years, and a day when all the suffering can be forgotten. When we look at the found appearance of the Son, there will be no sorrow, no pain, and no grievance. 

It will be a day of joy when we can say, "Yes, my son." That day is the day Heaven has been waiting for, and it is the day that humanity on earth has been longing for throughout a long historical journey.

In other words, when we can transcend the position of an adopted child and stand as direct children, saying that my Father's heaven is my heaven, and that the world my Father governs is the world I can govern, we will be able to appear as true owners of the garden, just like Adam and Eve before the fall, as the lords of all creation.

Even if one claims to govern all creation, if there is no content to communicate emotionally, creation will not want to be governed. If we are to be called true sons and daughters, we must stand in the position to resolve historical grievances. That is why the Bible says, "Creation waits in eager expectation for the children of God to be revealed." If one is not recognized as a true son or daughter, creation does not desire such a person. Therefore, we must go through the historical process of resolving Heaven's grievances today.

What position are you in?
At this time, when we are all saying that the end is near, what should we do? This is a significant question. 

Everyone, examine yourselves. What position are you in? Can you truly resonate with Heaven's heart, moving together when the Father moves, aligning when the Father aligns, feeling sorrow when the Father is sorrowful, and rejoicing when the Father rejoices? Even if the body is different, are you in a position where you can connect in the realm of heart? Are you in a relational connection?

No matter how luxurious and splendid the external environment may be, if it contradicts the heart, it can only be a fleeting illusion. The same goes for the world. No matter how precious the possessions of beloved sons and daughters may be, if those sons and daughters die, they can only be an illusion.

Becoming true sons and daughters through the connection of heart is the highest purpose desired by Heaven and the highest goal pursued by humanity. Therefore, from a calm perspective, critically assess what stage you are at now. After all, we are centered around the history of restoration to become true sons and daughters. We cannot deny that we are situated within the providential realm of heaven and earth.

So, how will you clarify your way through this process? There is no other way but to return centered on God's heart. That is why you must critically examine how your heart stands. This is the time to do so.

If the direction that Heaven aims for is such, and if that is what the Father desires, then what level are you at today? If you are in the realm of true sons and daughters where hearts resonate, you will not need prayer.

If you simply call out "Father," your heart will be filled with a shock as if your blood and flesh are moving, and you will have become a direct son or daughter whose heart of the Father can permeate your own heart. If that were the case, just thinking about it would allow you to resolve the grievances of the fall, and you would not be able to act in the fallen ways of the world.

Knowing the heart of God, who has grieved throughout history, and thinking about my efforts to escape the burdensome ties of sin that have caused God pain, sends chills down my spine. What feelings have you experienced? Critically assess yourself. How close are you to being in a position where you can claim the title of son before God, who is searching for true sons and daughters? If you are unsure whether you have a heartfelt connection, then you are not a son. However, those who can qualify as adopted children may not know the content of the Father's suffering, but they should be able to understand it to some degree when they hear it. 

Even if they cannot experience it emotionally, they should at least be able to say, "Yes, that is true." Have you reached such a position?

Jesus came to this earth as the true Father of humanity, as the true Son of God, and He died on the cross. He must have come with a decision that God had after 4,000 years concerning the people of the earth. Therefore, His eyes were the substitute for the eyes of God that had looked upon humanity for 4,000 years, His ears were the substitute for the ears of God that had listened for 4,000 years, and His mouth was the substitute for the mouth of God that had spoken for 4,000 years. His emotions and body were the same. He was a historical reality and a historical fruition. That is why Jesus also said, "I have come to fulfill the law." The purpose is the same.

Who is Jesus?

What does this mean? The people of that time did not know; they were unaware. He is searching for the lost Adam and the lost Eve.

You may be here today, but for you who are at the end, you need ancestors who can stand before the Father and boast about having the authority of victory, having cast off the ties of the fall that have persisted for 6,000 years, and who can confront Satan without dying. In the end times, many people come out with a religious view centered around themselves, claiming, "I am the center of the universe." He is the Second Adam. Although people talk about God and Jesus, that is not the case. The Bible refers to Jesus as the Last Adam.

God's position and Jesus' life

Today, we believe that Heaven is a garden of happiness, but it is not so. Go and check. No matter how much you search for joyful content, it is not found. Even with the authority to govern the world, there is no joy to be found.

Jesus came to this earth as the King of Kings. He was recognized with the authority of a leader from heaven and appeared on earth. However, from the day he was born, he had not a single hour of joy. Why was that? Because Jesus had to indemnify 4,000 years of history. To become the King of Kings, he first had to pass as the Prince of Sorrow and the Prince of Pain. Otherwise, he would not be able to comfort the countless spirits who passed through the heavenly sorrow.

Thus, the path of Jesus, who lived for over 30 years and went through three years of public ministry, was a sorrowful path. Today, we thought of Jesus as the Prince of Love, the Prince of Happiness, and the Prince of Glory, but he is the Prince of Pain and the Prince of Sorrow.

Jesus was a successful candidate in heart, appearing with the authoritative heart of a leader. What kind of Savior is he? A Savior of the body? No. He is the Savior of the heart, who is deeply missed, longed for, and wished to live together forever. Then, for whom did this Father endure such suffering? It was for pitiful humanity. When we think of this, we must have an overwhelming heart. *5) The humans standing in God's racecourse
1 Corinthians 9:14-27
<Prayer> Father, I know that this day is a time to share the words of your providential will, gathered with many of your sons and daughters who have gathered the flock of sheep. Please move upon their hearts and bodies with the same grace. We have also gathered before you as one of those, so Father, please look upon our standing with compassion and our sitting with pity.

Now, if there are any claims of the Lord centered around me or any conscious concepts that I feel, please remove all of these. We are in a fate that must be recreated, and we cannot escape the grief of restoration, so even if we have something to claim boldly before heaven, we know that it cannot be any ideological condition or object before you.

No matter how much we try to justify ourselves before heaven and present our difficulties, we know that we are pitiful and miserable beings that cannot be compared to your infinite goodness and efforts.

Now that I know I am not myself, I long for the original self that allowed me to be myself, and I ask that this hour be one where I can bow my head before the original protagonist.

My heart knows that there is an absolute protagonist of the universe. When I realize that this is what regulates all my actions, I understand that I am a being destined to go through an environment limited by an absolute purpose, not a purposeless connection. Please allow me to be a son or daughter who can feel this.

Now, with my heart picturing the glorious throne of the Father, I have gathered before the Father's knees, and I wonder where their hearts will flow and where their hearts will turn.
I do not know whether I am moving, Father, I earnestly ask that You guide me in a direction where my true self can enjoy with Heaven. Even if our faces are shameful and our gazes are shameful, we can look to You, longing for Your heart, and even that is embarrassing. Father! I hope that if I reach out with my inadequate hands, it will become a moment of promise where You will hold that hand. 

Even when we worship, we want to hold onto Your heart, and we wish to establish a connection with You, desiring nothing else. Even if there are splendid and glorious conditions like the treasures of Heaven, we do not wish for them, but only desire that one promise to hold onto Your heart and be able to dwell with You. We hope that such things will become eternal symbols of glory that we can boast of forever, and we bow before You, Father. Even if there is something lacking in us today, Father, please forgive us. We earnestly hope and wish that You will establish the heart that You wish to establish and bind us in an unbreakable father-child relationship with You.

Many people call upon You, but they do not know Your circumstances and Your heart. We do not wish to be such sons and daughters. Among sons, there are those who are like sons, adopted sons, and true sons, but we do not wish to be like sons or adopted sons. We wish to be true sons and daughters, who cannot forever disappear from Your heart, who cannot deny the fact that our flesh and blood are eternally connected to You, and who can dwell with You forever.

To become such sons and daughters, we must feel that the suffering You endured is our suffering, that Your sorrow is our sorrow, that Your grievances are our grievances, and that the responsibilities You must fulfill are the responsibilities we must bear. We earnestly hope and wish to become such beings.

Father, now that we stand here, what words shall we convey? We wish to become Your sons and daughters, but if at this moment we cannot feel the fact that You wish to share Your heart and establish a connection with us, then no matter how amazing the words may be, we know that a connection cannot be established between You and us. Therefore, we earnestly hope and wish that this time will be a moment where we can touch Your heart, communicate with Your heart, and hold onto Your body.

Now, may the heart of the one conveying the message be allowed to resonate with Your heart, and may the heart of the one listening respond to Your heart, creating a moment of glory exchanged between us. May we lose all of ourselves and be reshaped, and may we be able to move according to Your will in search of our original nature. Thus, I earnestly hope and wish that a self-governing history that longs for Your original form will unfold at this time.

On this day, lonely family members are widely scattered, enduring the arrows of severe persecution, yet they are appealing to Heaven, so please bless them. We know that even being driven along this path is part of Your will, and that this path is the final path of destiny that cannot be avoided. May our determined resolutions and all our actions become conditions for victory and be offered as sacrifices before You, and may we be shaped into sons and daughters who can live within Your promise. I earnestly ask that Satan may not find a way in at this time. I pray in Your name. Amen.

<Words> In 1 Corinthians 9:24, it says, "Do you not know that in a race all the runners run, but only one receives the prize? So run that you may obtain it." Based on this word, I would like to speak briefly before you under the title "Human Beings Standing in God's Racecourse."

Human beings are runners who have entered the racecourse of restoration providence. Just as many prophets of the past have done, so do the people living today, whether they know it or not, run their life paths toward some goal. Although the goal may be vague, it is a fact that various forms of life are unfolding toward that goal, and the forms of nations and history are also unfolding in various ways.

All of this has not appeared as a result without any connection. We must understand that it is moving toward some purpose under some connection. If we do not move centered on such connections and purposes, we cannot establish the existence of God or anything else.

If God exists, He will want to establish a connection with fallen humanity. Therefore, we cannot deny that we live within that realm of connection as we move toward some purpose.

We know that humanity, due to the fall, has not been able to establish a connection with God and has formed a connection with Satan and evil. God does not wish to abandon us, who have such connections with evil, but rather seeks to find us. We know that we are indeed holding onto the historical path of humanity, coming down to find us again.

The direction of history is moving toward a time that fulfills such a purpose. Therefore, you must recognize that you are a runner who is running toward that destination centered on your conscience through your life.

Anyone who has come and gone on this earth has been a human being standing in the racecourse of God's restoration providence.

God has been guiding fallen humanity in various ways. Depending on the differences in nations, the differences in thoughts, and the differences in traditions, Heaven is adjusting things in various ways behind the scenes of history. And as God works to achieve the one determined purpose, we must understand that He is fighting alongside us to eliminate evil until the moment the curtain falls on that game.

Then, if we acknowledge that we are in the position of such runners, we will face the question of what we should do. If we know that we are the result of Heaven's hard work and that we must run in this racecourse, what kind of training will Heaven give us to make us run in this racecourse, and what trials and paths will I go through to reach that destination? This is an important question that everyone must resolve.

Among the prophets and sages who have come and gone in the past, there may have been those who took on a part of the race program and established some standards. In other words, these prophets and sages did not go through the entire game until the final curtain falls; they took on and concluded certain parts and are still moving forward.

Since God has created such a racecourse of restoration, we must recognize that we are those who are risking our lives and running through the course of life, and that we are those who must run and cannot help but run.

Today, looking at this earth, there are many thoughts of the Lord, and in the religious world, there are many denominations and sects. Depending on the differences in nations, there are various thoughts or religions that have emerged for those nations. Such thoughts or religions should have been those that encompassed the entire content of God's providential program, but they have not been able to do so. They have been thoughts or religions corresponding to a particular nation or a particular era. We must understand that these are merely parts of the mission that were responsible for certain sections in God's racecourse.

The forms of the race and the rewards given
When we go to the racecourse, there are 100-meter races, 200-meter races, or even 5,000-meter and 10,000-meter races, and ultimately, there are marathon races. Then, you are bodies that have entered the racecourse of God's restoration providence. What kind of game will you be responsible for and perform to stand before the universe? This is the question. 

Even if there are differences in individual value or personality, Heaven is surely looking forward to establishing the standard it desires by having each person take responsibility in a designated field of that race. You are bodies that have entered such a racecourse, so you must run with all your life. During your life journey, you need to know what kind of game you will participate in and what you will become to stand before Heaven.

God has been guiding His providence for 6,000 years, but when viewed as a whole, all of God's games have not yet been completed. They are still ongoing. You must run today and run tomorrow. When this game is over, God will give rewards to all of humanity, and furthermore, to the countless people who have come and gone in the past, and to the many who will come until the end of the game, according to the fields of this game. What day is the day of giving rewards? Borrowing the terminology of Christianity, it is the day of judgment. The day of judgment is the day of giving rewards. If we borrow the terminology of the current era, it can be called the end day.

Now, turning to yourselves, the question is whether you have established a victorious standard that can receive a prize in one of the events. This is a matter for you to reflect upon. There are various ways to run. Even if you are supposed to run on the normal course in the racecourse, there are many who run according to their own whims outside the racecourse, and there are those who enter the racecourse and run on the normal course but collapse in the middle due to insufficient ability, and there are those who run to the end but do not receive a reward. The number of those who receive rewards is limited. We must understand this.

God has been guiding His providence for 6,000 years, but He is still in a position where He cannot personally give rewards to the competitors. Therefore, God is appearing before all humanity, and both the spirits of the spiritual world and we on earth are hoping for that day when He can give rewards to the countless competitors who have run until now according to their events. That day is the end day. You must understand this.

The posture that runners must have
This is how we must run. Then, how should we go about it? It requires preparation as those who are stepping into the racecourse—preparation. What kind of preparation? Both internal and external preparation are necessary. Internally, there must be a conviction that I am running toward a certain goal. If there are obstacles on that course, I must have the conviction to deal with those obstacles, and based on that conviction, I need the internal preparation to run toward the correct goal.

In other words, through the training of body and mind, I must have the conviction that I will not collapse before reaching the final destination and that I will not lose to anyone, and that I will need the conviction to stand as the final victor. Also, even if my body encounters obstacles while running toward the final destination, I must have the conviction that I can push through and continue running.

However, today, there are countless people living on this earth, but how many of them are truly prepared to stand in the position of runners in the racecourse and run toward some destination? If you cannot deny that you are indeed caught up in the movements of history, are you in a state where you are prepared to run as a runner toward that destination under such desires? Up until now, you have not been.

Human beings are destined to belong to some field. Those who do not have a position or situation they can stay in are pitiful. Those who do not have a view that they are running toward some course for some purpose are pitiful. Most of us are like that.

Then, what is needed here is a time of internal and external preparation, where I resolve to train my heart and body under such a goal and decide that I must fight and win against numerous enemies. If there are those among us who have not had such a time of preparation, they must examine themselves.

So, what kind of internal preparation should we make? It should not be preparation for oneself. Right? Let’s say there is a marathon runner representing a nation. When he runs, if he runs to win the final victory and carry that glory for himself, he may not have the capacity to overcome any difficulties. However, if he runs with the conviction that behind him is the nation that gave him birth and that he must uphold the dignity of his country before the world, he will have the capacity to overcome any difficulties.

However, if he runs only for his own glory and his own goals, when he encounters pain, he will easily give up. 

In our belief, it should not be a self-centered belief. We must have a belief centered on the nation, on the world, and even further, on Heaven and Earth. If we run with the conviction that the victory or defeat of all creation in this universe depends on us, then even if we fall, we will have the capacity to rise again and continue running. If we focus on ourselves, when we encounter difficulties beyond what we have sustained until now, we will collapse. When difficulties greater than what we have hoped for arise, we will break.

Therefore, we need the conviction that we are running under a mission-oriented goal that trains our body and mind toward Heaven and Earth. Thus, human beings live, albeit vaguely, for God and for goodness. Goodness transcends limited environments. Goodness is not limited. Goodness is the existence that goes beyond restricted boundaries. For this reason, human beings live under such standards, albeit vaguely.

To become victors in the racecourse
However, today we must not be vague. We must have the conviction that we must definitely place in a certain rank in some event. The path on which our thoughts can move, the path on which our lives can move, is not just the path of our individual selves. It is an official and common path that spans across the ages or history. We must long to be the heavenly people who can fight and win on such a path.
If it is not centered around oneself, then on the day that purpose is fulfilled, heaven and earth will rejoice together because of me. When a runner representing the nation wins, the entire nation wins. Even if the event is small, the glory of that value extends to the whole. Therefore, it is necessary for you to have a day where you can cultivate your own value-based beliefs under a valuable standard in order to achieve that valuable goal. However, until today, you have neither felt nor thought about such things.

Those who enter the arena should be as simple and straightforward as possible. Your body must be ready to move at any time according to the direction of your heart. Hence, training is necessary.

However, the racecourse is not set up for you to run freely towards your goals. There are numerous obstacles placed on this racing ground. Our path is littered with the places where our ancestors stumbled and fell over obstacles. Therefore, it is essential to keep things as simple as possible so that when your heart moves, your body can follow suit. You must train your body to be able to do this.

Training cannot be done in a comfortable place. Training occurs in a place where you are challenged. To repeatedly undergo this inner preparation, you need a body that can break through and overcome even if you are internally challenged. Your inner determination must not waver, and even if trials come crashing down upon your body, you must not be defeated.

That is why it is said that those who walk the path of virtue should abandon everything and follow me. When Jesus called Peter, who was mending his nets, he told him to leave everything and follow him. There is a reason for retreating into the mountains to seek the path of virtue. There is a reason for everything. Therefore, under your inner resolve, you must have an external resolve that is prepared with conditions for clearing away obstacles, and you must have the confidence to move forward regardless of what you encounter, even if you fall to the very bottom, you must be able to support your body and mind. Without this, you cannot run or step onto the racing ground. We are all runners who must choose a single event to run in this racing ground, and we must train with an unchanging belief to achieve our goals. That is why you must have the attitude of a believer, the attitude of a runner, and the attitude of one who walks the path of virtue. You must have a heart that burns with the resolve to conquer that goal day and night.

Among those who have come here today, there may be some who vaguely think that believing in Jesus will lead them to heaven. What is heaven like? It is composed of groups that have passed through various events. You should not think vaguely that you believe in Jesus and will go to heaven. The path of virtue is like this. Since the beginning of history, any person who has walked the path of virtue, even if they have stood before God with the honor of that path, God has not said, "You are the final victor," and has not given them a reward. From the ancestors of humanity to the end times of humanity, it operates under a consistent program with a consistent goal.

In this regard, if you want to feel that you have become a runner who is running a life path and wish to become a victor, you must seek a religion that has historical significance. There have been many religions in the past, but their lifespan has only lasted a few centuries. Considering this, God has been working in ways that humans do not know. It must be a religion that contributes historically, one that has ties to the origins of human history. It must be a religion that discusses the origins of good and evil and encompasses all historical aspects of the human journey, one that can determine victory or defeat at the final destination of life. From this perspective, Christianity presents a problem today.

Furthermore, they must be someone who has the criteria to be acknowledged by future humanity as well. Isn’t that so? That is why we believe in God. We are running the path of life. We are running towards the ultimate destination of the last day.

Then who is the God we believe in? He is a historical God. Furthermore, He is a God of the times and a God of the future. The goals established by that God are also historical goals, goals relevant to the times, and future goals.

If the God we believe in is like this, then the standards of hope that humanity desires must also be like this. Therefore, we must know and believe that God is a historical God, a God of the times, and a God of the future. Only then will God give rewards not with sorrow but with joy. The final moment must come when we can understand the heart of the one who gives the reward.

Young people, you must understand clearly. Just having a sense of the times is absolutely not enough. A runner who can enjoy and win together with God

Next, in running towards that goal, you must not lose the heart of fighting. You must have the heart that, having made all preparations and possessing knowledge, you will win against any enemy. You must not lose in the fight.

The practical field is a fight. You must become a courageous person who can say that you will not yield even if you face any challenge on this earth, even if God, who gives the reward, strikes you. That is how I see it.

The path of virtue is filled with many trials. Running on this racing ground is not only difficult for myself, but there are countless unexpected trials. As a warrior in this fight, I am running, but there is also a battle of the heart and a battle of the body. It cannot be done merely with determination. The struggles I faced collide with my very being. This is why such internal and external hardships manifest in me today. I am not merely running; I must engage in both internal and external battles while simultaneously overcoming the tests from Heaven. To achieve victory in the journey of life, I must win in those battles. It is absolutely necessary.

Why is that? Although 6,000 years of history have passed, no one has yet reached the finish line on this course. I have gone, but no one has made it to the finish line.

**Humans Standing on God's Racecourse**
The Reason Jesus Will Return  
Everyone believes that Jesus is currently in heaven, but He is in paradise. Jesus said He would go to paradise. Paradise is the waiting room for entering heaven. The reason Jesus will return is to push open the door of paradise and open the door to heaven. Since He could not complete all His tasks on this earth, He must run again to reach the final finish line.

Therefore, the event we are running in today is the ultimate course of faith. If we were to compare it to a game, it would likely resemble a marathon. Among the events, the most brilliant and the one that can claim the throne of the games is religion.

So how should we run in this event? We cannot run solely with our own determination. We must recognize that various struggles are intensifying here. There are battles of the heart and body, and battles against enemies. Thus, while we place our bodies on the line, the world is pulling us. Isn’t that so? While living a true life of faith, the world pulls on our bodies, and the ideology of the Lord pulls on our hearts.

What is the goal? It is vague. On this path, countless enemies are shooting arrows from unseen places. Not only that, but even the Jesus we believed in and God Himself will ultimately ask, "Who are you?" and claim not to know us. Such events will undoubtedly occur.

Then, what kind of resolution should we make as warriors in our battles? When we firmly decide that the goal of the path we are running is certain, we must resolve to go even at the cost of our lives. Only then can we win on that course. We must resolve to fail at the highest level, to die the most miserable death in this world, and to suffer the most in our struggles. We must be prepared to suffer one more than God has suffered.

Everyone, let us look at our current reality as we run. Especially we, the members of the Unification Church, have come out with specific goals and are currently running. The life of running is a struggle, and in a struggle, we pull our bodies along.

To become sons and daughters whom God can boast about, the faith concepts we have believed in until now are pulling us. Here, enemies also intrude. Once that is over, ultimately, God will intrude. He will ask, "Are you my son or daughter? Are you confident?" and will question us. Won’t He? "What did you win over?" "Yes, I won over these things." "Really?" At this point, we must show results. Even the masters of the world test their disciples in various ways before entrusting them with something.

Even if heaven and earth mobilize to oppose us, if there is one who has won there, he will become a son or daughter whom God can boast about forever.
