**Prayer**  
Our ancestors have run. Adam also fell while running in one area of God’s race. Noah, who should have been treated with reverence, was treated carelessly by Ham, which caused Noah to fall while running. Abraham, in his journey toward Heaven, should have respected everything as belonging to Heaven and established their relative values, but he could not do so and was broken.

When we look at the path of Moses, the Israelite nation also fell, and Moses fell as well. Moses, who should not have become angry before Heaven, and the Israelite nation, who should not have despaired before Heaven, all fell in the wilderness because Moses first became angry and struck the rock twice, and the Israelites stood in the position of not believing in God.

When we look at the time of Jesus, what about the three disciples who betrayed Him? It was a path they should have walked with their lives, yet they were unwilling to go, and their pitiful appearances, filled with fear of death, became a tower of sorrow for humanity.

Today, we have learned through the Principle of Restoration that the path taken by the prophets of the past is the path we must walk. From the family of Adam, through every historical hurdle, all of it has led to the point where Jesus said, "Father, not my will, but Yours be done." It was only in the time of Jesus that He finally had the appearance of a victor, risking life and death. Now, if we do not have such an appearance, we cannot claim to be capable of fighting as runners in this arena.

Father, we have understood what the content of restoration is, and we know what our resolution to restore must be, and we know how fierce the battle is. Now, please protect us from becoming losers in this racecourse. We, who have sworn before Heaven and Earth, no matter what death comes, no matter what difficulties and pains may sweep over us, even if the entire humanity opposes us like a storm all at once, even if Heaven and Earth change, we will maintain our center and will not change our firm conviction. We will remove all difficulties and break through the dark clouds to become victorious sons and daughters who can look forward to the joy of Heaven in the bright world. We earnestly hope and wish for this.

Father, please have compassion on us who are gathered here today. Even though we stand in this one arena of running, there are those who run and those who have not yet run. Please guide us not to avoid this fateful course we must run. Let us gladly accept the tribulations and trials that come our way and digest them into our own, establishing conditions of pride and glory before You, Father, and let us be set up as noble figures who can take that as a sacrificial condition, we earnestly hope and wish for this.

We have come to understand that the hidden legacy in the heart of the Father, who has wanted to give rewards for 6,000 years, is the legacy of the Father’s heart. This is why He said, "I am the bridegroom, and you are the brides," and "I am your true Father, and you are my true sons and daughters." It was the Father who spoke of the true family, true nation, and true world. However, today we have no families, no nations, and no countries. We are poor beings who have not fulfilled any of these. Before the parents who seek to restore all of this, before the heavenly family, before the heavenly nation, what is there to be ashamed of? What is there to hesitate about? With the determination of a single-minded heart, let us run and run to occupy Satan’s territory and raise the flag of Heaven’s victory.

Father, please relieve the sorrow. We must be able to do this. To do so, we must endure any suffering that may come and win in the battle.
will come. 

We have come to realize that we must become those who do not fall behind in the race of life. Please protect us so that we do not become the ones who lag behind. May we not lose the spirit that our Father desires and has established for us, and may we not be those who disturb His heart. 

Allow us to be the sons and daughters of Heaven who can run boldly and vigorously with our lives today and tomorrow, and grant us the permission to not become the sons and daughters who fall behind on this course. We earnestly ask that we may become precious sons and daughters who can be the final victors in God's racecourse, boasting of our Father's glory before all creation and the entire world. We pray all these things in the name of the Lord. Amen. 

6) 
What belongs to the Father is mine 
John 14:11 1 Corinthians 13:1-13 
<Prayer> We do not wish to believe in a Father of words, but we want to believe in the Father who has established a historical connection with us. We seek a Father who can have a direct relationship with us today, a Father who can give us words directly. 

Today, humanity believes in God as an objective existence, but we do not seek God as an object of faith. We desire that God exists as a living and empirical subject, who can encompass all the realities of our circumstances and lives, who cannot be divided, and who can coexist with us through time. As long as such a relationship is established on this earth, it is a time that humanity desires and a time that God desires. 

Today, we thought that the garden of desires that our Father wishes for would be an ideal garden in a conceptual sense, but that is not the reality. We have come to realize that it is time for us to have a concept of heaven that can penetrate from our hearts, be felt through practice, be experienced through our own reality, and be sung through our emotions. 

We understand that the purpose of the providence of salvation, the purpose of the restoration history, and the purpose of the cross of salvation was to establish such a relationship and connection. Therefore, we earnestly ask that today we may be able to truly call ourselves children of the Father and recognize ourselves in a position where we can sing, rejoice, and listen to the words without feeling ashamed. 

We have learned much about the historical Father and have known the Father who is in the words, but now we seek that Father whom we can testify to from our hearts, whom we can experience with our bodies, and whose words can be made our own through our mouths. We ask that this time may be one where the Father causes empirical feelings to arise, and we earnestly desire this. 

Father, please work to help your sons and daughters gathered here to organize their hearts and bodies. The master of the heart is not oneself, and the master of the body is not oneself. We are those who, without knowing what it is, look far away, believe, hope, and seek to rely on some absolute being, but we are in a position where we cannot be recognized by the objective absolute being. 

We know that we are insufficient to receive the grace of the absolute from the position of objective value, so we ask that You, as the absolute being and subject, place us in a relative position. Please allow us to exchange Your ideals, which are absolute, with our ideals, which are relative, and lead our hearts to be intoxicated by those ideals so that we may sing of the whole love of the Father. 

We ask that this time may allow for the work to occur where our hearts move, our hearts communicate, our hearts experience, and our bodies bow down and can be transformed. 

Now, we wish to convey the words, so please be with us. We do not seek the words of man. We have heard much of what humans say today and have already heard many words from the countless clergy who shout from the podium. However, we do not desire this. We seek new words that can awaken the dead life, stir the dead heart, and cleanse the muddied heart, and we desire the words of re-creation that can allow us to know that our Father is our heart, our will, our ideals, and our subject, and that we are eternally one with the Father. 

We earnestly wish for this time to be one where You can pour down the direct grace of the gentle rain. We understand that the gap between the heart of the one who conveys and the heart of the one who listens is the work of Satan, so let us avoid the position of standing on our own and stand in the position of being supported by the Father, entrusting everything to Him and becoming those who rely on, hope for, and expect from Him. We hope that this time may be a precious moment to receive the Father’s mercy, and we pray all these things in the name of the Lord. Amen. 

<Words> The title I wish to speak to you about today is "What belongs to the Father is mine." If we expand the scope, what belongs to God is ours. I will speak briefly on this title. 

Humans must live in a relationship with the absolute being. 

Until now, we have believed that our value is infinite. We are in a position where we only know ourselves as beings of value without knowing the content of that value. However, we feel that we are not in a position to proudly boast before the historical and cosmic great existence that can fully establish our complete value. 

Because we are in such a position, we cannot deny that we are longing for the existence of value, the appearance of value, the relationship of value, and the world of value. We are those who must seek such places. Acknowledging this, when we look at all things and the great universe, we cannot help but feel emptiness. 

Thus, we are in a destiny where we must pursue something we can rely on, and we are constantly experiencing this through our conscience and the workings of our conscience. From this perspective, even if there is no God, we must establish a hypothetical absolute being. 

We, who are in such a position, must consider whether the actions we are feeling, enjoying, and singing about are truly connected to value. You can conclude that they are not, even if I do not say so. 

Because we are in such a situation, if there is a heaven, we must have a responsibility to establish some connection here. If heaven is the subject of absolute value and the essence of value, we cannot deny from a logical standpoint that if heaven does not work to establish the connections of that value, then words like love and others cannot apply to God. 

We know that humanity has fallen. We know that we have lost our original position. Therefore, we are beings who have lost our original value. In light of this, we must look at the whole world and, if there is a heaven, we must cry out, "Heaven!" and if there is an absolute being, we must cry out, "Absolute Being!" and if there is something that has the form of goodness, we must seek for it to manifest in a substantial way, and we must earnestly long for such an absolute being, heaven, or good existence. 

Because heaven knows that humans are in such a relationship and position, it has come to us, not minding the labor, effort, and self-sacrifice, and if we affirm that heaven is searching for the value above all values to hold humanity, we must approach it with a humble heart and bow before it with both hands together. 

When we consider the movements of the whole and the movements of history, and when we feel the deep flow of our hearts, we may not know ourselves, but behind the history and the deep flow of our hearts, something is leading and urging us. We must recognize that deep within our hearts, there is something that causes us to pursue value. We should not dismiss this as accidental or natural. This is because there is an unbreakable connection established between us. 

When you unravel that connection and discuss that value, you will find that the utmost goodness of God is intertwined with it. This is a relationship that cannot be established without establishing it. 

Humans must become the princes of faith, hope, and love. 

In this way, heaven has been working hard behind the scenes, suffering its own pain to bestow absolute value upon humanity until today, and it must continue this effort in the future. When we come to understand this, we cannot help but bow our heads with a reverent heart at the mere thought of heaven. 

For this reason, God has proclaimed words to humanity that they do not know the content or the intention of. While there is an intention to establish a deep connection through religion, before us, who must establish that connection, we have been told vaguely to believe in Him. The content proclaimed has been vague. We have been told to look to Him. Furthermore, we have been told to love Him. 

Although we do not know what kind of connection or content this is, we cannot deny that there is something related to the world of emotional connections that cannot be severed. 

Humans have come out believing, hoping, and loving based on such vague words. Many believers have fallen in the position of believing, fallen in the position of hoping, and fallen in the position of loving. Many have fallen in the journey of faith. There are far more who have died believing in heaven than there are loyal patriots of any one nation. Many have died hoping, and many have died loving. Yet among them, there is not a single person who has been praised as the prince of faith, the prince of hope, or the prince of love. 

If that is the case, we must blame God. If that is the case, there should be no words like believing, hoping, or loving. 

When we look back at the providence of 6,000 years, there are those who have fallen while hoping to be victors of faith, but there has not been a single person who has been honored as the great king of faith before humanity, and many have wandered in search of a foundation of hope, but there has not been a single person who has been praised by heaven or humanity standing on that foundation of hope, and many have spoken of love, but the same applies to them. 

However, Jesus was the reality of faith that God had been searching for over 4,000 years, and He was the one who felt the heart of the Father. The nation did not know that He was such a being. The nation did not know. No one among the world’s humanity knew. If anyone knew, it was only God. 

Who is Jesus? 

Therefore, Jesus had no place to go. He came to create the history of faith, but since there was no one to acknowledge Him, He turned His back on the world and sought out the one who would acknowledge Him, and that path was the way of the cross. Thus, He became the substantial subject of faith that inherited God's faith and the subject of hope that inherited God's hope, becoming the substantial representation of the intangible God. 

Because He appeared on earth as the subject of absolute faith, not as the subject of relative faith, you must believe in Jesus even if you do not believe in God. 

The Bible tells us to believe in Jesus, hope in Jesus, and love Jesus. Why? Because the substantial is closer to the substantial being. For this reason, humanity must bow their heads and cry out a million times in gratitude for the efforts of God who has established Jesus as the substantial form of hope. We must understand this. 

However, the ideals of Jesus, who sought to establish the foundation of faith, pioneer the environment of hope, and build the fence of love, have not been realized on this earth. 

The history of 4,000 years has been a history to establish the reality of faith, and the 2,000 years after Jesus and the Holy Spirit have been a history to establish the reality of hope. The standards of the Lord or ideological standards are also based on this. However, the worldview that Jesus hoped for and the opposing worldview have manifested today as democracy and communism. Because hope has reached its end, this time is called the end. It is not merely said to be the end blindly. 

What kind of ancestor is Jesus? He is the ancestor of hope rather than the ancestor of faith. He is the ancestor who can hope as a reality among hopes. If there is hope for humanity, what will you hope for? We have understood that the heart is precious within the body. We have understood that the heart is precious within the heart. If there is hope, there is no greater hope than the one who becomes the substantial object of the heart and the substantial object of the heart, so Jesus said to humanity, "You are the bride, and I am the bridegroom." Understand this clearly. Therefore, the world cannot go beyond the limits of that which it hopes for, no matter how far it goes. 

Then what kind of hope is it? Today, Christianity is longing for the world of word-based hope. However, now is the time to look beyond the words and long for the substantial. More than a million nouns of faith, more than the great works of faith, we need one substantial being. If that one substantial being does not appear, the worldview of word-based hope will be blocked. As long as we cannot connect to the substantial, that world will flow away with history. Just wait and see. 

The purpose of faith, hope, and love 

Today, Christianity has become a truly global religion, and the world line of the democratic camp, which moves around democracy, is also influenced by the ideals of Christianity, but now that end is approaching. What is needed here? It is not the purpose to enjoy only the words. We must be able to enjoy life as a substantial being. 

History is spinning like a whirlwind. We, gathered under the swirling trends of today, admire the figures of our ancestors of faith, Abraham, and the prophets of the past. We look back at the fierce history of struggle while gazing at Jesus, the prince of hope for the past 2,000 years. 

However, what they sought to achieve was a hope based on the promise centered around the words, not a hope that could manifest as a substantial life. Therefore, the day they hoped for, when hope would be realized in substance, is the end, and what seeks to realize that is the Lord of the Second Advent. 

So what remains now? The era that was centered on faith has ended because of Jesus. Because Jesus is the reality of faith, if you believe in Him, you can possess a value greater than anyone who has believed for 4,000 years before Him. Jesus had to establish faith before a people without faith and establish hope before a people without hope. Wasn't that the case? 

Look at this Bible. Look at the prophecies after Abraham. The hope based on faith was to hold onto the Messiah. However, within the symbolic promise, we have come to have the hope of being the bride and bridegroom, which is because Jesus suffered death on the cross. You do not know this, yet you believe it. Even if you do not understand those words now, there will come a time when you will understand them later.
It will be. If it is a substantial work of God, shouldn't it be so? That is how it makes sense. 

Then, what is it that the One who is the substance of hope and the substance of faith is trying to accomplish? In other words, where is the purpose of hope and faith? It is for human beings to find themselves and sing of love. There is nothing else. What does it mean to seek to meet the Lord? It is to be recognized for my worth through the Lord and to live in the embrace of His love. This is the greatest purpose of humanity. 

The purpose for which God established faith, the purpose for which God established hope, the purpose for which God established love, is not for Jesus alone, nor for Abraham alone, nor for any of our ancestors, but for today’s me. Then who is the One who has believed in me and sought me for 6,000 years? It is God. Who is He? He is my Father. Therein lies the twist that turns heaven and earth upside down.

Through the love of Jesus and the Holy Spirit, regeneration

Therefore, when you hold onto the Father you have believed in, the Father you have hoped for, the Father you have loved, you can say that Jesus has struggled to meet you until now and has labored for you. God should be able to say the same. In such a place, when you say, "O God! Let us live together. O Jesus! Let us live together," the place where you can hear, "Yes, let us live together forever," is heaven. A delusional heaven, a fabricated heaven is not needed by humanity. We must fight to establish this substantial heaven.

The Father’s is mine

When Jesus came and left, He said, "I have not completed everything, so believe in the Holy Spirit instead." Do you think you can be saved just by believing in Jesus? Absolutely not. You can be saved by believing in the Holy Spirit as well. The Holy Spirit is the one who leads you to believe in the Son of God, so you must believe in the Holy Spirit too. 

What kind of spirit is the Holy Spirit? It is the Mother Spirit. Today, Christians do not know this. If you think my words are a lie, ask God. I do not speak with the thought that it might be so. It is true. 

The Holy Spirit is the Mother Spirit, and Jesus is the true Father of humanity. The true Father is the completed Adam. Since Adam fell and could not become the ancestor of humanity, we are all descendants of false ancestors, not true ancestors. The One who came as the true ancestor is the Messiah. He is the true Father. However, Christianity talks about the Trinity and other things. Since Jesus is the true Father and the Holy Spirit is the Mother, one must receive the love of this Father and Mother to be regenerated. Can a child be born without the love of their parents? 

That is why in Revelation, it says, "The Spirit and the Bride say, 'Come.'" Those who hear should come, and those who are thirsty should come, and whoever desires should take the water of life freely (Rev 22:17). That day is the day when the Holy Spirit uses substance. That time is the time of the Second Advent. It is the day when the Bride completes her adornment. What is the wedding feast of the Lamb? It is the day when the lost true parents are welcomed back. When that happens, the God who was needed as a noun, the God who was needed as a target of faith will pass away. There is no need for a God who is believed in only by name or a faith life that is only outwardly practiced. What is needed is the substantial God. 

Then, who was the subject of the substance of faith? It was Jesus. Who was the subject of the substance of hope? It was Jesus. Who was the subject of the substance of love? It was Jesus. Although such a Jesus was sent, humanity could not recognize Him and, due to disbelief, He had to go. Then when will He come again? Since no one knew that the Bridegroom had come, He cannot come again. He cannot come because if He comes, He will be treated poorly again. You must understand that there is such a grievance. 

When the Lord comes, He will surely come to find me. 

Such thoughts among believers ruin Christianity and undermine God's will. 

God will come. However, unless the substance of faith, the substance of hope, and the substance of love appear in this world, the purposes of establishing faith, the purpose of establishing hope, and the purpose of establishing love will undoubtedly remain unresolved. Therefore, you must understand that without me, God cannot fulfill His role as God. Without me, God cannot move this world. Jesus lived with such conviction. He knew that without Himself, He could not introduce God's love. 

The faith and responsibility of the saints in the last days

Now is the time of testimony. It is said to be a scientific age. Science is logical. Being logical means that cause and effect must systematically correspond. When logical facts can be substantiated and executed in practical life, it can be called scientific. Humans are originally made that way. There can be no happiness that departs from a practical and empirical standpoint. There can be no talk of nations or anything else apart from that. That is why God also wants to reason with substance. 

Then what time is the end? It is the time when the 4,000 years of history to establish faith and the 2,000 years of history to establish hope come to an end, and the Prince of Faith, the Prince of Hope, and the Prince of Love appear. They do not come floating on clouds; that is not the case. If that were true, on a sunny day with a clear sky, there would be no clouds, so the Lord could not come, right? 

I have experienced such a faith life as well. Out of frustration and despair, I have protested to heaven dozens of times while striking the ground. Ultimately, when I broke through, I realized that it was not like that. So, as I spoke the truth, I became the representative of those who are scorned. I carry the label of a heretic. In the past, Paul was also the leader of heretics, and the Messiah who brought the truth was mocked as a leader possessed by Beelzebub. That was a historical sorrow. Since history began with sorrow, it must end with sorrow.

There may be believers who have believed well, so value those who kneel and pray on the church floor. Follow those who, while shedding tears, look back at the flock being driven away by the ministers. You will feel that a new flower garden is close by. Who would have known that after a moment of cold winds, spring would come? The body may be in adversity, but the heart is like a brave bride ready to welcome spring; I believe the Lord will seek such a person. 

There are many princes of the word who speak eloquently before all, but there are no protagonists of substance. There are no ministers who are the substance of faith. There are no ministers who are the substance of hope. There are no ministers who are the substance of love. So, where will this denomination, these believers go? Where should the saints of the last days go? 

In this land of Korea, even if I am labeled as a leader of heretics and a traitor to the nation, if this nation becomes blessed, I will go. 

The substance more important than the word

Since the factual, evidential altar has disappeared, where is the heavenly prince of faith who can establish a substantial altar? Such a person is needed now. It is not a multitude that is needed. It is not someone who commands many soldiers; it is a general who cannot sleep for the sake of thousands of soldiers that is needed. Heaven has been concerned about humans, worrying about their coldness, their heat, and their hunger until now. 

They were Pharisees who shouted to see me at the forefront, but Jesus turned around and wept. This was the appearance of Jesus. It is not those who stand at the forefront and shout who save humanity. It is because those who have struggled while holding onto heaven and crying out, "Have mercy on me. What about them?" that history has flowed in this way. Those who do not know this will know when the time comes to be struck. 

Therefore, no matter how good the words of the Unification Church may be, there will come a time when the substance will be more problematic than the content of the word. What do you have? What do you have? You must clearly understand that you need to be the very self that can be the essence of faith, the essence of hope, and the essence of love. If you have only that, even if the Lord comes a thousand years later, He cannot forsake me. 

Wherever there is faith, I am there, wherever there is hope, I am there, and wherever there is love, I am there; if you can be that self, there will be no problem. 

Now the time is approaching when history must be explained substantively. The day we hope for is the day we meet the substance. This is a fact. It is a fact. It is not a delusion or a fabricated statement. 

Is there anyone among you who is qualified to be the Bride of the Lord? Who has said so? Have you seen anyone who has become so? There are many who say they will, but no one has. Then what kind of content must we have? We must have the content of historical faith, the content of historical hope, and the content of the heart of God throughout history. This wretched world of sin is tiresome just to think about. The 6,000 years of history that has struggled to find substance is a tiresome history that has been betrayed countless times by humans. It is a history I do not want to see again even in my dreams, nor do I want to dream about it. However, we must hold onto this and think again, grieve, and fulfill what must be fulfilled as substance. That is the problem. 

So, in conclusion, what should you do? You must have a self that can say, "Faith is mine, hope is mine, love is mine," and you must become a person who can believe in yourself for a thousand years. 

Do you understand what I mean? 

I am the substance of faith, hope, and love. You must believe in God, who has governed for 6,000 years, more than anything else. 

Do you believe in your own body? Do you believe in your own heart? Do you believe in your own feelings? You must be able to believe. God has sought you for 6,000 years and has given you all He has as a gift to find you. I must reach such a position. 

We must liberate God, Jesus, and the Holy Spirit

The time has passed when people said they would go to heaven by believing in Jesus. Do not say, "I will believe in God and go to heaven," but rather say, "Please send God to heaven." Do not say, "I will go to heaven and meet Jesus," but rather create heaven on this earth and welcome Jesus. Do you think you can demand the love of Jesus while you are stained with sin? Jesus is the Prince of God. Jesus is the Prince of God. It is impossible. Believing like that is impossible. If you want to receive love, you must have a heart that truly wants to love with a heart that surpasses the heart with which Jesus died. However, all are like thieves. Today’s believers try to do things their own way, but it does not work that way. No matter how much you look into the spirit world, it does not work that way. It is fundamentally wrong. 

Therefore, we are now in a destiny to liberate God. Humanity has caused God to be bound. I have caused God to be bound. I have caused God to be accused by Satan because of me. Jesus died because of me. The Holy Spirit has been embroiled in a bloody struggle because of me. O God, give me strength. I will bring my Father to a place of rest and liberation. I will bring Jesus and the Holy Spirit to a place of liberation. 

God has sought those who are hungry for a faith that can do so, those who are hungry for hope, and those who are burning with love for 6,000 years. We must understand this fact. 

Is there any contradiction in these words? If you say that you love us, then God is my Father. In such a realm, even when looking at the mountains, tears obscure my vision. As those who cannot take responsibility, we must strike our chests when we look back at history, and even if we take steps with joy, we can only become princes of lamentation. 

You must understand. God is not someone who sits comfortably on the throne of heaven. God, who sees hell being created, suffers more pain than hell itself, which humanity does not know. If God does not suffer more pain than hell and allows hell to exist, He cannot be called a God of love. God has not experienced any part of the suffering of hell during the 6,000 years of history. There is nothing He has not suffered. In fact, God is suffering the pains of hell. Even if you say there is no such absurd statement, we must believe in and serve God from this perspective. Only then can He be the true God of humanity. God has endured all the pains of hell to find me. 

After Jesus died on the cross, He spent three days in the underworld; what is this? He had to be the Savior on earth and the spiritual Savior. He had to preach even in hell. Therefore, those who believe in Jesus had to break through the bottom of the hell on earth. Thus, in the course of history, He was trampled upon and pushed away. Since God walked such a path, we too must become companions and co-workers of such circumstances. To such people, the glory of heaven will be inherited. This is the providence of restoration and the providence of salvation. Understand this clearly. 

O God, please allow me to go to hell and experience the pain of my Father. Those who pray with such a heartfelt desire do not go to hell. O God, I dislike hell, so please send me only to heaven. Those who say this go to hell. They go to hell. Jesus prayed on the cross, "Abba, Father, not my will, but Yours be done. Do not hold their sins against them." This was because He felt that He could not avoid the path of the cross when He examined God's heart and inner feelings, who had endured the pains of hell for 4,000 years to save this nation and this people. You must clearly understand that Jesus felt such emotions. 

Those who can take on the ideals and spirit of Jesus

Christianity, which should lay this foundation of justice, is collapsing. We have risen to rebuild this foundation with our own hands. We must fight silently and march silently. That path is not the path of wealth or glory. If we desire such things, our hoped-for time will not come. There is no time to devote to that. We are those who have set out to go our own way, regardless of what the world does. 

Are there those who have come to the Unification Church or to hear the words without knowing what it is? Let me tell you firmly; the path of the Unification Church is difficult. You must pass through the wall of pain, hitting your head and colliding your body, and go through a place where blood and flesh are soaked. The path we take is not a smooth one. The Lord walked that way, and the saints always walked that way. Those who have taken on history were those who bore the spirit of history and stepped forward as warriors soaked in blood. Just as such people have led history, those who can take on the ideals and spirit of Jesus must also be such people. You must understand this clearly.
I want to speak to you. The age of blind faith has passed, and the foundation of absurd and fabricated logic is based on ignorance, and I want to assert that there is no completion in this foundation. Therefore, the issue we need to raise at this time is believing in myself.

Just as God believes in Jesus and Jesus believes in God, just as Jesus believes in the Holy Spirit and the Holy Spirit believes in Jesus, I must believe in myself. Thus, even if the principles of heaven and earth change, I cannot change. Even if heaven and earth perish, the words of Jesus cannot change. Even if heaven and earth perish, I do not change. I must go as far as I can.

However, there is a problem for each of you. Do you believe in yourselves? You who are frantically claiming you will go to heaven, do you believe in yourselves? Faith that exists only in words, without substance, is useless. A shell without substance, chaff is useless. That is why there is a biblical saying about the parable of the wheat and the chaff. If we become embodiments of faith, hope, and love with substance, then no matter how vast this world is, no matter how expansive America is and how advanced the country may be, it is not a problem. It is not a problem.

Forever I believe in myself, I take myself as hope, and I love myself while saying, "God, please receive my love. God, rejoice in my hope. God, rejoice in my faith." When I do this, I should be able to hear God say, "Yes." The purpose of establishing faith is that, the purpose of seeking hope is that, and the purpose of longing for love is that, and when that happens, we will meet the Lord there. Humans spanning two worlds
If each of us believes we are living centered on ourselves in this world, it is a great misunderstanding. We know through our lives that our hearts pursue the purpose of living and that we desire to live for some goal. In this light, we cannot deny that this "I" is connected to some other world of purpose. Therefore, we must clearly understand that I am not living for my own purpose, but rather I must be born and live for some other purpose. In this regard, when we look at "I," it is either extremely small or extremely large. We know that we have woven history with this interconnectedness.

The emotions that "I" feel, the worldview that "I" observe, and all the social life that "I" live have corresponding and opposing phenomena, which we cannot ignore. That is, there are conflicting and contradictory aspects in living for some purpose, while on the other hand, there are aspects that correspond and coexist. This is the phenomenon of society, the global trends of today, and the manifestation of some heavenly providence.

When we analyze heavenly principles and the heavenly worldview, we cannot deny that there is some other existence that goes beyond my concepts and specifically clarifies me, rather than just moving from my singular self.

From this perspective, we must clearly understand that the place where I stand and the place where I dwell is not limited to one world but spans two worlds. The world my heart desires and the world my body desires are both unfolding within me. Therefore, while my heart has desires for joy, happiness, and some ideals, my body, centered on the five senses, experiences some pleasures and sensations that are tangible. We cannot deny this fact.

The Fall of Humanity from the Perspective of Heavenly Heart and Human Heart
We often say that people have hearts. We say they have human hearts. Furthermore, we say they have heavenly hearts. Humans should be those who can illuminate their lives with the corresponding heavenly principles and the order of the heavenly heart and human heart. However, we do not have the order to clarify the living standard that can combine human heart and heavenly heart. This is the Fall and the lamentation.

Departing from the human heart, and also betraying Heaven or good conscience, we often refer to this as evil heart or material heart. When we look at just one person, centered on the heart, the heavenly heart enters me, and centered on the body, the evil heart seeps into me. We cannot deny that all the saints and sages throughout history have lamented over themselves in this situation. Paul also cried out, "Oh wretched man that I am!" because he was in the midst of the law of the heart and the law of the body.

Then what kind of world is this world that I have enjoyed and continue to enjoy? It is a world where my heart and body cannot joyfully coexist, and it is not a world where the ideals of my heart can harmonize. You cannot deny that you are in such an environment, struggling and suffering. When we reflect on this, we can conclude that although there is a principle that the heavenly heart should move the human heart, there has never been a moment in our lives where this heavenly heart has manifested joyfully in our lives.

If there is a Heaven, would we want to live just one day centered on our hearts? We would want to live forever centered on our hearts. However, we find ourselves in a situation where our hearts and bodies are in conflict. When we ask whether Heaven can live centered on such a heart, the answer is no.

Heaven is goodness. Goodness is eternal, unique, and unchanging. However, because we do not possess the unchanging, unique, and eternal worldview, we cannot continuously enter into the heart that moves toward goodness.

For this reason, Heaven can operate through our conscience, but it cannot operate through our worldview or life perspective. Because it could not draw humanity under the universal ideals, the history up to now has been under the dominion of evil. Therefore, we cannot conclude that this world is a world that can establish a relationship with heavenly principles and eternity. For this reason, this world must be judged. The humans living in this world must also be judged.

The development of providential history
Today, humanity has not tasted joy since the beginning. We have not sung of happiness centered on this land. Throughout the long history of 6,000 years, conscientious people have never had the opportunity to boast about Heaven and Earth. Has there ever been such a time?

Look. The world of the heart and the world of the mind

Shouldn't there be a world that the heart desires, a master and family, nation, and world where the heart can eternally rejoice? If that does not exist, why is your heart like that?

The movement of your heart toward goodness does not come from some creative power. Power does not act independently. It cannot act without a counterpart. Whether observing chemical phenomena or physical phenomena, it is all like that.

When you see the undeniable reality of the clear conscience, you are undoubtedly removing one aspect of sorrow and pursuing one aspect of joy. The time when you can rejoice is the time of humanity's hope and the time of humanity's happiness. Therefore, the issue must be resolved there.

Today, the so-called democracy and communism are competing against each other while trying to dominate the world, but this should not be the case. So where should the resolution take place? We must return to the state of Adam and Eve before the fall, when they rejoiced centered on God and enjoyed hearing God's voice. God must be my eternal master, the head of my family, the master of my nation, the master of my country, and the master of my world. If I can say that my God is the standard that cannot be exchanged for anything in this world, then the garden of happiness will come to this earth.

The person God has been seeking for 6,000 years
Our world of the heart can enjoy, harmonize, and move, but it cannot take. We can harmonize and respond to each other, but we cannot take. Original love is not human love; it is the eternal and unchanging love of God. The moment you come into contact with God's love and acknowledge God as your master, you become one with Him. When you enter into a joyful place where you can exchange joy with God, you can conquer the world. The scene where I can enjoy with God is one where I can take joy greater than possessing everything in the universe. If humanity has experienced such a thing, then the stimuli felt through all the senses of this body are not the issue.

So what history has Heaven been making centered on my heart? It has been the history of cosmic development. You have forgotten that Heaven has been presenting the history of cosmic exploration to lead you. Under what goal does Heaven command your heart? It is to become a cosmic being. You are to become a being that can embrace the universe and grow based on everything in the universe. Heaven is leading us to become such beings.

That is why it has been said to love, to love the wicked, to love the good, to love all things, and to love all of Heaven and Earth. Isn't that right? How refreshing is that? We humans have lost the essence of this fundamental ideology. Now, our hearts must be able to enjoy. While the heart enjoys, the cells must also enjoy, and while the heart takes, the cells must also take. Furthermore, the sensations of that taking must be able to react to the world I relate to. You must clearly understand that such a person, who can create such content and actions, is the person God has been seeking for 6,000 years.

If there is a heart, what kind of person is the one who draws that heart, and what kind of person is the one whom the world, nation, and entire universe desires? It is the person mentioned earlier. For such a person, even entering a position of being conquered is infinitely grateful. Everyone, isn't that enough? I am willing to sacrifice infinitely. If there are many such people, it will become the kingdom of Heaven on Earth. The sons and daughters of God are such people. They give and give, wanting to give infinitely, and even if they sacrifice infinitely, they want to sacrifice more. 

Isn't that the love of parents? The love of God is several tens or hundreds of times greater than that love. The world you are seeking and envisioning is the world that God has been seeking for 6,000 years.
It has not come yet. The emotional world and the hearts of humans on earth must meet on that one day of connection. Through that, the absolute standard of judgment will be established on earth, and that will be the end. Based on that heart, the judgment will take place. 

That is why Christianity is a religion of heart that transcends the religion of the mind. God is not the master of the heart but the master of the heart's emotions. No matter how many villains there are, they cannot block the love of God that comes through the heart. When that love surges, everyone likes it. Even Satan and demons like that love. This must be understood. While they like God's love, they stand in the darkness where they cannot receive that love. Humanity is destined to pioneer such a place with their hearts, but how will this be accomplished? 

Now your path has become clear. There will be connections that come to you through the heart. There will be connections that come through material means. There will be connections that come through people and connections that come through the Word. After that, there will be connections that come through the heart without you even realizing it. The heart longs for such places, avoiding this world. Those who hope, seek, and long for such connections to appear at some time and place must not forget that heaven will surely help them connect with history. 

To develop the heart, those who walk the path of the Way must move toward the heavenly heart, so they cannot treat even a single word that comes to them carelessly. They cannot ignore the scene where an enemy is trying to stab them with a sword. They must think that there is a connection and let it go. However, those who say, "Ah! This is..." should not be. What appears good in this wrong world is not heaven. It is heaven that comes with something bad in this wrong world. One must have the capacity to consider even such problems and be able to feel the value of connections to make the first step in developing the heart. 

Then, when dealing with those around you or hearing, seeing, and feeling everything, you will be able to know with your heart whether it is good or evil. When you hear certain words or meet certain connections, your heart is drawn again and again. Whether there is some truth or some church, or whatever religion, without even thinking, you are unconsciously drawn to them. Isn't that so? The heart is like the principles of the natural world. 

Just as the needle of a compass always points north-south, our hearts are the same. When a positive heart appears, the relative negative heart is always drawn there. If you have not felt the sensation of your body being drawn into the religion you believe in, you are not a true believer. If you have not felt your body being drawn into that Way, your heart being drawn in, and your emotions being drawn in, you cannot be said to believe in the Way. Such people will eventually come to not believe in that Way. 

What is the entire human race looking for today? They are looking for an ideology. How should ideology be explained? It must be explained by truth. What is truth? It is the Word. The truth that my heart can enjoy forever, the truth that my heart can eternally savor, feels new no matter how many times I hear it, a hundred times or a thousand times. Dear friends, the truest truth is like the taste of rice. Whether eaten yesterday or today, even after eating the same rice for 70 or 80 years, it is still delicious, and truth is the same. We must be grateful. You know through the Word that there are two worlds for people. 

Jesus said that man does not live by bread alone but by every word that comes from the mouth of God, and it must be a truth that takes the body and takes my heart. Isn't that what matters? 

That is why, dear friends, this is not the time to sit still. The time has come for direction to change. We must move toward one subject in one direction. If we look to the side and go down a side path, it will be obstructive, so we must cut it all off and go. Everything is being deemed heretical. 

Now is the time to find the standard to become the main character of the universe. Now is the time when the direction is being reversed. Heaven must become earth, and earth must become heaven. Humans must become the subject. It is a time of change. Since it is a time of change, I must also become a central being of heaven and earth, the main character of the universe. Heaven is not the main character of the universe. You know well that God's purpose in creating humans was to elevate them as the main characters of the universe, substituting for His authority. 

To reach that standard, you must now lay the foundation to resolve from your center and to experience from your heart. To find a way to resolve from your heart, you must seek one direction. Since the current religions and ideologies cannot be the complete standard of my heart, emotions, and ideology, the time has come for something new to become my center. Now is that time. You and I are in the same position. Just as Jesus said, He did not call us servants but friends, we are in the same position. The universe is not above. Otherwise, a complete resolution will not emerge. 

That is why you should not be still right now. But what will happen if you try to be still?

The young person speaking here also feels that and knows that the feeling is undoubtedly true, so even if heaven and earth oppose it and the heavens and earth turn upside down, I walk this path. Even if your body demands that you must go there for some reason, even if such conditions are met, you must deny all of that, abandon it all, and go there. If there is a word that transcends time and space and gives you a feeling of being led, you should pack everything up and follow it, like carrying a bundle on your back in the style of a wandering poet. Dear friends, what need is there for a label in the world of the heart? What need is there for a label in the world of emotions? Just by being there, one knows by oneself. Just by being there, one will act by oneself. That is the first standard that can resolve. 

Dear friends, what kind of life have you lived? What position are you in today? You must remember that you are struggling in two worlds. What you can enjoy here is not the direction led by the body but the direction led by the heart. 

When you look at the world today, the direction led by the body, the external conditions, are perfect. They are completely equipped. They are equipped with hundreds of points. Because they extend beyond individuals and families to the world, they are equipped with hundreds of points. However, the direction led by the heart is only a few percent. When you think of this, heaven wants to judge this world. What would the sorrow of such a heaven be? You must seek a path that can find joy while knowing that sorrow. 

That is why those who believed in the Way in the past endured even when their necks were severed. I do not wish for you to come to the Unification Church. Who is God? He is the eternal master of my body. He is the eternal master of my heart. In the original world, no matter how much a couple loves each other, if the husband loves God more than his wife, the wife does not resent her husband. It is as it is. Likewise, if the wife loves God more than her husband, she does not say, "Why do you love God more than me?" The world that can see that and rejoice is heaven. The God who is in a subjective position that transcends any love or any desire of the world is the eternal master of my body. Being in the embrace of God, who is the eternal master of my body, in that garden, even dying is good. If He is the eternal master of my heart, the eternal master of my emotions, what more could I wish for? 

Then, what kind of world do you envision with your heart? It is not a world that comes through external senses, through the five senses, or a world formed in the realm of recognition. It is the world of God's love, a static world. That world is a world where one can feel God's love even through a tiny speck of dust. You must understand that. You must not fail to understand. We must sing with our bodies. And we must sing with our hearts. We must praise with our emotions. What should we praise? The One who is my Master. Who is that? God. That God is my Father. 

We are the sons and daughters of that God. Therefore, we must ask, "What can we exchange for this One?" "What can sever the connection with this One?" 

Human love, human desires, and human wealth and honor are not issues. If all creation and all beings have made God, who wishes to be our eternal master, our Father, then what greater happiness could there be? Even if one becomes the wife of a certain person, they will complain and make a fuss. But God is my Father. This joy cannot be exchanged for anything in heaven or on earth. In such a realm, God, who has been searching for me through the path of six thousand years of suffering, how much effort He has made! Heaven is looking for sons and daughters who can comfort the Father. You must know this. 

You must know how to judge yourself. 

To create such sons, heaven has moved our ancestors countless times over the centuries. But how much have humans betrayed? We must recognize that we have betrayed the hearts of people and the hearts of heaven. Furthermore, we are those who have betrayed the heavenly principle and the heart of the Father. We must repent of this sin. 

What has violated the heavenly principle? This body has violated it; therefore, our bodies are sinful. The enemy is not something that appears before you. Your own body is the enemy. You must suppress this body. You must know how to judge yourself. That is why those who walk the path of the Way are contrarians. The teachings are also paradoxical. However, you must fight with yourselves at stake. When Jesus was carrying the cross, He saw women beating their breasts and weeping as they followed Him and said, "Daughters of Jerusalem, do not weep for me, but weep for yourselves and for your children" (Luke 23:28). 

Your own problems must be resolved. You are the problem. You must not blame anyone or resent anyone. You must blame yourself. You must clear away the illusory self and accept Jesus, the friend of your original heart, the friend of your original emotions, as your heart's Father, your emotional Father, and furthermore, as your bodily Father, the Father of the universe. will be achieved. To walk that path, there must be words that guide one's heart. Whether one possesses a truth that can move the heart or not, whether one has such a religion or not, determines whether it is true or false. This must be clearly understood.
