10)
Family members living in God's home
Matthew 12:46-50
<Prayer> Father, we have gathered from various places. We were born as descendants of many people. Therefore, there are various causes and grounds, and we cannot help but think that our current selves have been shaped by various circumstances.

Father, there may be good people here and those who are not so good. The shapes of human hearts and bodies are diverse and varied, but our hearts, which long for truth and the greatest good, and which know that You are God and yearn for our original Father, will not change.

At this time, may we deeply feel and experience that You are not seeking any external appearance but are looking for the heart that yearns for You, awakening the original self that is deeply embedded within us. If we cannot acknowledge and prove that, let us realize that it is meaningless to be present here today.

As we think of the Father who has worked hard to find the hopeful image He desires through the complicated struggles of historical paths and times, we cannot help but feel that today I am not alone.

When we were born on this earth, we were born centered around relationships from above, below, in front, and behind. We come to know that these relationships push us to pursue a perfect and complete value of one purpose or the value of the whole.

Please help us to understand that above is heaven, below is the history of goodness moving with heavenly principles, and in front is the world of hope, with our comrades, nations, and fellow countrymen on either side. May we be sons and daughters who can hold onto our original feelings and observe all of this while struggling to establish relationships in all directions.

If there are those who forget everything about themselves and are struggling to yearn for this, even if they walk a path that is not accepted in their times and is opposed in their lives, we know that in the end, they will surely be established before heaven. We have come to this place hoping for such a path, so Father, please command us now. Speak to us. As we long for and admire Your heart with our hearts, if there are any distressing matters, please let us feel them, and if there are any tragic and sorrowful matters, please let us experience them through our bodies. May we be sons and daughters of hope who can feel Your existence in the place where You are manifested through our bodies and bow our heads in gratitude before You, beloved Father, we earnestly hope and desire this.

Even if we are bound by the chains of evil and sin, let us be those who realize that heaven is looking upon us with compassion. The more we go on, the more we feel, and the more we know, we are the greatest of sinners among sinners, and we are the heaviest burden bearers among those who bear burdens. We know that we must gather here. We cannot help but feel the undeniable fact that we cannot enter the original nature without settling our own assertions and perceptions.

Father, Your sons and daughters gathered here have already come, so please do not let every step be in vain. Since we have met as relationships, let this meeting not be meaningless. May this relationship not be a human relationship but be connected as a relationship of nature, heart, and life, we earnestly hope and desire this, Father.

What can I say? I long for only Your heart to be revealed and wish to see Your form, and I desire to feel Your divine image. At this time, may we feel that you, I, and we are brothers, and may the family members who stand in place of the Father form one altar before You. Father, we earnestly hope and desire this.

At this time, please bless the denomination gathered here on behalf of the 30 million people, and bless the countless sons and daughters who are bowed before You on behalf of the 2.7 billion humanity.

Until now, our ancestors have fought against evil, but the battle is not yet over. Today, we know that we must bear this fight, so please allow us to be sons and daughters who can stand before humanity and nations, fully equipped with both internal and external armaments as warriors representing heaven.

We have seen the sorrow of Jesus in the scriptures we have read. Jesus was born in the family of Joseph and had parents, siblings, and relatives, but He walked a pitiful path without parents and siblings, without relatives and kin. Father! Please relate the sorrowful circumstances of Jesus to ourselves, and we earnestly ask that You reveal the heavenly contents that must be clarified at this time.

I wish to offer this body and heart as Yours and to dedicate the whole to You. Father, I earnestly hope and desire that You personally protect us, and I pray all these words in Your name. Amen.

<Words> We have parents, siblings, and spouses. No matter how unworthy a person may be, they have a family to stay with. Whether good or bad, there are family members and a home where one can reside.

The human heart longs for the ideal world. You must live and die with this family. You are currently going through the life journey of sharing joys and sorrows with your family centered around this home. You believe that this family is one that will be eternally connected to you, but at some point, that family and those members will also be severed from you. Although many people have gathered here, there is not a single person who can confidently say that they will carry such relationships into the eternal world. While you dream of hope or happiness centered around this family, will that hope and dream cease at the moment you die, or will they continue to connect you to another world of happiness and hope? It is a disheartening thought.

Humans have an original heart. This heart urges us to move toward the great purpose of goodness that humanity must aim for, even at this time. And we cannot deny that this has moved along with history. From this perspective, when we see the movement of this heart, we can understand that this heart has been waiting for a good person to appear. Therefore, that person will surely appear in the historical path.

When we see people saying in unison that the end is near, it is certain that the end is approaching. Is humanity happy today, or unhappy? I think it is more unhappy than happy. The time when this world of unhappiness ends is the end. So what does our heart long for? It longs for a world of happiness, or an ideal world that is hopeful, free, and equal. Deep within our hearts, we cannot deny that we have walked our lives longing for that world until today. Everything that is truly hoped for and truly desired must surely be realized. If it does not, we cannot believe in heaven or anything else.

Nothing in this world has made our hearts happy, and there is no one who has lived in a happy living environment that stimulates the body. My family, my parents whom I have relied on and looked up to until now, are the same. We must understand that this world cannot be the eternal cradle of happiness. Why has this happened? Borrowing religious terminology, it is because of the fall. This world, this race, this family, and these members that have come about through the fall cannot possibly align with the ideals of happiness that the original heart pursues. The conclusion is obvious.

For this reason, we hope for this era to pass. This is a frank statement. Every man and woman, everyone wishes for this era to pass. The false society will pass, false parents will pass, false siblings will pass, false couples will pass, and false children will pass. You must deeply feel this fact in your hearts at this time. Parents do not recognize their children, and parents among themselves, children among themselves, siblings among siblings, and all those who say they are good among friends or nations will be shattered to pieces. That will happen.

You see and hear in newspapers or magazines about children killing parents and parents killing children. As we see these facts, traditional ideologies are gradually disappearing day by day. Why is that? The destination that our hearts long for is a place where we can enjoy it with heavenly principles. Since heavenly principles are in the process of transforming humanity toward the destination, they go through a history that changes in myriad ways and ultimately leads to a static revolutionary era. The era of consciousness revolution will pass, and the era of justice revolution will come. It will push humans into an environment where they cannot even trust each other's feelings. Those who dream of happiness here will one day face sorrow, and those who seek a place of rest here will one day encounter sorrow. Such conclusions naturally arise.

God who wishes to welcome humanity as family
To you in the world of grievances, this time of resentment is passing. Your hearts are seeking something new beyond this. Turn back your steps, turn back your hearts, and reflect on what feelings you are longing for to connect with, and what is blocking your path. Religion is what connects you to a reliable standard, a standard you can focus your heart on. If such a connection is not made, it is as if God does not exist.

The heart urges us to escape from the painful environment of stimulating reality and move toward ideals. Any leader must fight against this reality. However, no one knows about this heart that aims for ideals and longs for them. We must act according to the command of that heart. Many prophets throughout history have not resisted that heart. The same will be true for any person in the future. We must respond to that heart; it will not happen because someone else does something. If we acknowledge and recognize that we are in a fate that cannot be resisted and must respond, we must clearly understand that the world you are living in today is not the ideal world, and that you cannot establish a relationship with the ideal world you dream of and hope for. Why? Because it has fallen.

Thus, we have come to need feelings, hopes, and relationships. As that era draws closer, the fear in your hearts is increasingly intensifying. Thinking about this, it is an unbelievable world, a world where you cannot sit comfortably. It is a world where you cannot even take a single step on the path. You have walked this path for decades. We cannot deny that there is a heavenly principle that injects something new into humanity, pushing them toward a new history. Based on conscientious phenomena, we cannot deny that there is a heaven and that there are heavenly principles. When God created this earth, there must have been some purpose and ideology. What was that purpose? It must be a good person. It must be a good person who aligns with God's heart. It must also be a free person. That person will be one who can enjoy life with God and live in the garden of freedom with God. However, even after thousands of years of historical paths, there has not yet been a person who has established a relationship as a family that can live with God, as a member of God's family.

Then what is God's purpose of creation? It is to establish an ideal family where God can live with humanity. Although humanity has fallen, in their hearts, they are longing for the day when God can be the father of that family or the father of humanity, and humans can live as members of that family. If we can acknowledge God as our eternal Father and if I can become a member of that family and live with God forever, then if we can live with God, who is the essence of hope, the essence of ideology, the essence of life, and the essence of happiness, then our desired purpose will be fulfilled.
The day we appear as family members and reveal the dignity and value of that family before the Father will be the day of resurrection and the day of the Second Coming as spoken of in Christianity.  
The goal of our faith  
Humanity has lost the True Parents due to the Fall. While there are fallen parents, we do not have our original parents. Therefore, no matter how good or virtuous one may be, even if one is a person of character who can boast before God, they are still a descendant of fallen parents. This means they cannot speak boldly. No matter what one possesses, if we look deeper, there is still anxiety and dissatisfaction flowing in their heart.  
So what is the groaning of humanity and the groaning of all creation? It is that human beings cannot participate as members of the heavenly family. This is the lament of heaven. The goal of our faith today is nothing other than to call out to God, "Father!" It is to welcome the day when all of humanity can rejoice as brothers and call God their Father, and you must understand that God has been working for 6,000 years to bring about this restoration.  
If this is God's purpose and the purpose in the hearts of humanity, then that purpose must surely be fulfilled. That day must come without fail. If that day does not come, we cannot establish a relationship with heaven as we live today. If we cannot establish a relationship, God cannot look at our hearts and claim them as His own. He cannot definitively say that we belong to heaven. The moment this relationship is established on earth, the grievances of heaven will be resolved on earth, and the cries of the earth will not be heard in heaven. Furthermore, at that moment, a family ideal world that can connect heaven and earth will be opened. It is because of this goal that our ancestors, albeit vaguely, held onto the words of heaven.  
Humans have lost the True Parents, the True Siblings, the True Couple, and the True Children due to the Fall. Therefore, for us who have embarked on the journey to find them, the words of the True Parents are necessary.  
What kind of responsibility must we take on in the process of restoration as fallen beings seeking the True Parents, and what kind of resolve and conviction must we carry? We must long for the words of our original parents with our hearts. Furthermore, we must yearn for the appearance of our original parents with whom we can enjoy life together with God. What do those parents look like? We must also think about what the heart of our original parents is like. We must contemplate what the love of our original parents is. Have you all thought about this?  
In order to live as a member of the heavenly family, what does heaven bring to us? It comes with the words based on faith. What is the desire of humanity? It is to listen to the words of the True Father with body and heart. It is to want our body and heart to act according to the words. It is not just action; it is also the desire to hold onto the Father and see what He is like. Furthermore, we want to know the ideals of that Father and understand His heart. We want to know what His love is like.  
Until today, many prophets and sages have conveyed new words throughout different times and centuries. They have said how the world should be and how the world we hope for in the future should be. History is unfolding through a revolutionary process of overturning. Because of the distance between God and fallen humanity, God cannot speak directly to humans. Thus, He has raised many prophets to mediate and connect God and humanity until now. In the Old Testament, He sent angels, in the New Testament, He sent His Son, and now history is flowing toward a direct era where we can call God our Father. How can this be achieved? It is through the words of the Father. For this, the words must be imbued with heart, and there must be a reality through those words.  
The Savior, the center of the heavenly family  
Fallen humanity must pass through a time of longing for the words. Heaven has come forth with history, centering on these words, urging the hearts of humans to want to live according to the words of the Father.  
What does it mean to live centered on the words? It means to live with the Son sent by heaven, who is the substantial being of the heavenly ideals. That Son is the True Father of humanity. The one who came with such a mission was Jesus.  
What kind of being was Jesus? He was a being who could become the True Father of humanity, lost due to the Fall. He came as the substantial reality of the words established on the practical foundation of long history, existing as a substitute for the Father. Therefore, Jesus said, "I am the way, the truth, and the life. No one comes to the Father except through me." (John 14:6) Only Jesus is the center of the way, the center of the heart, and the center of the spirit. Why? Because He embodies the content of the Father. Thus, Jesus is the Savior of all humanity and represents heaven and earth. Therefore, through those words, we can grasp the appearance of the Father, through those words, we can feel the heart of the Father, and through those words, we can touch the love of the Father, which is Christianity today.  
Jesus came to this earth. He came with infinite ideals. If He had a wish, it was a wish on behalf of God. What is God's wish? It is to fulfill the ideal of creation and the purpose of creation. When Jesus appeared with that wish in the position of an individual, the environment was not favorable. The environment that could not stand before the will rebelled against Jesus. Even if Jesus had to fall, He had to leave behind the determination He held in His heart on this earth. Thus, Jesus emphasized the relationship, "I am your Father, and you are my children." There must be a True Father and a True Mother. The one who came as a mother figure after Jesus' departure is the Holy Spirit.  
The sorrow of Jesus was that He could not have a day of blessing to bless sons and daughters as a substantial being who united spirit and flesh on this earth. It was His grief that He could not fulfill all the words He had to say and could not establish the standard of the heavenly family. Since He could not establish a heavenly family, He could not raise up the members of the heavenly family, and thus could not form a lineage centered on family, a nation centered on lineage, and a world centered on nation.  
Although the nation of Israel was chosen and had to establish a national foundation, it was cut off, and Jesus was driven away from the Jewish community. Jesus was labeled a wretched rebel whom heaven could not help. Eventually, He was betrayed even by the twelve apostles. The sorrow of Jesus was that He could not form a single bloodline that could convey the heart of heaven on this earth.  
Before establishing the family that God desired, He could not establish the nation that God desired, and before establishing a nation, He could not establish a world. Therefore, Jesus, who fought to find the family, could not fulfill this will and left behind the statement, "I am the bridegroom, and you are the bride."  
Do you know what that means? It means that the family is the center of the Kingdom of God.  
What is the feast of the Lamb spoken of in Christianity? It is to re-establish the image of the True Parents that God had to establish 6,000 years ago at the end of time, and to once again establish the bonds of brotherhood and the bonds of children. This is the hope of our Lord Jesus and the hope of God, who has struggled for 6,000 years to lead us.  
If we understand this, we must think about what we are holding onto. What are you holding onto? 2,000 years ago, the nation of Israel was in a position to hold onto Jesus. The Jewish community was in a position of privilege to welcome Jesus. The entire chosen people of Israel were in an environment where they could welcome Jesus and crown Him as the King of Kings, yet the Jewish people rejected Jesus, the Jewish community rejected Jesus, and all those who claimed to be loved by heaven because they were chosen betrayed Jesus, severing all the relative standards that Jesus hoped for. When that was severed, the history of the nation of Israel was also cut off, and all the words of the Old Testament that came down to Israel were severed as well.  
It is our grief and sorrow that we are in a position to hold onto the words of Jesus and cry out. It is sorrowful to pray in the name of Christ. When you pray, do you not pray in the name of Jesus? Living in such a way, bound to a noun, is pitiful. Now is the time to pray in your own name. That day is the day of hope.  
Now, we must hold onto the words and find the actions that Jesus practiced ourselves, and we must understand that this is what the image of Jesus is like. We must rediscover it. The image of Jesus, who prayed for His enemies even while being nailed and bleeding on the cross, what circumstances were in His heart that led Him to that destiny? If Christianity hopes to be completed solely through the words of Jesus, it will fail. It cannot escape judgment. Only after holding onto the very essence of Jesus, who struggled to speak, and the heart of Jesus, who spoke with anguish, can we enter the Kingdom of Heaven after discarding worldly things.  
When we think this way, we fallen beings must understand the true meaning of the words of the True Parents and the words of God. We must clearly understand the words as they are, not as parables or symbols. Even though we have studied the Bible for 2,000 years, we do not understand. Today, Christians claim to act through the words, but they are in a position that has no relationship with the actions of Jesus. The purpose of the words is to prompt action. If Christianity has lived relying on the words, why has it become what it is today? It is because the goals of the words spoken by Jesus and the goals of the Christians who heard those words are different. That is where the problem lies.  
So what should we do now? In the end times, it was said to hold onto the Holy Spirit and pray through the night. In the end times, it was said to anoint our heads with oil and enter the secret place to pray. How will the Lord come? He does not come by speaking but comes with a reality in silence. The more we are distanced from the position we stand in and the goals that the original words claim and desire, the more Jesus must suffer again on the cross to find us, and believers do not realize this. Now is the time to discern whether we can stand as active subjects equipped with the inner shock that can stir us and allow us to boldly overcome the valley of death.  
To do this, what must you do? Now we must long for it. For 2,000 years we have longed for the words, so now we must long for actions that align with those words. We must have the resolve that since Jesus walked this way, I must walk this way too.  
Who is Jesus? He is our True Parent, the True Parent. Since He spoke the words and acted personally, we must long for those actions. We must long for the words, long for the actions, and then long for that very image… Is that not so? We must long for Him more than we long for our beloved parents. We should forget about eating, forget about sleeping, and not even care about how we look; we must want to see that face. Have you ever had such a time?  
Where does the meeting take place? It does not happen by speaking well. It does not happen by acting well. It only happens in the place of longing, in the place of pure longing. What did the Lord's face look like, and what did His hands and feet look like? What did His eyes and nose look like? This desire to touch and feel that appearance is what ultimately determines whether you meet or do not meet Him. The Jesus who conveyed the words has no relation to this. He has no relation to God. Salvation does not come by calling on the name of Jesus. It is Jesus' salvation, Jesus' salvation. We must long for the substantial Jesus.  
Even if we struggle to see Jesus, who promised to return, why does He not come? Why does the Jesus who appeared before the apostles not appear? What is the reason for this? There are many apostles and many people who long to see and meet Him with earnest hearts, yet why is there a reason He cannot appear? If there is someone who longs for His appearance, regardless of the passing of time and years, they will surely be able to meet Him. There is a way to do so.  
We are orphans. In the eyes of God, we are orphans. No matter how well we live in our family environment on this earth, in God's eyes, we are orphans. We are those who have lost the True Parents, lost the True Siblings, lost the True Couple, and lost the True Children. We are like orphans. Being such, how can we be comfortable? Our hearts urge us. What do they urge us to do? They urge us to find our original parents, original siblings, and original spouses. However, even as we go around this earth, we wonder if we will find them. The content that cannot be found even in the words, where can we find it?  
Therefore, the solution is to become one who enters the secret place with oil on their head, yearning to see the Father and crying out in longing. If there is a way for the Father to find us and for the Lord to find us, we must become those who are determined to go regardless of any path of death or any treacherous mountains. Jesus walked the path of Gethsemane and Golgotha to find such sons and daughters. When He could not find them, He walked the path of death. We, who long for the day when we can meet our original parents, how many hours have you cried out longing to call Him Father and to call Him Lord?  
Now is the time for Christians around the world to solve this problem. More than any other thing, more than my own sons and daughters, we must long for Him so much that we cannot live without Him, wanting to touch even the hem of His garment, wanting to touch even His hands. Since He is our Father, we must meet Him, establish a bond with Him, and pour out all our past troubles and receive comfort for our pains and struggles in that one hour. This is the highest hope that we humans seek.  
We must long for the essence itself more than we long for the words or the actions. After longing for that essence, we must long for that heart. We must long for that heart.  
In the past, the believers of Judaism could hold onto Jesus Himself. But was there even one person who longed for Him like a parent they missed and wanted to see again in order to meet the lost parents? When God sent His only begotten Son, Jesus, to this earth as the Father of all mankind and the King of Kings, would He have sent Him to be treated with such contempt? Throughout history, He was sent as a central being…
As the Father of all mankind, He hoped that all people would welcome Him as a being they want to see again and again, longing for Him endlessly. This is the sorrow of Heaven and one of the greatest grievances. He came, shedding His blood and flesh for His children, yet they treated Him with weapons; how can this remain a joy for Heaven? If there is sorrow in Heaven, there is nothing sadder than the death of Jesus.

Words are less important than reality. Jesus, as the Son of Heaven, had to leave a will. He said to the apostles that He was leaving without being able to say everything He wanted. "If I have told you earthly things and you do not believe, how can you believe if I tell you heavenly things?" (John 3:12) He also said, "I still have many things to say to you, but you cannot bear them now." (John 16:12) If the beloved apostles had truly become His sons and daughters, there would have been no reason for Him not to speak. Yet, Jesus left without being able to leave a will. He departed without revealing the secrets that weighed heavily on His heart. He is our Father. What greater unfilial act could there be than this?

We must repent to shed the historical sins that have entangled us. All people must repent because they have committed the sin of killing their parents. What is repentance? It is regretting and realizing the sin of killing the Father. No matter how stone-like a child may be, when they feel that they have killed their true Father, who is pure goodness, who would not repent with tears? This is how it is. Regardless of how the world perceives it, the God and Jesus I know are like this.

Who can understand the circumstances of Heaven, which has walked for six thousand years with eyes wide open, longing for the original family, the children, the siblings, and the household? No matter what adversities Jesus faced during His thirty years of life, even when spending lonely nights in prayer at the foot of Gethsemane, His thoughts were on His original children. Even as He died on the cross, He prayed, "Father, forgive them, for they do not know what they do." (Luke 23:34) He was in the position of a parent who came to find His lost children, thinking that He must take this path. From this, we can understand Jesus' heart.

Today, Christians around the world recognize Jesus as wonderful and regard Him as the Son of God. However, in reality, He was a pitiful and sorrowful figure. He was treated as a monster of treason, a monster of betrayal, and a monster of heresy. The Jesus known in history was great, but in reality, He was pitiful and sorrowful. Jesus was striving to find His sons and daughters with the burning heart of a parent, overcoming all circumstances and trials. The day when the children who have struggled to find their parents, who have labored for their parents, meet again is a day when God can join and bless them.

What remains now? The words are not more important than the reality. The words are letters sent by the bridegroom to the bride. It is time to conquer the satans and return the world to God’s embrace. Only then will the reality appear. Therefore, there is nothing else for you. When approaching Jesus, my children, my lineage, and my attachments become obstacles. One must be able to feel the pain of the cross to sever these ties. We must bear the pain of the cross. Those who dislike this will never meet Jesus. Absolutely not.

The path to reunion with the Father. Before Jesus bore the cross, He said He would come again; after crossing that hill, He became a companion of the heart, and because the apostles could die with Him and share in His sufferings, the twelve apostles, along with the seventy and one hundred twenty disciples, could stand before Jesus and pass through the barrier of death without issue.

The heavenly family can only be established when it is centered on Jesus here on earth.

Many humans claim that God is in the position of a parent and that they are in the position of children. However, this is merely a name, just a name. It is like being adopted. Therefore, you must now meet Jesus through words and actions. If you cannot meet Him in prayer, you must seek Him even in the mountains; if He is not in the mountains, you must find Him even in death. If you cannot find Him in the mountains or in prayer, He will be in death, so you must seek Him. Jesus also went through this process. He traversed the path of the secret room, spent time in prayer in the mountains, and even crossed the hill of death to find His children. We, too, must seek Him with this determination. You must look at the Bible and understand it.

So, what will you do on the day you meet Him? What must we do first regarding Him? When sinful humans meet the Lord and the True Parents, we must call out to the Father and the Lord, saying, "I have fought like this and brought these offerings. You may think that when the Lord comes to this earth, the Kingdom of Heaven will be established around me, and the world will be entirely as I wish. That is utterly wrong. I must disappear. I must abandon all my desires, expectations, and hopes. From the day we meet Him, if we do not know His heart, we must be able to act according to His commands and directives.

What we must do is recognize how much He has labored. I have struggled to find this path, and how much have You labored over six thousand years of history to find Your children? We must have a heartfelt desire to comfort Him. What has Your heart been like? What has Your heart been like after traversing the long six thousand years? This child knows Your heart. This child knows Your heart.

Do not think of being praised first. When you go to meet Him, you must be silent. After the resurrection, Mary Magdalene appeared before Jesus in silence. They were historical transgressions. They had to be resolved. Please forgive me. We must confess.

After resolving the past and present, we must become the protagonists of the future. On the day we meet, we must recognize the historical transgressions once again. We have no face to show. However, since the Father does not abandon us but seeks us out and calls us, we are infinitely grateful for that grace.

Only after this can God say, "My son," and the Father and son can reunite. This is the path that believers must take toward the good family, the heavenly family, and you must understand this.

If you were to reunite, what would you wish for at that moment? Jesus or God has the sorrows of history. We must be able to say this. Can you do that?

Furthermore, we must understand how God created the heavens and the earth, how the fall occurred, why God accepted Abel's offering and rejected Cain's, why He chose Noah's eight family members, why He is called the God of Abraham, the God of Isaac, and the God of Jacob, why Jacob deceitfully took Esau's birthright, why after choosing Jacob's twelve sons, He sent seventy people to Egypt, why He made six hundred thousand people after suffering for four hundred years in Egypt, why He raised Moses, why He fought for the return to Canaan, why He fought to establish the rights of the chosen people of Israel, why Jesus came and died, and why He must come again, and what will happen in the future.

You must know these things. You must confess the historical, contemporary, and future sins that humanity has committed against God's will. The end is a time of confession. < Message > The title of the message I wish to share with you is God's effort to raise beloved children. I will speak on this title.

What is the most essential thing that all beings need? Regardless of whether they are in heaven or on earth, the most essential thing is love. It is true that love is important both in heaven and in the human world centered around humanity.

The original purpose of creation was for the human ancestors to live with God at the center of love, making His eternal love their life philosophy and life's ideal. However, due to the fall, humanity could not establish a connection of love with God and instead formed a connection of love with Satan, who is the enemy of God, as we understand through the principles.

The reason humanity lives in such a miserable state is that they have lost God's life, God's love, and God's ideology. We must deeply contemplate this once again.

If this shock does not explode from your heart, then even if God's life, God's love, and God's ideology exist, they cannot relate to us.

The time is drawing near to the end. Humanity is saying in unison that the world has come to an end. Only when a person who possesses these qualities emerges can true love, true life, and true ideology be established in this world.

God, who loves humanity infinitely, has come forth since the day humanity fell. To what extent does God love humanity? You may not be able to comprehend it with your own ideas. Even in a fallen world, parents love their children. If a beloved child is struggling in the throes of death, parents do not care about pain or fear, nor do they care about death or any action. Today, when a beloved child dies or when a loved one dies, humans feel sorrow and pain. Some even lose consciousness or go insane. Furthermore, some die. If those living on the earth can feel sorrow, pain, and even madness over the death of a loved one, what would God feel? Please think about it.

God created Adam and Eve as the protagonists who could govern all of creation, and as the source and motive of love, He created Adam and Eve to pour out all His love.

The purpose of God's creation of humanity is not only to govern the universe. We must understand that He created humans to give His love.

If God's love is the driving force that can move all of creation, what is the purpose for which He created and blessed Adam and Eve? He created Adam and Eve as the object who could receive the love of God flowing from heaven to earth. We must recognize that our ancestors were created centered around that love.

They were such Adam and Eve.

Jesus’ circumstances 
Jesus had to go through the path of suffering on this earth from the moment He was born. He had to endure even the worst suffering without dying. He was born in a stable. No one has been born in a stable throughout history, no matter how pitiful and difficult their circumstances may be. The providence of salvation starts from the lowest place. Jesus, who was born in such a lowly place, was not loved while growing up. Christians must understand this clearly. The life of Jesus over thirty years is filled with infinite sorrow.

Jesus was born into the family of Joseph, but to Joseph, He was a stepson, a stepson. He was a stepson with no relation to Joseph. When Joseph and Mary raised their own children, they neglected Jesus. Think about it carefully. Jesus grew up as a stepson. He was a pitiful Jesus who was looked down upon by His siblings. He had no parents to rely on politically, nor could He find rest in His family. That was not all. However, Jesus grew up under the direct guidance of Heaven. Moreover, because He had a heart full of hope for the future, He was destined to look upon the nation and the world even in such an environment.

However, the reason Jesus could not blame such a position was that He understood God’s heart. He knew that the Father He believed in and served had walked this unjust path for four thousand years, and that He had the mission to take responsibility for the mistakes of His ancestors who had repeated the history of unfilial conduct and to restore it. Therefore, He could not blame the opposing crowd. Because He thought with a heart equal to God’s heart, you must understand that even while being crucified, He blessed the opposing nation.

Today, Christians believe that Jesus came to die. It may seem simple when looking only at the outcome. However, they do not understand the circumstances of Jesus until His death, nor do they understand the heart of God who looked upon Jesus as He died.

Do you love someone in this world? Do you love someone who understands your circumstances, or someone who does not? 
Jesus said, 
“I came to cast fire upon the earth, and how I wish it were already kindled! You may believe that if you just believe in Jesus, you will go to heaven and treat the Lord as your bridegroom, but that is utterly unfair. You must understand that while you may believe in the words, you do not believe in the heart and reality.

Historically, was there anyone who became a true son or daughter who comforted Jesus, who shared the sorrow of God? Jesus appeared on this earth as God’s only begotten Son, but where are the sons and daughters who can become His only begotten ones? Have you thought about that?

What was the purpose of sending Jesus? 
God did not bless the original Adam and Eve merely for them to live well and happily. He blessed them on behalf of their descendants, their family, their nation, and the entire world. What is the purpose of sending Jesus? It was to find sons and daughters who could become His only begotten ones because He came as God’s only begotten Son. Believers should not just become disciples of Jesus. They must become His sons and daughters. In John 3:16, it says, 
“For God so loved the world that He gave His only begotten Son, that whoever believes in Him should not perish but have everlasting life.”

Do not think that you will be saved just by believing in Jesus. Such people are thieves, thieves. Jesus came to this earth and regarded the world as more precious than His own body. He said, “For God so loved the world that He gave His only begotten Son,” and Jesus knew that He gave Himself because He loved the world. The historical God...
When I try to understand your feelings, I cannot deny it. What is needed before the nation of Israel is the embodiment of God's love, and I have come to know that it is oneself that must stand before the world. 

Therefore, Jesus' three years of public ministry was not for the purpose of establishing Himself. It was a three-year public ministry to establish His disciples. For three years, He worked hard to raise three disciples as His own children and to make the twelve apostles true direct descendants.

Just as God worked through the three sons lost in Adam's family, the three sons lost in Noah's family, and the three generations of Abraham, Isaac, and Jacob, and the three generations of King Saul, King David, and King Solomon, Jesus was to establish three sons of faith that could represent the whole according to the principle of heavenly restoration. 

Thus, even if Jesus had to give up everything, these three disciples must not fall away. They were the three disciples He wanted to take with Him to the Garden of Gethsemane and to the summit of Golgotha, but they betrayed Him in the Garden of Gethsemane. The sad history unfolded here. 

If the three disciples had wanted to die with Jesus, it would mean that Jesus would not ascend. It is fulfilled on earth. The Holy Spirit comes, and there are sons and daughters of faith, so the Father and Mother are spiritually establishing a foundation on earth and fulfilling their will. Some may say that this is not in the Bible, but that is fine. Why would Jesus, who came to seek the earth, ascend, and what would the Holy Spirit, who is the Mother, come to do on earth instead of Jesus? The betrayed earth symbolizes the Mother. The sun and the fall were due to the Mother, so it is the Mother who must wash away the sins of this fallen land. The Holy Spirit, who is this Mother, and the believers today are climbing to the position where they can welcome Jesus, who is in heaven, by crossing the boundary. 

God sent Jesus, whom He could love, over the course of 4,000 years of history, but He could not embrace Him and love Him deeply. Although humanity welcomed the beloved Jesus, they could not hold Him and love Him. When Mary Magdalene tried to hold Jesus after His resurrection, He told her not to touch Him. Why did He stop her? This is sorrow. If God is resentful, Jesus was also resentful. Because the twists and turns of heaven and earth are tied up here, it is a heavenly principle that cannot move without resolving that. How heartbreaking it must be for heaven to see that which is tied up unresolved. 

God is searching for the substitute existence of the lost Adam and Eve. In 1 Corinthians 15:45, Jesus is referred to as the last Adam. Adam is called the tree of life. Therefore, Jesus is the one who came as the substitute for the lost tree of life. Then, has God ever boasted before the people who believe in Him, placing that beloved Jesus on earth? Has He ever boasted before the families that are searching for the one He loves? Even after 2,000 years of history, has He ever boasted before any nation or any world? He has not. 

Even at the time when God had to expel Adam and Eve from the Garden of Eden, He was indignant, but we must understand that God's indignation is even greater when He sends Jesus to this earth, has Him killed, and then has to send Him again. He sent Him as the mission bearer of the Son, but He could not complete that mission. Because there was no day when God and the Son could rejoice together during Jesus' time, the term "Second Coming" was left behind. There will come a day when God can rejoice with the Son and daughters, opening the heart of 6,000 years of resentment and establishing a connection with God or the Lord who is to come. 

Think about it, everyone. If God's only begotten Son, Jesus, had come to this earth and had not died, what would have happened? Since Jesus is the only begotten Son, God would have sent an only begotten daughter before Him. In Ecclesiastes 7:28, it says, "I found one man among a thousand, but I have not found a woman among all these." 

God's 2,000-year history is a history of seeking a bride. It is a history of seeking a bride. Can we deny that? It is a history of seeking a bride. 

Jesus appeared as a true son, but there was no appearance of a true daughter, so God's will could not be fulfilled. That is why the 2,000-year history is a history of seeking a daughter. This is also the reason why our Unification Church will struggle in the future. The Holy Spirit has come as God's daughter. 

Then, what kind of day will the day of restoration be for God? It will be the day of the Lamb's feast. When the Lord appears as the chosen man among a thousand men, where will His one bride be? The Holy Spirit has come to prepare the bride that must be ready on this earth for 2,000 years. 

When God established Adam and Eve in the Garden of Eden and blessed them, it was not just to love Adam and Eve. It was to love their descendants as well. But are there descendants who can do that? Were there sons and daughters whom Jesus could love? If there had been sons and daughters whom Jesus could say, "These are my sons and daughters who will be loved forever and are my direct descendants," this world would have already become God's nation. 

Jesus died in place of God's historical heart, the heart of the times, and the heart of the future. The Lord who is to come will come to inherit that will and practice it on earth. When He comes, what should the countless saints on earth do? Just as Jesus became a son before God, you must become true sons and daughters before the Lord who is to come. Shouldn't it be so? 

What kind of person is a filial son on this earth? To be a filial son, one must not only serve their parents well but also have children. No matter how much one claims to be a filial son or how excellent they may be, if they do not have the children their parents desire, they cannot be considered a filial son. Jesus was born as a historical filial son before God. Even if He stood in a place where He had the glory of the only begotten and claimed to have accomplished everything, if He had no children, He could not lift His face before God. Do you know why Jesus worked hard for 2,000 years? 

Jesus knew that God was working desperately to find the beloved son, and He also had a desperate heart for the people on earth, spending over thirty years of His life. Even in heaven, He is praying. For 2,000 years, He has been desperately longing for and missing humanity. You must know this. Even if you forget all the words of the Bible, it is enough to understand the heart of Jesus. Even if you are fluent in all 66 books of the Bible, you cannot go before the Father. The saddest, most resentful, and happiest things for Jesus must be resolved. 

There are those who boast of being part of the 144,000 or being the chosen people, but these three things must be resolved. Where was the saddest moment in Jesus' life, the moment He felt the most resentment, and the moment He felt the most joy? The moments of sadness and resentment are present, but the moment of joy cannot be found. 

To become a friend and to be loved more than anyone else, one must understand that person's sorrow and pain and hold onto it to comfort them. Only then can one become their friend and have the ability to influence them. If you connect through the heart and establish a relationship through love, that person can move according to your heart, and you can move according to theirs. 

Jesus knew what God's sorrow and joy were after 4,000 years. However, Jesus could not speak of it as He left. "If you do not believe when I speak of earthly matters, how will you believe when I speak of heavenly matters?" You must understand the sorrowful heart of Jesus. 

Since Jesus knew God's sorrow, God's pain, and God's joy, we must also know God's sorrow, God's pain, and God's joy. Furthermore, we are also participating in the historical work of God, who has been working hard for 2,000 years, so we must also engage in that. 

Then what is God's sorrow and what is God's pain? The sorrow of losing sons and daughters is sorrow, and the pain of struggling to find sons and daughters is pain. From the moment one loves sons and daughters with a heart that can forget all historical sorrow and pain, joy begins. 

That is why we believers must go crazy for Jesus. We must go crazy. To what extent? We must go crazy with love beyond any couple in the world. Even if my bones and my life are completely consumed, will my heart of loyalty for you change? Will my heart of admiration for you change? Those who have the heart that everything they eat, see, and hear is for Jesus are Christians. Shouldn't it be so? 

Among those who claim to believe in Jesus, there are many who just come to watch. Even though there is sorrow and twisting grief between parents and children, they come to watch. Such people have nothing to do with God. They cannot be direct descendants. Why does God struggle to come forth? We must understand that He has come forth repeatedly to establish beloved sons and daughters. 

Do you truly want to become a son of God? Do you truly want to become a daughter whom God loves? Is there a sorrow in your heart that cannot be blocked by any comfort from anyone on earth? Is there a sadness in your heart and body that cannot be blocked by any comfort or love? There must be something like that. 

No matter what humans may offer, it cannot make one a son or daughter. If you only think of the Father while living, fighting, and running, that heart must not disappear in your life and journey; only then do you have a chance to become His sons and daughters. 

You must be so captured by that heart that even holding onto a stick can bring tears to your eyes. You must know that all beings are groaning in anticipation of that day of restoration and be able to bow your head and say, "I am sorry for being ignorant." This is not abstract. If you see a comrade struggling to find that path, you must have the heart to hold them and say, "You are our brother," and weep. 

No matter how sad and lonely your heart may be, you must know that it cannot compare to God. When you look at the mountains and rivers, you must know that God's tears are left there, and when you see flowing water, you must know that God's tears are reflected there. You must feel that the place where you lie is a sea of God's tears and a place where the traces of the cross on Golgotha remain. Heaven is waiting for such hearts, crying out, "Father, who had to make the Son carry the cross on Golgotha!" Jesus left behind resentment on this earth when He died, but I will not die and will resolve this resentment in substance. 

He is searching for sons and daughters who can do that. 

Therefore, the 6,000-year history has been God's work of labor to establish beloved sons and daughters. Thus, we must feel that we are debtors to God, who has labored for 6,000 years, that we are the crystallization of God's tears over 6,000 years, and that we have paid the price of sacrifice on Golgotha. 

So, when we repent of historical sins, indemnify the sins of the times, and call upon the Father with hope for the future, when we stretch out our hands to enter, the Father will personally embrace us and say, "Oh, my son, my daughter," causing us to forget the Father's dignity and shed tears of joy and sorrow. Only those who can do this can become sons and daughters. Only those who know that the Father is such and that Jesus was such can become God's sons and daughters. 

God can proudly present these sons and daughters before the world of Satan and all beings in heaven and earth, saying, "These are the children you have been waiting for, the children I have been searching for." Only when these sons and daughters appear can God finally forget His 6,000 years of labor and entrust heaven and earth, entering into a place of rest. 

Just as Jesus wept and died holding onto the history of sorrow, if you have a way for the Father's will to be fulfilled, you must become someone who can go forth with joy. Please keep in mind that you must live such a faith life.

<Words> The message I wish to share briefly is about the Jesus you were seeking. I will speak on this title, "The Jesus You Were Seeking." 

The Purpose of God in Establishing Jesus 

We know that Jesus is the only begotten Son of God. This Jesus was the one God sought for 4,000 years. This Jesus was the one who was sought after going through the various hardships of the chosen nation of Israel. We also know that this Jesus worked hard to fulfill the will of heaven and the will of the people He wished to embrace. Therefore, the heavenly connections surrounding this one Jesus are intertwined, and the historical, temporal, and future connections of the chosen people of Israel are intertwined. Thus, when God completely finds this Jesus, the purpose of choosing Israel will be fulfilled, and when God fully embraces this Jesus, He will embrace the chosen people of Israel, and only then can He live with the people of Israel whom He has chosen. 

To completely find this Jesus can be said to be God's work, and to fully embrace Jesus is the hope of humanity, the fallen descendants who are seeking salvation. 

We must not forget that heaven worked hard to find this universal Jesus until the time of His coming after the fall. Furthermore, the chosen people who wished to embrace this one Jesus have walked the path of unimaginable persecution and death throughout history, repeatedly experiencing the history of falling and rising again. 

The Israelite chosen people, who have embraced this history, could release their grief when they held onto this one Jesus, and God's grief over sending Jesus could also be released.
