Jesus was to command the heavenly soldiers to march toward the world of Satan, but you alone remained, and everyone else disappeared. Where have the Eastern magi gone? Where has Anna gone? Where have the shepherds gone? Where has John the Baptist gone? Where has the household of Joseph gone? Where have the brothers and relatives gone? Where have the denominations gone? Where has the nation gone? They all passed away. They all passed away. Since everything has passed away, Jesus is saying, "I died for you." He is carrying the cross to establish this connection and is praying for the nation again. Everything may pass away, and this nation may perish, but Jesus, who believes that heaven will look upon it, has ascended to heaven and is praying for that nation again.

Everyone, if Jesus' situation is like this, what would Jesus' desire be? It is to find true disciples. The true disciples that Jesus is looking for are the disciples that God is seeking, the disciples that Jesus can testify about.

Have the disciples ever created an environment where Jesus could rest comfortably? Did Jesus have a family? When his mother and brothers came to him, he said, "Whoever does the will of my Father in heaven is my brother and sister and mother." Jesus had no mother, no brother. Jesus had no relatives and no nation. Jesus had no family and no siblings. Is that not so? After his death, Jesus, filled with resentment, sought out his mother, brothers, relatives, nation, church, country, and world in the spirit world, and that is the 2,000-year history of Christianity. Jesus lost the Israel that God had sought to establish and left this earth without establishing even a piece of property, so he must come again. He left without establishing the family of Jesus, the lineage of Jesus, the nation of Jesus, and the world that Jesus dreamed of, so he must come again.

Do any of you worry that Jesus, who must come again at the end times, will feel sorrow again? Have you ever tried to be a brother to Jesus? This is what heaven wants to ask. To the older ones, have you ever had the desire to love Jesus as a mother or father? Have you ever tried to love God's beloved son with the same heart as Jesus, to the point where your bones melt away, and even when fatigue and hardship come upon you, you do not care and live a life of faith shedding tears?

One day, Jesus will come again to this earth. Why does he come? To find his beloved disciples again. He must go back to the disciples who betrayed him throughout history, bow their heads, gather them, and establish his will centered on them, but he could not do that, which is God's grievance and Jesus' grievance. We must recognize that this grievance left behind is the shame of our ancestors and the shame of our history.

Today, we elevate the apostles highly, believing that they are those who receive God's utmost love, but that is not the case. When you look closely, it is not so. They are those who should have comforted humanity but failed to do so. They must bear the shame of having to ask for forgiveness after death.

The true family of the heavenly kingdom
Who were the ones that Jesus met after his resurrection? They were the group of betraying disciples. Who understood Jesus' heart, which should have welcomed and joyfully received the disciples in the providence of salvation? No one understood. This was an endless sorrow. It was sorrowful, but it was a destiny that had to be fulfilled. To gain a foothold spiritually on earth, he could not avoid going back.

When the apostles chosen as representatives to meet humanity betrayed him, and the disciples who represented humanity betrayed him, it became a total betrayal, so when Mary Magdalene tried to hold onto the resurrected Jesus, she was stopped. You must understand this situation. They are the ones who betrayed the sorrowful Jesus. Among the apostles we hold in high regard, was there even one who did not betray Jesus? You, who believe in them, are also of the same lineage of betrayers. But is there anyone who did not betray Jesus? No, there is not. Because they are a lineage of betrayers, they are living a faith life of repeated betrayal, betrayal, and betrayal. They are living in sin.

When Jesus comes again, there will be a multitude that must be forgiven before him, so when will heaven's sorrow end? When will it end? We must know Jesus. Jesus was one who sought to establish historical connections and to establish connections of the times and the future. Since Jesus left behind a sorrowful story on earth, it is the mission of the brides to bear that grievance.

Everyone, "Lord, come! Please take all my burdens of sin! Lord, come!" and we are earnestly longing for the Lord to come. Why do we long for that? Is it for me to live well and prosper? A person who sets their own coffin or their own purpose and faces heaven will become a betrayer at some point. Regardless of how their faith is or how their devotion is, until all beings in heaven and earth declare it to be right, no religion or person can say, "You must follow this." You cannot say, "You must believe in our denomination." You are in a position where you can pass through the Unification Church as much as you want.

You must understand Jesus' situation. The Jesus that heaven seeks, the Jesus that Jesus seeks, we who seek Jesus, now we must not strive to reveal ourselves, but we must become the beloved siblings who can receive Jesus' love before we die. To stand on Abel's side, we must become siblings. Before we die, we must be the beloved disciples to whom Jesus can pour out all his heart and reveal all the secrets in his heart without reservation. As the Bible says, Jesus left the words, "I have much to say to you, but you cannot bear it now." Now we must look forward to the coming Jesus. The Jesus that God wants to establish again at the end times, the Jesus that heaven seeks, the Jesus we must serve, the Jesus that Jesus himself wants to establish, we must know and serve that person.

You must not just become Jesus' disciples. You must become his sons and daughters. If there are victorious sons and daughters of heaven, even the apostles will bow down to them. If there is someone who can say, "My beloved sibling, my beloved family," then the apostles will become their servants. We must advance to the position where even the apostles kneel and worship. Some may say this is heretical, but that is the talk of those who do not understand. Everyone, the term "bride" is not a term directed at the apostles. The term "bride" is not a term granted before the apostles. If it had been granted, why would he come again? It is a word granted for the future generations of people. Know this clearly. The term "children" is not a term granted before the apostles but is a word for the sons and daughters of future generations who do not betray heaven.

Since Adam, countless prophets have come and gone, but to my knowledge, there are no ones who can become the sons of Jesus. There are no true direct descendants of Jesus. That will only happen after Jesus comes again. Understand this. When Jesus comes again to this earth, who will he come to find? He will come to find his siblings. He will come to find his parents. He will come to find his relatives. He will come to find his nation. He will come to find his people. He will come to find the world. This is not the world as it has been until now. That is why the Unification Church uses the term "family." You must not just be a church member; you must become a family member.

You cannot follow Jesus unless you surpass the apostles
What is Jesus' sorrow? Where have the three disciples of Gethsemane gone? Where are the loving parents, the loving siblings? Jesus missed them all. If the tribe had welcomed Jesus centered around the household of Joseph, Jesus would not have died. If the tribe had welcomed Jesus, he would not have died. But he was driven out of his family, driven out by John the Baptist, whom heaven had established, driven out by the denomination, driven out by the nation, and driven out by the disciples, so how could he not die? Not knowing this situation, people have believed until now that Jesus came to die. If what the speaker here is saying is true, then those who believed that way are playing a game of taking on the second cross before Jesus.

Jesus is searching. He is searching for his beloved siblings. Where have my beloved parents gone? Where have my brothers gone? Where have my relatives gone? Where have my tribe gone? Where has my church gone? Where has my denomination gone? To resolve this grievance, he has been saying for 2,000 years, "Father, please forgive me again. I came as the representative of the world and failed, and I came to lead Israel and failed."
I came to take care of the church, but I failed. I came to take care of my tribe and family, but I failed, so please forgive me. This is what I am praying for. 

The truth is that it is so. It turns out to be that way. What is God's sorrow? When He sees His own flesh and blood, His brothers being rejected, how sorrowful must heaven have been? When He saw that the parents who cherished Him did not know Jesus and were divided, how sad must heaven have been? After preparing for thousands of years and choosing Joseph's lineage to send Jesus, how must He have felt when that lineage, which should have welcomed and cherished Him, betrayed Jesus? How must He have felt when the Jewish church rejected Him? How must He have felt when the nation of Israel betrayed Him? When He is rejected by individuals, brothers, families, those who sent Him, churches, society, and nations, you must understand that God's heart was about to burst.

The Jesus whom heaven is sending again will surely come and take responsibility for this age. You who are looking toward the end, you are in a position to welcome that coming person. The time to welcome Him is approaching, so what position must you enter to be able to welcome Him? If you continue to believe only in the Bible as you have so far, you will not be able to welcome Him. When Jesus came, those who only enjoyed the Old Testament could not welcome Him. If you blindly believe in God, you will not be able to welcome Him. It was so in the Old Testament, it was so in the New Testament, and who can assert that it is not so today? We must enter the position of sons and daughters. We must enter the position of family. Otherwise, we cannot welcome Him.

Now we must enter the position of establishing a historical relationship with God and a future relationship with God's heart. This is the time. In such a time, can you go to heaven just by carrying the Bible and attending church? Where will you go? You will see when you die. I sometimes see this. Pastors who boast about going to heaven are sitting in a miserable place in the spirit world. There are many such people. Do not boast loudly. Just because you have influence in the current church does not mean you are a son or daughter of God. Even if you are praised by someone or recognized as a doctor, you are not a son or daughter of God.

As I have said, even the apostles said they could not be the sons and daughters of Jesus or His family, so who on earth can claim to be the son or daughter of Jesus or His brother? Why could the apostles not stand in such a position? It was because they did not recognize the historical Jesus and the Jesus of the times. Therefore, for us today to step into the position of sons, we must know the historical God of 6,000 years. We must know the historical Jesus. We must believe in the God of the times who governs 2.7 billion people and the Jesus of the times. Furthermore, we must believe in the future Jesus, who will appear in a completely different form after this time. Do you think the Lord will come and just take us out from such a position? Not at all. It must be a complete turnaround. The words will be different, the writings will be different, everything will be different. The key point is here. We must step into the position of sons and daughters beyond the apostles, disciples beyond the apostles, brides beyond the apostles, and brothers beyond the apostles.

The family of Jesus that heaven seeks to establish
The apostles who did not understand the heart of the historical Jesus betrayed Him. They betrayed the Jesus who moved with a historical purpose. They did not know and betrayed the Jesus who moved with a future purpose. Therefore, to block and settle this history of betrayal, we must become the true brothers of Jesus and become the brides whom Jesus can love. We must become a family that can live with Jesus forever. If we cannot do that, we must at least become a people who can go out to the battlefield and fight alongside Jesus.

Do you know the heart of the historical God? Do you know what position the God of this age is in? I want to say that today, the global Christian community is in a dangerous stage where it may repeat the history of betrayal.

God has sought. He sent Jesus before humanity and sought those who would become Jesus' brothers and family. Heaven has worked hard for this for 4,000 years. The family of Joseph had to love Jesus and live according to His will, whether they lived or died. Joseph and Mary should have reached the level of bride before Jesus went, but they could not. Among His brothers, there was no brother who would say, "Brother, where are you going? I will go with you." What happened in the Gospel of John? Even Jesus' brothers did not understand or believe in Him. John the Baptist testified that he saw the Spirit descending from heaven like a dove and coming upon Him, yet he asked, "Lord! Where are you going and how will you live?" Did the disciples ask? Did the Jews ask? Did the chosen people of Israel ask? Because of this, Jesus went with an unspeakable sorrow.

The day when this sorrow is resolved is the end day, and the day when unresolved sorrow is settled is the day of judgment. You who wish to remain on the day of judgment, examine your hearts and critically assess your situation. Have I become one who can find the Jesus that heaven seeks? Am I qualified to be a family that Jesus wants to welcome into the heavenly home, or at least a citizen of that ideal nation? Furthermore, have I become a bride, or at least a direct son or daughter whom Jesus loves? If I cannot be a bride, then I must be a son or daughter, and if I cannot be a son or daughter, then I must be a brother, and if I cannot be a brother, then I must be a family member, and if I cannot be a family member, then I must be a tribe, and if I cannot be a tribe, then I must be a citizen of that nation. Is that not the case? People do not realize that Jesus is praying with such a sorrowful heart.

You who are gathered here, we are walking a difficult path, and we are also pioneering that path. We are doing things that have not been done in history. We are speaking words that are not found in the New Testament. We are experiencing truths that some spiritual people have not experienced. Our purpose is to become a family, a tribe, and a people who can live in the embrace of the Lord when He comes to the earth. We are the gathered multitude for that purpose.

Who should stand closest to Jesus? It should be the bride, the brother, the children, and collectively, it can be said to be family. We are the family of Jesus, the family of Jesus. This is the family that God has longed for, and this is the family that Jesus sought. Establishing this family on earth is the historical wish, and to fulfill that wish, we must become the brothers of Jesus, or the children of Jesus, or the brides of Jesus, or at least enter into the lineage. Only then can we enter the 144,000. Do you know what the 144,000 is?

It was a pitiful God, a pitiful Jesus. It was our pitiful ancestors. They died and died again but could not have a day of reconciliation, a day of reconciliation lost on this land, ancestors who followed without knowing a day of reconciliation. We must advance to a position where we can welcome the Jesus who sought us, the Jesus who wanted to save us.

We are following the providential path. Looking at the history of our Korean people, this nation has been a pitiful nation. Despite being a pitiful nation, the currents of world history have trampled over this nation. And today, the Christian community is trampling over this nation.

Order of Prayer
The time is coming when we must prepare our hearts and bodies. In this preparation, we must not prepare for ourselves as individuals. Those who have had spiritual experiences pray for themselves last. When entering the spiritual world to pray, for whom should we pray first? We must pray for God first. Since it is the time to meet the Lord, we must first ask for the Lord's blessings. Then we must know how to pray for Jesus. We must pray for God to understand the heart of the historical God. We must pray for Jesus to understand the heart of the historical Jesus. After that, we must pray for the countless people who have fought for the will in the Christian community until now.

Since the fall, from Adam to now, many prophets have walked, and while tracing their steps, I must become the offering that reconciles them. After praying to God, I must know that I am aware of the grievances that remain on earth and wish to resolve them, and I must be able to shed tears. After that, I pray for my beloved sons and daughters, and then I pray for myself. This is the heavenly law.

Before praying for the nation, Jesus prayed for the Father. For over 30 years of His life, He prayed, "God! How sorrowful You are?" to comfort God and prayed for God. Then He prayed for many prophets. "You who have longed for and prophesied, and you who have promised, I have been sent as Your substitute, so I will be faithful not to go against the standards you hope for."

He prayed for that age with a historical heart, prayed for Israel, which was going against the will, prayed for the Jewish church that did not know the will, and prayed for John the Baptist, who testified but did not follow. Then He prayed for His disciples and apostles who followed Him. You must know that Jesus has not yet prayed for Himself.

"Abba Father, if it is possible, let this cup pass from me. Yet not as I will, but as You will." Jesus left without fulfilling all His wishes.

The day when Jesus can pray for Himself will be the end day. The day when Jesus can boast about Himself will be the end day. The day when Jesus' grievances are resolved, and His heart overflows with joy to comfort God and give glory to God will be the end day. Jesus did not have such a day. It was because of you, because of humanity, because of heaven and earth. Do you understand how pitiful Jesus is?

It is unreasonable to see that our ancestors were in such a fate and then say, "Please save me." It does not work that way. I do not pray that way, but I know that the prophets who cried for the pitiful nation were there. Jesus cried for the nation. Jesus cried for the denominations. Therefore, if one is to walk the normal path of faith, they must cry out for the world, cry out for heaven and earth, cry out for the nation, cry out for the church, cry out for their family, and finally pray, "Please give me responsibility."

No one knows the situation of heaven that has not yet had a day of reconciliation, a day of wish fulfillment. While saying they are seeking the will of heaven, there is no one on this earth who knows the heart of heaven and strives to uphold that will.

Now, even if we lose everything and face rejection in this world and find ourselves in a pitiful position, if we can become the brothers whom Jesus recognizes, the family whom Jesus recognizes, and the bride whom Jesus can recognize, then as humans, we could not hope for anything more.

From the evil world, those who are hated can meet Jesus.
"My beloved, I have labored for 2,000 years to find sons and daughters like you on earth. My death was for this, and my suffering and pain were for this. Now that I have found you, I will pray before my God so that you can receive the blessings of heaven and earth."

You must know that Jesus hopes for and seeks sons and daughters who can bless and be blessed in this world.

If there is such a person on this earth, the Jesus who has come will have a yearning heart for the Jesus who has not yet appeared. He cannot look at the world without tears and cannot live without feeling sorrow, resentment, and injustice. He will feel wronged when he looks at heaven and wronged when he looks at earth. He will think that he has the responsibility to resolve the grievances of heaven and earth and will be someone who sacrifices everything and still feels inadequate while calling upon the Lord.

When Jesus carries the cross, just as His mother followed Him, beating her chest and weeping, when we think of the historical Jesus, who is still laboring for us today, tears will blur our vision, and we will feel as if our bones and flesh are being crushed, and our hearts will feel tight. We must say, "I am sorry." Is there anyone living with such a heart on this earth? There is not. If Jesus has the sins of the nation, let me be accepted as the offering, and if there are the sins of the world, let me be the offering to be accepted. Just as He stood before heaven, we must be able to stand before Jesus in that way.

You must know that heaven has been waiting for a brother who can stand like that.

Heaven wants to see the image of Jesus rejoicing with His family. "Oh beloved bride, beloved my sons and daughters, beloved my brothers, beloved my relatives! My wish has been fulfilled, so let us rejoice, rejoice with heaven, rejoice with earth, rejoice with history, rejoice with the times, rejoice with the future. God, please bless us."

You must understand that Jesus longs for that position. He must come to this earth to find it, but He cannot come and is praying in the spirit world. He is not someone else. He has labored for me, suffered injustice for me, and died for me. You know that even fallen humans in this world can shed tears and wail for their brothers or sisters, but the Prince of Heaven came to this earth and died to take the lowly and humble people as His siblings. Is there anyone who cannot cry or wail?

When will Jesus come and say, "My beloved bride, my beloved sons and daughters, my beloved brothers!" and resolve the grievances that are bound in His heart? It is by resolving those grievances that the wishes of heaven, the wishes of Jesus, and the wishes of humanity will be fulfilled.

You must know that if there are children of heaven, they will be isolated in this world. If there are sons and daughters of heaven, they will be those who are hated in this evil world. You have emerged as those responsible for destroying the kingdom of the enemy, the city of Satan, so when you enter your homes, you will face persecution from your families, and when you go out into society, you will face persecution from society. Because Jesus did so, because God did so, and because those who died for heaven did so, the historical mountain of sorrow is also before us. It is the Jesus we can welcome after crossing that mountain. Therefore, Jesus comes to befriend those who stand in such positions. 

You must feel the guilt of having turned your back on Jesus and having killed Him. "Lord, I am in awe!" You can say, and you can thank Him for granting you the glory to participate in the historical foundation where the ancestors of the past shed blood and in the future path. You must know that Jesus longs for and seeks a group, a church, a nation, and a world that can do so. 

Even those with emotions can feel their bones and flesh melting away while searching for lost children. How must the heart of Jesus, who came to seek on behalf of heaven, have felt? You see, in this world...
The relationship that one claims to love the most, which is a static connection, must be compared to the relationship between God, Jesus, and myself. The connection between heaven, Jesus, and me must be greater.

Adversity is the foundation for the grace of heaven to come. The world of heart transcends historical distances. It transcends time and space. No authority or fearsome force can block that static path. Even if it is blocked by a mountain or the entire heaven and earth, it cannot be stopped. There can be no obstacles in the exchange of that heart. The protagonist of the heart is Jesus. Therefore, he said that in the end, love is what remains. Jesus came to live in the world of the heart on behalf of God's heart, which is why today the power of Jesus is expanding. In this heart, his heart is my heart, and my heart is his heart. We cannot be separated eternally, and any worldly condition can be overcome together. Only those who become such a group can be Jesus' disciples and family. In the early church era, Jesus' disciples could not reach the position of family. Whether you can boldly and freely overcome that boundary and step forward for Jesus, or not, is an important issue that you must resolve at this time.

Where will Jesus, who is to be established, go? Where will Jesus, whom God sent to establish on earth, stand? If this cannot be resolved, there is no place for Jesus to stand. Jesus must come to the earth, but there is no place for him to come. He must come and work, but there are no companions. He will be captured and killed again. He will be driven to the cross again. He will be troubled again. Therefore, he must connect through the heart of the family, the heart of the children, and the heart of the bride. He must be immersed in longing. There is a promised day, so one must have a heart that is deeply yearning and almost mad with longing. Those who have experienced a power that leads them infinitely in one direction, transcending their living emotions and any consciousness or concept, will surely enter the heavenly world.

Jesus came 2,000 years ago. He came to find the earth. But who are the people who met Jesus? If they met him, they might have met Jesus centered on their individual selves, but no one has met Jesus who can govern beyond the individual, beyond the family, beyond society, nation, ethnicity, world, and heaven and earth. To solve such problems, you must be deeply moved in your heart. There is no way to resolve it before entering the world of heart. If there is something that can resolve such issues, if there is something that can move your heart, then you will be drawn into it. If there is someone who has gone to church and has come out struggling in agony, do not go back there.

Our hearts are reaching out. Look, the radio waves do not work just anywhere. They only work where there is a receiver. If there is a relative standard, it works anywhere. The same goes for people. If there is a person with a true conscience, a true emotional standard, and a heavenly emotional foundation, that person will find a way to live even in a place of injustice and sorrow, without even realizing it. A way to live arises even in a place of misunderstanding. That way does not arise much in good places. Among those who have made historical revolutions, historical discoveries, and historical successes, no one has succeeded in a smooth place. It starts from a place faced with death. God is coming to find you in such places.

Therefore, anyone who stands before heaven must encounter twists and turns. They encounter material twists and human-centered circumstances and emotional twists. When they stumble there and cry out that this is where they must go, they become representatives who can lead many people who are struggling with various circumstances and twists. Jesus was like that. While helping the work of Joseph the carpenter, he did not live a comfortable life. His heart has gone through an infinite path of twists. He has overcome the historical, temporal, and future paths that humanity has traversed, and because he established a standard of victory in the battle against Satan, he could claim to be the Messiah. This is not written in the Bible.

The value of love that cannot be compared to anything. In the world of heart, the heart of heaven is eternally the same. What does it mean that he is the Alpha and the Omega? It is because God is the embodiment of love, the central existence of love, that there is no Alpha and Omega. True love cannot have a beginning and an end.

In the providential course heading towards such a static world, digging into the background of history, one can cry out, "Oh! Here is the heart of God hidden. Oh! This path is the way for our nation." Such a voice will save the nation. If there is someone who finds the heart of God flowing behind the history of the world and cries out that this is the way for all humanity to live, that person will be one who can pioneer the way for all humanity. Furthermore, if there is someone who claims that this is the heart of heaven and earth, the spirit world, and the whole, that person will be the Lord who will come again. Then, the history of the transformation and recreation of heaven and earth will unfold.

Because of this, seeking such a world is our wish and our faith life. If we are to walk that path, you must determine the direction of your heart. Ultimately, you must set the direction of your heart. As long as you love something in this world, you must know how to love God, how to love Jesus, how to love the world that Jesus loves, and how to love the nation that Jesus loves. After loving something greater, if there is anything left, then think of yourself. But today, it is the opposite. Whether the nation falls, whether the world falls, whether heaven grieves, as long as my sons and daughters and I do not fall, that is enough. This is a trap.

To break this, Jesus said that your family members are enemies. For the public good, one must abandon personal feelings. A person who moves for the organization they belong to, even more than for their family, is a loyal subject of that organization. Furthermore, if one sacrifices for that organization and the nation, they are a loyal subject of the nation. If there is someone who dies for the public ideals of the world, they may be considered a traitor to the nation, but they are a loyal subject of the world. Moreover, the one who walks the path for God beyond the world is the greatest loyal subject. Jesus is such a representative.

The greatest standard of happiness bestowed upon humanity is to become a true servant of God, a true loyal subject, and a true filial son or daughter. It is a grateful and overwhelming message. How did you know this? Have you become a loyal subject, a filial son or daughter, that heaven can recognize? You must step up from your family, your nation, and this world to find God. You must go boldly. Jesus went that way.

If my family opposes, I will break through my family. If my nation opposes, I will break through my nation. If my country opposes, I will break through my country. If the world opposes, I will break through the world. If countless evil spirits in the spirit world oppose, I must break through that too. The question is whether you have that heartfelt determination. In front of that heart, the iron net of Satan will naturally be lifted.

Father! I love you more than anyone else. I love you more than any humanity in the world. Just as Jesus loved, I also love you, Father. Those who can say this become brides. When such sons and daughters emerge, Jesus will say, "Hey, why are you like this? Did you think it would be like this?" No, he has waited for such sons and daughters for 2,000 years. Those who long for such family, brothers, and children, and who struggle to become such people on earth, will be the people who can establish the Jesus they seek, become family, and become kin.

The inability to fulfill historical missions can be achieved if one has a heart of love, so one must seek such a place. Love cannot be compared to anything in heaven and earth. A handkerchief given by a loved one is not worth exchanging for a fortune. Even if there are few, if there are those who can communicate emotionally, move to the marrow of Jesus, encompass the world of hope that Jesus desires, and can comfort God and humbly worship alongside him, how wonderful it would be!

Jesus longed for family who could worship with him before God, and he fought for 2,000 years to establish that standard on earth. You must understand that heaven sent Jesus to see humanity living with him. For this purpose, you must have a burning heart that transcends the individual, steps over the grief of the nation, and overcomes the peaks of the world's grief to connect with heaven. Whether you have become an existence that can automatically explode with such a heart is what determines whether you can properly welcome Jesus and establish the Jesus you seek.

<Prayer> Father! I am overwhelmed. I am a human who should live crying tears over the grievances of heaven, discovering my own inadequacies as I go along, yet the heavens remain as they are, and the heart of the nation remains as it is, allowing us to go through lives fighting and stumbling against each other. Please forgive us.

I know that Jesus came to establish a relationship that can enjoy beyond recognition, so I earnestly hope that I may become a true disciple of Jesus, a true family, true children, and true brides who can seek that relationship.

Only then can we establish the Jesus that God intended to establish, resolve the historical grievances of Jesus, and settle the mistakes made by our ancestors throughout history. I hope and desire that we may become heavenly family members who can live with Jesus from that standpoint, heavenly children.

Father, if what I feel in my heart has begun from heaven, please do not let it disappear from my heart forever. Do not let it disappear from my brain. Do not let that vitality disappear. If I must go, please allow me to transcend time and everything and dominate vertically, and let me connect, Father, I earnestly hope and desire.

Please let me remain with the word for a long time, and bless us so that we can keep pace in the course of the fight for victory and can make efforts and give our all. I pray in the name of the Lord. Amen. *
